vyāsakṛtam |
yasyā''jñayā jagatsraṣṭā virañciḥ pālako hāraḥ |
saṃhartā kālarudrākhyo namastasmai pinākine || 1 ||
tīrthānāmuttamaṃ tīrtha kṣetrāṇāṃ kṣetramuttamam |
munīnāmāśrayo nityaṃ naimiṣāraṇyamuttamam || 2 ||
śaunakādyā mahātmānaḥ śivabhaktā mahaujasaḥ |
dīrghasatraṃ prakurvantastatreśānasya tuṣṭaye || 3 ||
tasminsatre mahābhāgo munīnāṃ bhāgyagauravāt |
ājagāma munīndraṣṭuṃ sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ || 4 ||
taṃ dṛṣṭvā te mahātmāno naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ |
prahṛṣṭāḥ praśumudyuktāḥ papracchū romaharṣaṇam || 5 ||
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ –
kathaṃ bhagavatā pūrvamādityenā''tmarūpiṇā |
purāṇaṃ kathitaṃ sauraṃ tanno vaktumihārhasi || 6 ||
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanātsākṣātpūrve hi viditaṃ tvayā |
tvatto nāsti paro vaktā purāṇānāṃ mahātapaḥ || 7 ||
santyanye bahavaḥ śiṣyā api tasya mahātmanaḥ ||
tathā'pei śiṣyavātsalyāttvaṃ purāṇeṣu yojitaḥ || 8 ||
yānyanyāni purāṇāni tvayoktāni mahāmune |
alaṃ taiḥ pārvatīkāntabhaktau bhaktiyutaṃ tvidam || 9 ||
na yajñairna tapobhirvā na dānairna taistathā |
śivabhaktimṛte yasmānmuktirnāstīti śuśruma || 10 ||
devo'yaṃ bhagavānbhānurantaryāmī sanātanaḥ |
yo brūte sarvavastūnāṃ tattvaṃ jñātvaiva nānyathā || 11 ||
ataḥ śraddhā hi mahatī śrotuṃ tvadvadanāmṛtam |
asmākaṃ vartate sūtaṃ romaharṣaṇa suvrata || 12 |
sūta uvāca -
natvā sūrya paraṃ dhāma ṛgyajuḥ sāmarūpiṇam |
trisatyaṃ trijagadyoniṃ trimārga ca tritattvam || 13 ||
purāṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sauraṃ śivakathāśrayam |
yacchrutvā manujaḥ śīghraṃ pāpakañcukamutsṛjet || 14 ||
lokadvayaṃ paṭhedyastu lokamekamathāpi vā |
śraddhāvānpāpakarmā'pi sa gacchetsavituḥ padam || 15 ||
paurāṇī vṛttimāśritya ye jīvanti dvijātayaḥ |
tanmaṇḍalaṃ vinirbhidya tatsāyujyaṃ vrajanti te || 16 ||
vaktā yatra raviḥ sākṣācchrota tasya suto manuḥ |
māhātmyaṃ kathyate śaṃbharnāstyasmādadhikaṃ dvijāḥ || 17 ||
idaṃ purāṇaṃ vaktavyaṃ dhārmikāyānasūyave |
dvijāya
dhānāya śivaikātibuddhaye || 18 ||
āsīnmanuḥ sūryasuto vartate yo mahātapāḥ |
sa kadācinmahābhāgaḥ kāmikākhyaṃ vanaṃ yayau || 19 ||
pratardanasya nṛpatairyajñe vipuladakṣiṇe |
tattvaṃ vicārayāmāsurmitho yatra maharṣayaḥ || 20 ||
aśaktāste mahābhāgā bhṛgvādyāstattvanirṇaye |
evaṃ sthiteṣu vipreṣu māyayā mohitātmasu || 21 ||
saṃśayāviṣṭacitteṣu vāgabhūdaśarīriṇī |
tapaḥ kurudhvaṃ viprendrāttapo'jñānanibarhaṇam || 22 ||
tapasā prāpyate sarvamiti te śuśruvurgiram |
śrutvā tu munayaḥ sarve bhṛgvādyā dagdhakilviṣāḥ || 23 ||
mainuṃ puraskṛtya yayuḥ kṣetraṃ vai dvādaśātmanaḥ |
viśrutaṃ dvādaśādityamiti lokeṣu tadvijāḥ || 24 ||
,
ete ca munayaḥ sarve tapasā dagdhakilviṣāḥ || 27 ||
paśyantu māṃ paraṃ devaṃ viśvāntaryāmiṇaṃ vibhum || 28 ||
sūta uvāca -
iti dṛṣṭvā raviṃ sākṣātpratyakṣaṃ purataḥ sthitam |
mene kṛtārthamātmānaṃ manurvaivasvatastadā || 29 ||
ātmanyātmānamādhāya sarvabhāvena saṃyamī |
stutiṃ cakāra sa manurmunibhiḥ saha suvrataḥ || 30 ||
manuruvāca-
nama namo vareṇyāya varadāyāṃśumāline |
jyotirmaya namastubhyamanantāyājitāyaṃ te || 31 ||
trilokacakṣuṣe tubhyaṃ triguṇāyāmṛtāya ca |
namo dharmāya haṃsāya jagajjananahetave || 32 ||
naranārīśarīrāya namo mīdṛṣṭamāya te |
majñānāyākhileśāya saptāśvāya trimūrtaye || 33 ||
namo vyāhṛtirūpāya trilakṣāyā''śugāmine |
haryaśvāya namastubhyaṃ namo haritaṃvāhave || 34 ||
ekalakṣavilakṣāya bahulakṣāya daṇḍine |
ekasaṃsthādvisaṃsthāya bahusaṃsthāya te namaḥ || 35 ||
śaktitrayāya śuklāya ravaye parameṣṭhine |
tvaṃ śivatvaṃ harirdeva tvaṃ brahmā tvaṃ divaspatiḥ || 36 ||
tvamakāro vaṣaṭkāraḥ svadhā svāhā tvameva hi |
tvāmṛte paramātmānaṃ na tatpaśyāmi daivatam || 37 ||
evaṃ stutvā manuḥ prāha bhagavantaṃ trayīmayam |
munibhiḥ saha dharmātmā samyagdarśanakāṅkṣibhiḥ || 38 ||
jñāte tasmiṃstu kiṃ rūpaṃ tasya jñānaṃ kimātmakam || 41 ||
caritaṃ tasya kiṃ tāta kiṃ tīrthaṃ tadadhiṣṭhitam |
keṣāmanugrahastasya tīrthe nivasatāṃ prabho || 42 ||
lakṣaṇaṃ ca purāṇānāṃ vratānāṃ ca kramo yathā |
varṇānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca varṇācāravidhiḥ katham || 43 ||
śrāddhaṃ kathaṃ vā kriyate prāyaścittavidhiḥ katham |
etatsarvaṃ hi bhagavanpṛṣṭaṃ vaktumihārhasi || 44 ||
evaṃ manorvacaḥ śrutvā bhagavānbhāskaro dvijāḥ |
yatpṛṣṭaṃ tadaśeṣeṇa vaktuṃ samupacakrame || 45 ||
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde naimiṣāraṇya- praśaṃsādikathanaṃ nāma prathamo'dhyāyaḥ || 1 ||
bhānuruvāca -
śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi tattvaṃ yatra pratiṣṭhitam |
purāṇe'sminmahābhāga sarvavedārthasaṃgrahe || 1 ||
tattvaṃ yadbhagavato rūpamīśasya śūlinaḥ |
viśvaṃ tenākhilaṃ vyāptaṃ nānyenetyabravīcchrutiḥ || 2 ||
sa evā''tmā samastānāṃ bhūtānāṃ manujādhipa |
caitanyarūpī bhagavānmahādevaḥ sahomayā || 3 ||
masti bahudhā bhāti līlayā kevalaḥ śivaḥ |
brahmaviṣṇvādirūpeṇa devadevo maheśvaraḥ || 4 ||
pṛṣṭo brahmādibhirdevaiḥ kastvaṃ deveti śaṃkaraḥ |
abravīdahamevaiko nānyaḥ kaściditi śrutiḥ || 5 ||
ātmabhūtānmahādevāllīlāvigraharūpiṇaḥ |
ādisarge samudbhūtau brahmaviṣṇū surottamau || 6 ||
tamekaṃ paramātmānamādi kartāramīśvaram |
prāhurbahuvidhaṃ tajjñā indraṃ mitramiti śrutiḥ || 7 ||
na tasmādadhikaḥ kaścinnāṇīyānapi kaścana |
tenedamakhilaṃ pūrṇa śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā || 8 ||
mumukṣubhiḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ śiva eko nirañjanaḥ |
sarvamanyatparityajya mukta eva vimucyate || 9 ||
na tasya karmakārya vā bandhamuktī maheśituḥ |
ānandarūpayā gauryā krīḍati sma maheśvaraḥ || 10 ||
akṣeraṃ paramaṃ vyoma śaivaṃ jyotiranāmayam |
yastanna veda kiṃ vedairbrāhmaṇasya bhaviṣyati || 11 ||
+ nānyo vedyaḥ svayaṃjyotī rudra eko nirañjanaḥ |
tasmijjñāte'khilaṃ jñātamityāhurvedavādinaḥ || 12 ||
ahaṃ brahmā ca viṣṇuśva śakraścānye divaukasaḥ |
adyāpyupāyairvividhaiḥ śaṃbhodarśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ || 13 ||
na dānairna tapobhirvā nāśvamedhādibhirmakhaiḥ |
bhaktyaivānanyayā rājañjñāyate bhagavāśivaḥ || 14 ||
yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha |
bhargādviśvasya bharaṇādviśvayonerumāpateḥ || 15 ||
tasya jñānamayī śaktiravyayā girijā śivā |
tayā saha mahādevaḥ sṛjatyavati hanti ca || 16 ||
ācakṣate tayorbhedamajñā na paramārthataḥ |
abhedaḥ śivayoḥ siddho vahnidāhakayoriva || 17 ||
māyā sā paramā śaktirakṣairā girijā'vyayā |
māyāviśvātmako rudraratajjñātvā hyamṛtī bhavet || 18 ||
chasaṃjñitapustake na tasyetyādiślokātpūrva dharmārthakāmetyādi vedasiddhāntatyadhika dṛśyate |
tadyathā-
-
dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ prāyaṇe kāraṇaṃ param |
śivabhaktiḥ sadā satyaṃ nānyakiṃcana bhūtale || 1 ||
trilokyāṃ sukhakāmo yastena pūjyaḥ sadāśivaḥ |
śivabhaktiḥ mṛte saukhyaṃ kutaḥ syāt dehinām || 2 ||
śivabhaktyā dhanaṃ vidyā yaśaḥ śatranayastathā |
prāpyate vijayaḥ sarve satyametanna saṃśayaḥ || 3 ||
rogakṣayastathā''rogyaṃ yyaddhi manasecchati |
janastatsarvamāpnoti vedasya vacanaṃ yathā || 4 ||
tarhi sarve śivabhakti kathaṃ na kurvanti tathāss-
yadā lalāṭe dhātrā hi likhitaṃ saukhyamuttamam |
śivabhaktau tadā buddhijīyate nānyathā bhuvam || 5 ||
yadā lalāṭe sukhaprāptirlikhitā bhavetsadā śivasevāyāṃ matirbhavatīti vedasiddhāntaḥ |
svātmanyavasthitaṃ devaṃ viśvavyāpinamīśvaram |
bhaktyā paramayā rājañjñātvā pāśairvimucyate || 19 ||
saṃkalaṃ tasya bhāsaiva bhāti nānyena śaṃkaraḥ |
tasminprakāśamāne hi naiva bhāntyanalādayaḥ || 20 ||
tasminmaheśvare gūḍhe vidyāvidye kṣarākṣare |
vidhātari jagannāthe viśvaṃ bhāti na vastutaḥ || 21 ||
tasminmaheśvare viśvamotaṃ prorta na saṃśayaḥ |
tasmiñjñāte'khilaiḥ pāśairmucyate manujeśvaraḥ || 22 ||
brahmaviṣṇvādayo devā munayo manavastathā |
sarve krīḍanakāstasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ || 23 ||
sa evaiko na cāneko na dvirūpaḥ kadācana |
tasyā''jñayā'khilaṃ viśva vartate tanniyantritam || 24 ||
ādisarge mahādevo brahmāṇamasṛjatprabhuḥ |
dakṣiṇāṅgādvirūpākṣaḥ, sṛṣṭyarthe līlayā kila || 25 ||
tasmai vedānpurāṇāni dattavānagrajanmane |
vāsudevaṃ jagadyoniṃ sattvodriktaṃ sanātanam || 26 ||
asṛjatpālanārthaṃ ca vāmabhāgānmaheśvaraḥ |
hṛdayātkāla rudrākhyaṃ jagasaṃhārakārakam || 27 ||
asṛjadyogināṃ dhyeyo nirguṇastu svayaṃ śivaḥ |
viśvaṃ tasmāddhi saṃbhūtaṃ tasmistiṣṭhati śaṃkare || 28||
layameṣyati tatraiva trayametatsvalīlayā |
sa evā''tmā mahādevaḥ sarveṣāmeva dehinām || 29 ||
jñānene bhaktiyuktena jñātavyaḥ parameśvaraḥ |
na paśyāmi mahādevādadhikaṃ devatāntaram || 30 ||
vedā api tamevārthamāhuḥ svāyaṃbhuve'ntare ||
vedā ūcu:-yaṃ prapaśyanti vidvāṃso yoginaḥ kṣapitāśayāḥ |
niyamya. karaṇagrāmaṃ sa evā''tmā maheśvaraḥ || 31 ||
brahmaviṣvindracandrādyā yasya devasya kiṃkarāḥ |
yasya prasādājjīvanti sa devaḥ pārvatīpatiḥ || 32 ||
na jānanti paraṃ bhāvaṃ yasya brahmādayaḥ surāḥ |
adyāpi na vayaṃ vidmaḥ sa devastripurāntakaḥ || 33 ||
śṛṇvantu devatāḥ sarvāḥ satyamasmadvacaḥ param |
nāsti rudrānmahādevādadhikaṃ daivataṃ param || 34 ||
na yathā kūrmaromāṇi śṛṅgaṃ na śaśamastake |
na yathā'sti viyatpuṣpaṃ tathā nāsti harātparam || 35 ||
śivabhaktimṛte yastu sukhamāptumihecchati |
ajāgalastanādeva sa dugdhaṃ pātumicchati || 36 ||
mahādevaṃ vijānīyādehamasmīti paṇḍitaḥ |
anyatkimasmādapyasti jñātavyaṃ muktihetave || 37 ||
brāhmī nārāyaṇī raudrī pū̃jayitvā maheśvarīm |
yatprapaśyanti yogīndrāttadvidyācchāṃkaraṃ padam || 38 ||
kramāccatrāṇi caṃkramya śaṅkhinyāmupari sthitam |
yadabhivyajyate jyotistadvidyācchākaraṃ padam || 39 ||
devayānapathaṃ hitvā pitṛyāṇaṃ tathottaram |
gaganādyo ravaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śaṃkarasya sa vācakaḥ || 40 ||
viśvataścakṣurīśānatriśūlī viśvatomukhaḥ |
janakaḥ sarvabhūtānāmeka eva maheśvaraḥ || 42 ||
vālāgramātraṃ hṛtpadme sthitaṃ devamumāpatim |
ye'nupaśyanti vidvāṃsara teṣāṃ śāntirhi śāśvatī || 42 ||
pṛthivyāṃ tiṣṭhati vibhuḥ pṛthivī vetti naiva tam |
rūpaṃ ca pṛthivī yasya tasmai bhūmyātmane namaḥ || 43 ||
apsu tiṣṭhati naivāsspastaṃ viduḥ parameśvaram |
āpo rūpaṃ ca yasyaiva namastaramai jalātmane || 44 ||
yosar tiṣṭhatyameyātmā na taṃ vetti kadācana |
abhī rūpaṃ bhavedyasya tasmai vahnātmane namaḥ || 45 ||
tiṣṭhatyajastraṃ yo vāyau na vāyurvetti taṃ param |
vāyuryasya bhavedrūpaṃ tasmai vāyvātmane namaḥ || 46 ||
vyoni tiṣṭhati yo nityaṃ vyoma vetti na taṃ haram |
vyoma yasya bhavedrūpaṃ tasmai vyomātmane namaḥ || 47 ||
sūrye tiṣṭhati yo devo na sūryo vetti śaṃkaram |
yasya sūryo bhavedrūpaṃ taramai sūryātmane namaḥ || 48 ||
yaścandre tiṣṭhati virbhuścandro vetti na śāśvatam |
candro yasya bhavedrūpaṃ taramai candrātmane namaḥ || 49 ||
yajamāne tiṣṭhati yo na taṃ vetti kadācana |
yajamāno'pi yadrūpaṃ yajamānātmane namaḥ || 50 ||
tvatto vayaṃ samudbhūtāstvayyeva vilayastathā |
pramāṇapadamārūḍhāstvatprasādādvṛṣadhvaja || 51 ||
bhānuruvāca -
evaṃ vedastutiṃ śrutvā bhagavāngirijāpatiḥ |
pratyakṣaḥ samabhūtteṣāṃ vedānāṃ manujādhipa || 52 ||
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt |
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sūrya somāgnilocanaḥ || 53 ||
sthūlātsthūlataraḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmātsūkṣmataraḥ paraḥ |
vedānuvāca bhagavāndevadevo maheśvaraḥ || 54 ||
īśvara uvāca -
matprasādādbhaviṣyadhvaṃ he vedā lokapūjitāḥ |
yuṣmānāśritya viprendrāḥ karma kurvanti nānyathā || 55 ||
ye yuṣmānsamatikramya yatkicitkarma kurvate |
niṣphalaṃ tadbhavetkarma teṣāṃ yuṣmadaivajñayā || 56 |
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ yaccānyanmokṣasādhanam |
yuṣmadvaco nānyaditi matvā dhīro na śocati || 57 ||
ye vai yuṣmānanādṛtya śāstraṃ kurvanti mānavāḥ |
niraye te vipacyante yāvadindrāścaturdaśa || 58 ||
śreyase triṣu lokeṣu na vedādadhikaṃ param |
vidyate nātra saṃdeha iti datto varo mayā || 59 ||
yuṣmatkṛtaṃ paraṃ stotraṃ ye paṭhiṣyanti vai dvijāḥ |
teṣāmadhyayanaṃ puṇyaṃ matprasādādbhaviṣyati || 60 ||
bhānuruvāca -
- yadetadaiśvaraṃ tejaḥ sarvagaṃ bhāti kevalam |
tadeva śaraṇaṃ gaccha yadīcchasi paraṃ padam || 1 ||
tadeva sarvabhūtasthaṃ cinmātraṃ tamasaḥ param |
akṣaraṃ nirguṇaṃ śuddhamānandaṃ paramavyayam || 2 ||
pratyakṣaṃ sarvabhūtānāmajñānāṃ tadviparyayaḥ |
viśvamāyāvidhātāraṃ diraṣṭādaśarūpaṇam || 3 ||
bhaktigrādyaṃ mahādevaṃ jānīyātmani saṃsthitam |
ātmabhūte mahādeve yogidhyeye sanātane || 4 ||
bhaktimāsthāya paramoṃ paraṃ nirvāṇamāpnuhi |
tīrthayātrā bahuvidhā yajñāśca vividhāḥ kṛtāḥ || 5 ||
yeṣāṃ janmasahasreṣu teṣāṃ bhaktirbhavecchive |
akṣayaḥ paramo dharmo bhaktileśena jāyate || 6 ||
nāsti tasmātparo dharma ityāhurvedavādinaḥ |
dharmo bahuvidhaḥ prokto munibhistattvadarśibhiḥ || 7 ||
tatrākṣayaḥ paro dharmaḥ śivadharmaḥ sanātanaḥ |
yajñāttīrthājjapādānāddharmaḥ syādbahusādhanaḥ || 8 ||
sādhanaprārthanākleśaḥ parasaṃpattiduḥkhadaḥ |
yaḥ punaḥ śivadharmastu na sādhanamapekṣate || 9 ||
saṃcitaṃ janmasāhasraiḥ pāpaṃ rūpamaṃ yadi |
karoti bhasmasocchaktiḥ śaṃbhoramitatejasaḥ || 10 ||
kurvannapi sadā pāpaṃ sakṛdevārcayecchvim |
lipyate na sa pāpena yāti māheśvaraṃ padam || 11 ||
ye smaranti mahādevaṃ yadi pāparatā api |
te vijñeyā mahātmāna iti satyaṃ bravīmyaham || 12 ||
pādmakalpa samudbhūtāṃ brahmaṇā samudīritām || 14 ||
'śraddhayā parayā rājañśṛṇu tvaṃ gadato mama |
vakṣye'haṃ taṃ praṇamyāssdāvīśaṃ bhuvananāyakam || 15 ||
āsīdādye kṛtayuge saptadvīpaikarāvalī |
indradyumna iti khyāto rājā paramadhārmikaḥ || 16 ||
tasya putro mahābhāgaḥ sudyumna iti viśrutaḥ |
aiśvaryairakhilairbhāti yathā divi śacīpatiḥ || 17||
pratiṣṭhānapure ramye gaṅgātīre manorame |
tatra sthitvā'khilāṃ pṛthvīṃ tasminrājani śāsati || 18 ||
kadācittatra bhagavāṃstṛṇabindurmahāmuniḥ |
ājagāma sa taṃ draṃ sudyumnaṃ priyadarśanam || 19 ||
tamāyāntaṃ muniṃ dṛṣṭvā rājā rudrārcane rataḥ |
udvāsyāca mahābāhurutthāya ca kṛtāñjaliḥ || 20 ||
yathāvadabhivādyātha dadāvāsanamuttamam |
yathāvanmadhuparkādi tasmai sarva nyavedayat || 21 ||
adya dhanyaḥ kṛtārtho'smi saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ mama |
bhagavānāgato yasmānmāṃ draṣṭuṃ munisattama || 22 ||
kimarthamāgato brahmankṛtakṛtyo'smi suvrata |
viśeṣācchaṃkare bhakto na durlabhamihāsti te || 23 ||
bhānuruvāca -
sudyumnasya vacaḥ śrutvā munirāha mahāmanāḥ |
śivabhaktyamṛtāsvādaparānandaikanirbharaḥ || 24 ||
tṛṇabinduruvāca -
rājanyaduktaṃ bhavatā tattathaiva na saṃśayaḥ |
tathāpi caritaṃ śrutvā tavāhaṃ vismayānvitaḥ || 25 ||
tuṃ samāgato rājañjanmanastava gauravam |
kathayasva mahābāho śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi me || 26 ||
jānāti bhagavāneko viśvavyāpī maheśvaraḥ || 32 ||
idaṃ puṇyamiti jñātvā kṛtaṃ nānena yadyapi |
āhara praharetyādi nāmasaṃkīrtanaṃ ca yat || 33 ||
karoti tena puṇyena duṣkṛtaṃ bhasmasātkṛtam |

sudyumna uvāca -

sūta uvāca -
punarjagāma bhagavānkṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ |

brahmovāca -
aho dakṣa mahāmūṃḍha durbuddhe kiṃ kṛtaṃ tvayā |

dharmādharmavyavasthā ca varṇāścaivā''śramaṇi ca || 19 ||

ahaṃ nādyāpi jānāmi cakrī śakrasya kā kathā |
svecchāvigraharūpiṇyā gauryā saha pinākadhṛt || 22 ||

sa eva badhnāti paśūnasmadādīnmaheśvaraḥ || 23 ||

nāmasaṃkīrtanādyasya bhidyate pāpañjaram || 24 |

gate caturṣukhe deve sarvalokapitāmahe |
dadhīcirabravīdakṣaṃ munīnāmagraṇīḥ svayam || 27 ||
dadhīciruvāca -
kathaṃ devādhideveśaḥ karmasākṣī sanātanaḥ |
viśveśvaro mahādevastvayā dakṣa na pūjyate || 28 ||
vācakaḥ praṇavo yasya jñānamūrterumāpateḥ |
anugrahaṃ vinā tasya kathaṃ jānā̃ti śūlinam || 29 ||
eka eveti yo rudraḥ sarvavedeṣu gīyate |
tasya prasādaleśena muktirbhavati kiṃkarī || 30 ||
prasaṅgātkautukāllobhādbhayādajñānato'pi vā |
hara ityuccaranmartyaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate || 31 ||
aho dakṣa tavājñānaṃ tava nāśasya kāraṇam |
evaṃ dadhīcervacanaṃ śrutvā dakṣo vicakṣaṇaḥ |
dadhīcimabravīdviprāḥ śakrādīnāṃ ca saṃnidhau || 33 ||
dakṣa uvāca -
nāhaṃ nārāyaṇāddevātpaśyāmyanyaṃ dvijottama |
kāraṇaṃ sarvavastūnāṃ nāstītyaiva suniścitam || 34 ||
dadhīciruvāca -
umayā saha yo devaḥ soma ityucyate budhaiḥ |
sa eva kāraṇaṃ nānyo viṣṇorapi hi vai śrutiḥ || 35 ||
tasmadyaḥ sarvadevānāmadhikaścandraśekharaḥ |
ijyate sarvayajñeṣu kathaṃ dakṣa na pūjyate || 36 ||
yajñasya pālako viṣṇuriti yanniścitaṃ tvayā |
bhaviṣyatyanyathaivā''śu paśyataḥ kamalāpateḥ || 37 ||
ete ca brāhmaṇāḥ sarve ye dviṣainti maheśvaram |
bhavantu vedavādyāste tamopahatacetasaḥ || 38 ||
pāpaṇḍācāraniratāḥ sarve nirayagāminaḥ |
kalau yuge tu saṃprāpte daridrāḥ śūdrayājakāḥ || 39 ||
sarvasmādadhiko rudraḥ paśupāśavimocakaḥ |
parāṅmukhastu yuṣmākaṃ mā dijyākarī gatiḥ || 40 ||
iti vā yayau vidadhīcirmunipuṅgavaḥ |
svāśramaṃ munibhirjuṣṭamoṃkāraṃ narmadātaṭe || 41 ||
etasminnantare gaurī paravyomātmikā śivā |
dakṣayajñasya vṛttāntaṃ śrutvā devaṛṣermukhāt || 42 ||
māha viśvādhikaṃ rudraṃ mãṇatārtiprabhañjanam |
nirīkṣyamāṇaṃ deveśī parānandaikavigraham || 43 ||
śrīdevyuvāca ---
yo'yaṃ prācetaso dakṣaḥ pitā me pūrvajanmani |
āvāmavajñāya kathaṃ yajñaṃ kartuṃ pracakrame || 44 ||
devāḥ sarve samāhūtā viṣṇunā saha śaṃkara |
ādityā vasavo rudrāḥ sādhyāścaiva marudraṇāḥ || 45 ||
ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhā daiteyā dānavāśca ye |
rājānaśca mahābhāgā gandharvāḥ kiṃnarāstathā || 46 ||
t
avajñākāriṇastasya yajñaṃ śīghraṃ vināśaya |
tena me jāyate prītistulā bhaktavatsala || 47 ||
evaṃ devyā vacaḥ śrutvā devadevaḥ pinākadhṛt |
asṛjattatkṣaṇācchaṃbhuvīrabhadraṃ mahābalam || 48 ||
sahasrāsiṃhavadanaṃ pralayānisamaprabham |
sahasrabāhuṃ jaṭilaṃ duṣṭānāṃ ca bhayaṃkaram || 49 ||
bhaktānāṃ varadaṃ devaṃ sūryasomāgnilocanam |
umākopodbhavā devī bhadrakālī bhayaṃkarī || 50 ||
anyāśca devyo rudrāśca śataśo romasaṃbhavaḥ |
bhadrakālyā saha tadā vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ || 51 ||
prahito devadevena dakṣayajñajighāṃsayā |
gatvā sa yajñaṃ dakṣasya bhasmasādakarodvijāḥ || 52 ||
dakṣastadadbhutaṃ karma dṛṣṭvā'tha bhayavihvalaḥ |
gatastaccharaṇaṃ śīghraṃ vīrabhadrasya śūlinaḥ || 53 ||
uvāca vīrabhadrastaṃ dakṣaṃ prācetasaṃ dvijāḥ |
tasya pāpavimokṣāya kāruṇyāmṛtavāridhiḥ || 54 ||
vīrabhadra uvāca -
gaccha vārāṇasīṃ dakṣa sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm |
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ yatra tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ || 55 ||
anugrahādbhagavato devadevasya śūlinaḥ |
anenaiva śarīreṇa tatra mokṣaṃ gamiṣyasi || 56 ||
sūta uvāca -
vīrabhadrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā dakṣo mahāmatiḥ |
gatvā vārāṇasīṃ śīghraṃ sarvasaṅgavivarjitaḥ || 57 ||
pratiṣṭhāpya mahāliṅga gaṅgātīre manorame |
ārādhya parayā bhaktyā tasmĩlliṅge layaṃ gataḥ || 58 ||
dakṣeśvarasya māhātmyaṃ kathitaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ |
trilocanasya māhātmyaṃ sāṃprataṃ varṇyate mayā || 59 ||
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrī saure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde dakṣeśvara- māhātmyādikathanaṃ nāma saptamo'dhyāyaḥ || 7 ||
sūta uvāca -
trilocanātparaṃ liṅgaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ na dṛśyate |
yāni sthitāni liṅgāni vārāṇasyāṃ dvijottamāḥ |
dṛṣṭānyeva bhavantyeva dṛṣṭe liṅga trilocane || 2 ||
asaṃkhyātāni pāpāni jñānato'jñānato'pi vā |
kṛtāni nāśayatyevaṃ devadevastrilocanaḥ || 3 ||
māyāpāśena baddhānāṃ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināmapi |
muktiṃ dadāti paramāṃ devadevastrilocanaḥ || 4 ||
paścimābhimukhaṃ liṅgaṃ sarpamekhalamaṇḍitam |
tasya darśanamātreṇa koṭiliṅgārcanaṃ phalam || 5 ||
trilocanaṃ susaṃpūjya kṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ |
yayau kāmeśvaraṃ draṣṭuṃ siddhaliṅgamanuttamam || 6 ||
dadau durvāsase yatra devadevo maheśvaraḥ |
prasanno vividhāḥ siddhīḥ sarveṣāmapi durlabhāḥ || 7 ||
anyaśvāpi varo datto devadevena śūlinā |
kṛtānāṃ kriyamāṇānāṃ sarveṣāṃ tapasāmapi || 8 ||
krodho nāśakaraḥ prokto dhanyathaiva mune'stu te |
tasya dakṣiṇadigbhāge kāmakuṇḍamiti smṛtam || 9 ||
tatra snātvā naro bhaktyā dṛṣṭvā kāmeśvaraṃ śivam |
brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpairmukto yāti parāṃ gatim || 10 ||
anyānyapi ca liṅgāni vārāṇasyāṃ sthitānyapi |
.. saṃkhyāmapi na jānāti teṣāṃ devavaturmukhaḥ || 11 ||
ko vā vadati māhātmyamṛte devānmaheśvarāt |
nandīśvaro vā jānāti prasādāgirijāpateḥ || 12 ||
atha satyavatīsūnudraṣṭuṃ devīṃ śivāṃ parām |
viśālākṣī dvijaśreṣṭhā yatra saṃnihitā śivā || 13 ||
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā vidhivadbhaktyā saṃpūjya ca mahāmuniḥ |
parīnandātmikāṃ gaurīṃ stutiṃ matvā cakāra saḥ || 14 ||
vyāsa uvāca --
viśālākṣi namastubhyaṃ parabrahmātmake śive |
tvameva mātā sarveṣāṃ brahmādīnāṃ divaukasām || 15 ||
ṛjvī kuṇḍalinī sukṣmā yogasiddhipradāyinī || 16 ||
svāhā svadhā mahāvidyā meghā lakṣmīḥ sarasvatī |
satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā sarvaśaktimayī śivā || 17 ||
aparṇā caikaparṇā ca tathā caikaikapāṭalā || 18 ||
umā haimavatī cāpi kalyāṇī caitra mātṛkā ||
khyātiḥ prajñā mahābhāgā loke gaurīti viśrutā |
gaṇāmbikā mahādevī nandinī jātavedasī ||19 ||
sāvitrī varadā puṇyā pāvanī lokaviśrutā |
āryatī niyatī raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī || 20 ||
kālarātrī mahāmāyā revatī bhūtanāyikā
gautamī kauśikī cāssrthā caṇḍī kātyāyanī satī || 21 ||
vṛṣadhvajā śūladharā paramā brahmacāriṇī |
mahendropendramātā ca pārvatī siṃhavāhanā || 22 ||
evaṃ stutvā viśālākṣī divyaistaiḥ sunāmabhiḥ |
kṛtakṛtyo'bhavadvyāso vārāṇasyāṃ dvijottamāḥ || 23 ||
vārāṇasyāṃ viśālākṣī gaṅgā viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ |
bhaktiḥ paśupatau tatra durlabhaṃ hi catuṣṭayam || 24 ||
yaḥ paśyati viśālākṣīṃ snātvā gaṅgāmbhasi dvijāḥ |
aśvamedhasahasrasya phalamānotyanuttamam || 25 |
vārāṇasyāstu māhātmyamiti kiṃcinmayoditam |
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvā'pi yāti māheśvaraṃ padam || 26 ||
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde trilocana- māhātmyādikathanaṃ namāmo'dhyāyaḥ || 8 ||
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ -
kiṃ lakṣaṇaṃ purāṇānāṃ teṣāṃ dānena kiṃ phalam |
anyeṣāmapi dānānāṃ vratānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ || 1 ||
varṇānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca teṣāṃ vai lakṣaṇaṃ yathā |
tataḥ śrāddhavidhānaṃ ca prāyaścittaṃ kathaṃ bhavet || 2 ||
sarvametadaśeṣeṇa sūta no vaktumarhasi |
mātsyaṃ ca gāruḍaṃ proktaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ ca tataḥ param || 11 ||
bhāgadvayena kathitaṃ brahmāṇḍamati saṃjñitam |
khilānyupapurāṇāni yāni coktāni sūribhiḥ || 12 ||
idaṃ brahmapurāṇasya khilaṃ sauramanuttamam |
saṃhitādvayasaṃyuktaṃ puṇyaṃ śivakathāśrayam || 13 ||
āyā sanatkumāroktā dvitīyā sūryabhāṣitā |
iyaṃ puṇyatamā khyātā saṃhitā pāpanāśinī || 14 ||
vaivasvatāya manave kathitā raviṇā purā |
dānamasya purāṇasya dānānāmuttamaṃ dvijāḥ || 15 ||
yo dadyācchivabhaktāya brāhmaṇāya tapasvine |
yāni dānāni lokeṣu prasiddhāni dvijottamāḥ || 16 ||
sarveṣāṃ phalamāpnoti caturdaśyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ |
brāhmaṃ purāṇaṃ prathamaṃ dadāti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ || 17 ||
sarvapāpavinirmukto brahmaloke mahīyate |
brahmāṇamudiśya yo dadāti gurordine || 18 ||
dvijāya vedaviduṣe jyotiṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet |
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇumuddiśya dvādaśyāṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ || 19 ||
anūcānāya yo dadyādvaiṣṇavaṃ padamāpnuyāt |
dadāti sūryabhaktāya yastu bhāgavataṃ dvijāḥ || 20 ||
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvarogavivarjitaḥ |
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgramante vaivasvataṃ padam || 21 ||
vaiśākhe śuklapakṣasya tṛtīyā'kṣayasaṃjñitā |
tasyāṃ tithau saṃyatātmā brāhmaṇāyā''hitāśaye || 22 ||
bhaviṣyākhyaṃ purāṇaṃ tu dadāti śraddhayānvitaḥ |
aśvamedhasya yajñasya phalamānotyanuttamam || 23 ||
ma.rkaṇḍeyaṃ tu yo dadyātsaptabhyāṃ prayatātmavān |
sūryalokamavāprati sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ || 24 ||
āgneyaṃ pratipadyeva pradadyādāhitāgnaye |
rājasūyasva yajñasya phalaṃ bhavati śāśvatam || 25 ||
dadāti nāradīyaṃ yaścaturdaśyāṃ samāhitaḥ |
dvijāya śivabhaktāya śivaloke mahīyate || 26 ||
yo dadyādbrahmavaivarta vaiṣṇavāya samāhitaḥ |
brahmalokamavāpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabham || 27 ||
kārtikasya caturdaśyāṃ śuklapakṣasya suvaitāḥ |
laiṅgaṃ dadyādvijendrāya śivārcanaratāya vai || 28 ||
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvaiśvarya samanvitaḥ |
yāti māheśvaraṃ dhāma sarvalokopari sthitam || 29 ||
dvādaśyāṃ saṃyato bhūtvā brāhmaṇāya tapasvine |
yo vai dadāti vārāhaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati || 30 ||
skāndaṃ śivacaturdaśyāṃ pradadyācchviyogine |
jñānī bhavati viprendrā mahādevaprasādataḥ || 31 ||
dvādaśyāṃ vā caturdaśyāṃ dadyādvāmanamuttamam |
tasya devasya taṃ lokaṃ mānotyakṣayamuttamam || 32 ||
dadyātkarma caturdaśyāṃ yogine prayatātmane |
sarvadānasya yatpuṇyaṃ sarvayajñasya yatphalam || 33 ||
mānoti tatphalaṃ vidvānante śaivaṃ paraṃ padam |
mātsyaṃ dadyādvijendrāya prayatīttarāyaṇe || 34 ||
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ śivaloke mahīyate |
gāruḍaṃ śivamuddiśya dadyācchvitithau dvijāḥ || 35 ||
vājapeya sahasrasya phalamānotyanuttamam |
pradadyācchivabhaktāya brahmāṇḍamiti yatsmṛtam || 36 ||
śivasya purato bhaktyā saṃprāpte dakṣiṇāyane |
candrasya grahaṇe vā'tha bhānorapi ca suvratāḥ || 37 ||
gaṇādhipatyamānoti devadevasya śūlinaḥ |
evamuktaḥ purāṇānāṃ kramo dānena yatphalam || 38 ||
proktaṃ samāsato viprāḥ sūryo yatsvayamabravīt |
yaḥ paṭhedimamadhyāyaṃ mahādevasya saṃnidhau || 39 ||
sarvapāpavinirmukto vājapeyaphalaṃ labhet || 40 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde brāhmādi- purāṇa kramadānaphalakathanaṃ nāma navamo'dhyāyaḥ || 9 ||
sūta uvāca -
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ vimalaṃ ca caturvidham |*
dānaṃ pātre pradātavyaṃ nāpātre 'pyaṇumātrakam || 1 ||
pātrabhūtānpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ |
bhānunā devadevena manave kathitāśca ye || 2 ||
na dānādadhikaṃ kiṃcidvidyate bhuvanatraye |
dānena prāpyate svargaḥ śrīrdānenaiva labhyate || 3 ||
dānena māpnuyātsaukhyaṃ rūpaṃ kānti yaśo balam |
dānena jayamāmoti muktirdānena labhyate || 4 ||
dānena śatrūñjayati vyādhirdānena naśyati |
dānameva na caivānyaditi devo'bravīdraviḥ || 6 ||
taramādānāya satpātraṃ vicāryaiva prayatnataḥ |
dātavyamanyathā sarve bharanīva hutaṃ bhavet || 7 ||
vedavedāṅgatatvajñāḥ śāntāścaiva jitendriyāḥ |
śrautasmārtakriyāniṣṭhāḥ satyaniṣṭhāḥ kuṭumbinaḥ || 8 ||
tapasvinaratīrthatāḥ kṛtajñā mitabhāṣiṇaḥ |
guruśuśrūṣaṇairatā nirtya svādhyāyaśīlinaḥ || 9 ||
mahādevārcanaratā bhūtiśāsanabhūṣitāḥ |
vaiṣṇavāḥ sūryabhaktā vā pātrabhūtā dvijottamāḥ || 10 ||
ebhya eva pradātavyamīheśanaphalaṃ yadi |
āpadyapi na dātavyamanyebhya iti niścitam || 11 ||
yastu māheśvaro vipro jātimātrospi yadyapi |
uttamaḥ sarvapātrāṇāṃ taramai dattaṃ tadakṣayam || 12 ||
śivabhaktamatikramya yaccānyasmai pradīyate |
niṣphalaṃ tadbhaveśanaṃ narakaṃ ca prapadyate || 13 ||
tasmātpāyatamaṃ jñātvā śivabhaktamakalmaṣam |
tasmai sarva pradātavyamakṣayaṃ phalamicchatā || 14 ||
dānaṃ phalamanuddiśya sarvadā yatpradīyate |
tānaṃ nityamityuktaṃ devadevena bhānunā || 15 ||
dānaṃ pāpaviśuddhayarthaṃ śraddhayā yatpradīyate |
proktaṃ naimittikaṃ dānamṛṣibhirvedavādibhiḥ || 16 ||
putrārthaṃ vā dhanārtha vā svargārthaṃ vā'nyato'pi vā |
yaddānaṃ dīyate bhaktyā kāmyamityabhidhīyate || 17 ||
harasya prīṇanārthaṃ yacchivabhaktāya dīyate |
dānaṃ tadvimalaṃ proktaṃ kevalaṃ mokṣasādhanam || 18 ||
yatkiṃcidīyate dānaṃ daridrāya viśeṣataḥ |
svalpāmapi mahīṃ yastu dadāti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ |
sa yāti brahmasadanaṃ yatra devaḥ svayaṃ virāṭ || 20 ||
ikṣugodhūmatuvarīyavaiśca sahitāṃ mahīm |
yo dadāti daridrāya sa yāti savituḥ padam || 21 ||
api gocarmamātrāṃ yo dadāti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ |
śivabhaktāya śāntāya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate || 22 ||
na bhūmidānādadhikaṃ dānamastīha bhūtale |
tavānaṃ hi daridrāya dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam || 23 ||
āḍhayāya naiva dātavyaṃ bhūmidānaṃ viśeṣataḥ |
yo dadāti bhayātsnehātso'kṣarya narakaṃ vrajet || 24 ||
yairdattā brāhmaṇebhyaśca grāmāḥ paramadhārmikaiḥ |
gṛhṇanti ye karaṃ teṣu lobhāndhāḥ pāpino nṛpāḥ || 25 ||
narakeṣu vipacyante yāvatkalpāyutatrayam |
tadante makṣikā yūkā matkuṇā maśakāstathā || 26 ||
kṛmayo jālapādārthe śūkarāḥ pakṣiṇastathā |
śvāno godhāḥ śaśāḥ sedhā gardabhāśva pipīlikāḥ || 27 ||
mūṣakāḥ kṛkalāsāśca vṛkṣagulmādayastathā |
bhavanti yugasāhasraṃ tadante mlecchajātayaḥ || 28 ||
na teṣāṃ niṣkṛtirddaṣṭā prāyaścittaśatairapi |
brahmahā śuddhimānoti kālena munipuṅgavāḥ || 29 ||
dvijagrāmakaragrāhī naiva śuddhimavāpnuyāt |
tasmātpariharettatra karaṃ yatnena buddhimān || 30 ||
vimaidānakarādānādadhikaṃ nāsti pātakam |
dānānāmuttamaṃ dānaṃ vidyādānaṃ vidurbudhāḥ || 31 ||
tacca dānaṃ vinītāya varṇāśramaratāya ca |
brāhmaṇāyaiva śāntāya śuśrūṣaṇaratāya ca || 32 ||
dattaṃ tadbrahmalokāya vidyādānaṃ pracakṣate |
annadānaṃ praśaṃsanti viduṣo vedavādinaḥ || 33 ||
anameva yataḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇadānasamaṃ hi tat |
tasmādaharahardeyamanameva vicakṣaṇaiḥ || 34 ||
aparīkṣyaiva sarvebhya iti svāyaṃbhuśāsanāt |
prīto virañciramena prītaca kamalāpatiḥ || 35 ||
mītaśca bhagavāñranenaiva śacīpatiḥ |
tasmādviśiṣṭaṃ tadeyamāhurveda vido budhāḥ || 36 ||
āmamanaṃ gṛhasthāya naiva parka kadācana |
nādhvagāya niṣiddhaṃ taditi devo'bravīdraviḥ || 37 ||
jaladānamapi proktamannadānena vai samam |
jīvanaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ jalameva dvijottamāḥ || 38 ||
tiladaḥ putramāproti vāsodaḥ kāntimuttamām |
dīpadī nirmalāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ yānadaḥ śriyamuttamām || 39 ||
śayyāpradaśvāpi tathā dhānyadaḥ saukhyamuttamam |
aśvinorlokamāoti saundarya ghoṭakamadaḥ || 40 ||
brahmadānaṃ mahaddānamiti vedavido viduḥ |
tena dānena mahatā sāyujyaṃ brahmaṇaḥ smṛtam || 41 ||
gṛhītvā vetanaṃ vedaṃ yo'dhyāpayati mūḍhadhīḥ |
adhīte yo hi vā dattvā tāvubhau pāpinī smṛtau || 42 ||
tayormukhagaitā vedā ninditāḥ sarvakarmasu |
surābhāṇḍagataṃ toyaṃ yathā bhavati ninditam || 43 ||
gavāṃ grāsapradānena mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ

smṛtvā madhye punardhyācchuklavarṇī svarasvatīm |
ased ca śirorogaṃ mukharogānvināśayet || 26||
prajñā caivaṃ smṛtirmedhā kavitvaṃ buddhiruttamā |
stambhanaṃ duṣṭatvānāṃ sarvavāyuñjayetsadā || 27 ||
hṛtsarojagataṃ devamaṣṭādaśabhujairyutam |
nīlāruṇaṃ mahākārya kcindrajaṭādharam || 28 ||
siṃhacarmāmbaraṃ bhīmaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam |
bhujaṅgamhārābharaṇaṃ sarvakaṅkanūpuram || 29 ||
jvālāmālākulaṃ dīsaṃ bhābhāsitadigānanam |
abhedyaṃ vijayaṃ raudramobhyaṃ tridaśeśvaram || 30 ||
tayathā-vṛṣṭama tre tu tasminnai maneneotyāpayetkṣaṇāt |
lakṣamādhāya tatraiva yojayenmāye ṣaṇmukha |
ghṛtaṃ ghṛteṣveva yatha niyuktaṃ prayāti caikyādaviśeṣabhāvam |
tathaiva līno na bhavetsa bhūyaḥ pare caturthe tvanayā ca yuktyā |
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure śivaskandasaṃvāde sāttvikarājasa- vighnādikathanaṃ nāma trayodaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 13 ||
sūta uvāca -
bavāni saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ |
tatra kṛṣṇāṣṭamī puṇyā sarvapāpapraṇāśanī || 1 ||
kamasaśita pustakeṣu ya ekādaśo'dhyāyaḥ sa evātra saṃgṛhītaḥ |
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvratānnānyadvatamasti vibhūtidam |
kṛṣṇāṣṭamītrataṃ kṛtvā brahmā brahmatvamāpnuyāt || 2 ||
viṣṇutvaṃ prāptavānviṣṇuḥ sureśatvaṃ śacīpatiḥ |
kubero yakṣarājatvaṃ niyantṛtvaṃ yamaḥ svayam || 3 ||
candraścandratvamāpanno gaṇeśatvaṃ gaṇādhipaḥ |
rakandaḥ senāpatitvaṃ ca tathā cānye gaṇeśvarāḥ || 4 ||
kṛtvā caiśvaryamāpannāḥ saubhāgyaṃ devavallabhāḥ |
vratasyāsya prabhāvena lakṣmyāḥ patirabhūddhariḥ || 5 ||
yayātiḥ sārvabhaumatvaṃ tathā cānye nṛpottamāḥ |
ṛṣayo munayaḥ siddhā gandharvāṇāṃ ca kanyakāḥ || 6 ||
kṛtvā caiva parāṃ siddhiṃ prāptāśca munipuṅgavāḥ |
nandīśvareṇa yatproktaṃ nāradāya mahātmane || 7 kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam |
meroryadākṣiṇaṃ śṛṅgaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam || 8 ||
tatra nandīśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvajñaṃ śaṃbhuvallabham |
upāsyamānaṃ munibhiḥ stūyamānaṃ marudgaṇaiḥ || 9 ||
sarvānugrahakartāraṃ stutvā tu vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ |
abravītpraṇipatyātha daṇḍavannārado muniḥ || 10 ||
nārada uvāca -
bhagavansarvatattvajña sarveṣāmabhayaprada |
kena tena cīrṇena tapovṛttiḥ prajāyate || 11 ||
saubhāgyaṃ kāntimaiśvaryamapatyaṃ ca yaśastathā |
śāśvatīṃ muktimante ca paśupāśavimocanīm || 12 ||
bhagavaṃstadvrataṃ brūhi kāruṇyācchaṃkarabhiyam |
nandikeśvara uvāca –
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ śreṣṭhamasti devaṛṣe śṛṇu || gaṇeśatvaṃ mayā labdhaṃ yena cīrṇena nārada || 13 ||
māse mārgaśire prāpte kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ jitendriyaḥ |
aśvatthadantakāṣṭhena kṛtvā vai dantadhāvanam || 14 ||
snānaṃ kṛtvā ca vidhivattarpaṇaṃ caiva nārada |
āgatya bhavanaṃ paścātpūjayecchaṃkaraṃ prabhum || 15 ||
gomūtraṃ prāśya vidhivadupavāsī bhavenniśi |
atirātrasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet || 16 |
pūjayecchaṃ bhunāmānaṃ bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram || 17 ||
vājapeyāṣṭakaphalaṃ prāpnoti śraddhayā'nvitaḥ |
māghe vaṭasya kathitaṃ gokṣīraṃ prāśanaṃ smṛtam || 18 ||
māheśvaraṃ susaṃpūjya gomedhasyāṣṭakaṃ phalam |
phālgune ca tadevoktaṃ kāryaṃ vai prāśanaṃ ca tat || 19 ||
saṃpūjayenmahādevaṃ rājasūyāṣṭakaṃ phalam |
kāṣṭhamaudumbaraṃ caitre prāśane varjitā janāḥ || 20 it pūjayetsthāṇunāmānamaśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet |
śivaṃ saṃpūjya vaiśākhe pītvā caiva kuśodakam || 21 ||
naramedhāṣṭaphalaṃ prāpnotyeva hi nārada |
jyeṣṭhe lākṣaṃ bhavetkāṣṭhaṃ pūjyaḥ paśupatirvibhuḥ || 22 ||
gavāṃ śṛṅgodakaṃ prāśya svapedevasya saṃnidhau |
gavāṃ koṭipradānasya yatpuṇyaṃ tadavāpnuyāt || 23 ||
āṣāḍhe cogranāmānamiṣṭvā prāśya ca gomayam |
sautrāmaṇyāstu yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet || 24 ||
pālāśaṃ śrāvaṇe proktaṃ śarteṃ saṃpūjya nārada |
prāśayitvā'rkapatrāṇi kalpaṃ śivapure vaset || 25 ||
māse bhādrapade'ṣṭamyāṃ tryambakaṃ saṃprapūjayet |
māśanaṃ bilvapatrasya sarvadīkṣāphalaṃ bhavet || 26 |
āśvine jambuvṛkṣasya dantakāṣṭhamudīritam |
īśvaraṃ pūjayedbhaktyā prāśayettaṇḍulodakam || 27 ||
pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ labhet |
māse tu kārtike'ṣṭamyāmīśānākhyaṃ prapūjayet || 28 ||
pañcagavyaṃ sakṛtpītvā agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet |
varṣānte bhojayedviprā śivabhaktiparāyaṇān || 29 ||
pāyasaṃ madhusaṃyuktaṃ ghṛtena supariplutam |
śaktyā hiraṇyaṃ vāsāṃsi bhaktyā tebhyo nivedayet || 30 ||
devāya dadyādadhyannaṃ vitānadhvajacāmaram |
saratnāṃ tāmrakalaśīṃ gāmalaṃkṛtya nārada |
alaṃkāraṃ ca vastraṃ ca dakṣiṇāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ || 32 ||
kalpakoṭiśataṃ sāgraṃ śivaloke mahīyate |
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ samyakprāptaṃ devaṛṣe mayā || 33 ||
yaduktaṃ devadevena devyai viśvasṛjā purā || 34 ||
sūta uvāca -
evaṃ nandīśvarācchrutvā nārado munipuṅgavāḥ |
kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvrataṃ puṇyaṃ yayau badarikāśramam || 35 ||
vratasyāsya prabhāvaṃ yaḥ paṭhedvā śṛṇuyādapi |
atisatrasya yajñasya phalaṃ prānotyanuttamam || 36 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde kṛṣṇāṣṭamī- vrataṃ nāma caturdaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 14 ||
sūta uvāca -
anyadvataṃ pāpaharaṃ devadevasya cakriṇaḥ |
yaduktaṃ bhānunā pūrva yājñavalkyāya yogine || 1 ||
yājñavalkya uvāca -
jayā ca vijayā caiva kiṃphalā kiparāyaṇā |
tasyāṃ viśiṣṭaṃ yatpuṇyaṃ vada kaśyapanandana || 2||
sūrya uvāca -
dvādaśī viṣṇudayitā dvādaśī vaiṣṇavī tithiḥ |
śravaṇena samāyuktā kadācidyadi labhyate || 3||
śuklapakṣe dvijaśreṣṭha vijayā sā prakīrtitā |
upoṣyā sā prayatnena sarvapāpapraṇāśanī || 4 ||
yā tu puṣyeṇa saṃyuktā phālgunasya sitā tu vai |
sā jayā dvādaśī nāma sarvapāpakṣayaṃkarī || 5 ||
kṛtārtho jāyate martyastāmupoṣya dvijottama |
tasyāṃ snātaḥ sadā snāto bhavedvai nātra saṃśayaḥ || 6 ||
saṃpūjya vastrapuṣpādyaiḥ phalaṃ sāyaṃ samaśnute |
ekaṃ jatrā sahasrasya japtasyā''noti vai phalam || 7||
dānaṃ sahasraguṇitaṃ tathā vai viprabhojanam |
homaścaivopavāsaśca sahasrasya phalapradaḥ || 8 ||
ṛcamekāmadhīte yo vimaḥ śraddhāsamanvitaḥ |
ṛgvedasya samagrasya sadaiva phalamaśrute || 9 ||
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ svalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu |
tanāśayati govindaratarayāmabhyarcya yatnataḥ || 10 ||
yaśvopavāsaṃ kurute tasyāṃ snāto dvijottama |
sarvapāpavinirmukto viṣṇuloke mahīyate || 11 ||
yaḥ kṛtvā dvādaśīmimāṃ kṣapayedbhaktimānnaraḥ |
brahmaṇo divasaṃ yāvattāvatsvarge mahīyate || 12 ||
tasmindine tu saṃprāpte yatkartavyaṃ bravīmyaham |
ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāro dvādaśyāṃ viṣṇumarcayet || 13 ||
gandhapuṣpopahāraiśca vividhairvidhivannaraḥ |
matsyā pādau prathamaṃ kūrmāya ca tathā kaṭim || 14 ||
varāhāyeti jaṭharaṃ narasiṃhāya vā uraḥ |
vāmanāyeti vai kaṇṭhaṃ bhujaṃ rāmadvayeti ca || 15 |
yajedrāmeti ca mukhaṃ pradyumnāyeti nāsikām |
kṛṣṇanāmnā ca netre dve buddhanāmnā tathā śiraḥ || 16 ||
aferral art haānvāmaneti ca sarvataḥ |
bhaktyā cāssrādhya govindaṃ gopālaṃ ca tathā niśi || 17 ||
tatastasyāgrataḥ śuddhaṃ nyasetkṛṣṇājinaṃ budhaḥ |
tasyopari tilānāṃ tu kṛṣṇānāmāḍhakaṃ nyaset || 18 ||
madhyataḥ prasthamekaṃ tu daridraḥ kuḍavaṃ tathā |
tilālābhe yavāḥ kāryā godhūmāratadalābhataḥ || 19 ||
sukhaṃ tatra phalaṃ brahmastilaiḥ mābhoti mānavaḥ |
sauvarṇa raupyaṃ tāmraṃ vā pātraṃ kuryātsvaśaktitaḥ || 20 ||
pracchādya pātraṃ vāsobhirahataiḥ suparīkṣitaiḥ |
sauvarṇa vāmanaṃ kṛtvā sākṣasūtra kamaṇḍalum || 21 ||
yathāśaktyā kṛtaṃ haravaṃ kṛtayajñopavītinam |
evaṃrūpaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā vāmanaṃ bhaktimānnaraḥ || 22 ||
sthāpayettantupātrasthaṃ bhaktyā samyagupoṣitaḥ |
puṣpairgandhaiḥ phalairdhūpaiḥ kālotthairarcayeddharim || 23 ||.
matsyaḥ kūrmo varāhaśca nārasiṃho'tha vāmanaḥ || 24 ||
rāmo rāmaśca kṛṣṇaśca buddhaḥ kalkī ca te daśa |
aitairmanapadairdevaṃ naivedyaiśva prapūjayet || 25 ||
bhaktasyātra viśeṣeṇa phalaṃ koṭiguṇottaram |
tatastasya samīpe tu dadhibhaktaṃ ghaṭe nyaset || 26 ||
karakaṃ vāripūrṇa ca sugandhadravyasaṃyutam |
chatraṃ caivākṣasūtraṃ ca pāduke guḍikāṃ tathā || 27 ||
evaṃ saṃpūjya vidhivaddevadevaṃ janārdanam |
jāgaraṃ tatra kurvīta gītavādināditaiḥ || 28 ||
evaṃ sarvarajanyante prabhāte vimale sati |
pradeyaṃ śāstraviduṣe brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine || 29 |
viṣṇubhaktāya śāntāya viśeṣeṇa dīyate |
gurau ca sati nānyasmai dātavyamiti niścitam || 30 ||
vedādhyetre samaṃ dānaṃ dviguṇaṃ tadvide tathā |
ācārye dānamekaṃ ca sahastraguṇitaṃ tathā || 31 ||
gurau sati tato'nyasya vrataṃ yaśca nivedayet |
sa durgatimavāprati dattaṃ bhavati niṣphalam || 32 ||
avidyo vā savidyo vā gurureva janārdanaḥ |
mārgastho vā vimārgastho gurureva sadā gatiḥ || 33 ||
pratipannaṃ guruṃ yaiśva mohādvipratipadyate |
sa janmakoṭiṃ narake pacyate puruṣādhamaḥ || 34 ||
evaṃ dattvā vidhānena brāhmaṇāya ca bhaktitaḥ |
mantreṇānena dātavyaṃ purāṇapaṭhitena ca || 35 ||
mantreṇa pratigṛhṇīyādbrāhmaṇaśca dvijottama |
vāmano buddhido dātā dravyastho vāmanaḥ svayam || 36 ||
vāmano'sya pradātā vai vāmanāya namo namaḥ || iti dānamantraḥ |
vāmanaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vāmano vai dadāti ca |
vāmanastārako dvābhyāṃ vāmanāya namo namaḥ ||37||
iti pratigrahamantraḥ |
annaṃ prajāpatirviṣṇurudrendraśaśibhāskarāḥ |
anirvāyuryamaścaiva pāpaṃ haratu me sadā || 38 ||
ityannadānamantraḥ |
parjanyo varuṇaḥ sūryaḥ salilaṃ keśavaḥ śivaḥ |
svaṣṭā yamo vaiśravaṇaḥ pāpaṃ haratu me sadā ||39||
iti saliladānamanyaḥ |
viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ dattvā yathāśaktyatha dakṣiṇām |
pṛṣadājyaṃ ca saṃprāśya paścādbhuñjīta vāgyataḥ || 40 ||
bhūyo yathecchayā rātrau sarvatraiṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ |
samāpite vrate tasminbrahmaśṛṇu ca yatphalam || 41 ||
brahmaṇaḥ pralayaṃ yāvattāvatsvarge mahīyate |
brahmalokādilokeṣu bhuktvā bhogānanekaśaḥ || 42 ||
punaḥ svargādbhuvaṃ prāpya jāyate mahatāṃ kule |
saptadvīpādhipatyaṃ ca prāpnuyānnātra saṃśayaḥ || 43 ||
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti tato muktiṃ ca gacchati |
indrasyāvarajo devo ramāhṛdayanandanaḥ || 44 ||
balirvaddhastvayā deva gṛhāṇārghyaṃ tu vāmana || ityarghyamantraḥ |
itīdaṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ paṭhevatamanuttamam |
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ śravaṇadvādaśīphalāt || 45 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtayājñavalkyasaṃvāde śravaṇa- dvādaśīvratakathanaṃ nāma pañcadaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 15 ||
sūta uvāca -
anyadvratamidaṃ vakṣye śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ |
saubhāgyavardhanaṃ puṇyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam || 1 ||
sarvaduṣṭopaśamanaṃ sarvaiśvaryamadaṃ śivam |
yaṃ yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ taṃ taṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ || 2 ||
purā devena rudreṇa dagdhaḥ kāmo durāsadaḥ |
upoṣitā tithistena tenānaṅgatrayodaśī || 3 ||
śuklapakṣe trayodaśyāṃ māsi mārgaśire dvijāḥ |
snānaṃ kṛtvā'tha vidhinā sopavāso jitendriyaḥ || 4 ||
bhaktyā tvananyayā devaṃ pūjayecchaśiśekharam |
puṣpairnānāvidhairdhūpairnaivedyaiśva phalaistathā || 5
śaṃbhunānā tilaihoṃmaṃ kuryādaṣṭottaraṃ śatam |
anaṅganāmnā saṃpūjya madhu prāśya svapenniśi || 6 ||
daśānāmaśvamedhānāṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ |
yogeśvaraṃ susaṃpūjya pauṣe prāśrīta candanam || 7 ||
rājasūyasya yajñasya phailamānoti mānavaḥ |
nāṭeśvaraṃ susaṃpūjya māghamāse jitendriyaḥ || 8 ||
mauktikaṃ prāśya viprendrāḥ phalaṃ tasya vadāmyaham |
bahusvarṇasya yajñasya phalaṃ śataguṇaṃ bhavet || 9 ||
saṃpūjya phālgune vīraṃ kaḍūnelaṃ prāśayonārī |
gomedhasya phalaṃ prāpya modate devarāḍiva || 10 ||
surūpaṃ nāmaṃ vai caitre citraratnavinirmitam |
karpūraṃ prāśayedrātrau naramedhaphalaṃ labhet || 11 ||
vaiśākhe ca mahārūpaṃ deveśaṃ ca prapūjayet |
jātīphalaṃ ca saṃprāśya gosahasraphalaṃ labhet || 12 ||
jyeṣṭhe pradyumnanāmānaṃ lavaṅgaṃ prāśayenniśi |
vājapeyasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇottaram || 13 ||
umābhartetināmānamāṣāḍhe saṃprapūjayet |
tilodakaṃ tu saṃprāśya puṇḍarīkaphalaṃ labhet || 14 ||
pūjayecchrāvaṇe śūlapāṇinaṃ parameśvaram |
prāśayedgandhatoyaṃ tu abhiṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet || 15 ||
māse bhādrapade vimāḥ sadyojātaṃ prapūjayet |
agaruṃ prāśayitvā tu sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet || 16 ||
māse cāśvayuje prāpte tridaśādhipatiṃ yajet |
svarṇodakaṃ tu saṃprāśya svarṇakoṭiphalaṃ labhet || 17 ||
viśveśvaraṃ ca kārtikyāṃ pūjayedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ |
madanaraya phalaṃ prāśya kāmavatdyutimānbhavet || 18 ||
pratimāsaṃ pravakṣyāmi dantakāṣṭhāni vai dvijāḥ |
mallikā khādiraṃ caiva lakṣāpāmārgajaṃ tathā || 19||
jambudumbarajāśvatthaṃ mālatī vaṭajaṃ tathā |
mālatyāḥ prathamaṃ tāvattato marutrakaṃ tathā || 21 ||
karavīraṃ tathā kundamarkapatrāṇi suvratāḥ |
tato mandārapuṣpāṇi mallikākusumāni ca || 22 ||
kādambaṃ yūthikāpuṣpaṃ dhatturaṃ śatapatrakam |
durvāṅkurāṇi deyāni naivedyāni yathākramam || 23 ||
odanaṃ kṛśaraṃ caina śarkarāmodakāstathā |
kaṃsāraṃ yāvakāstatra tataḥ sauhālikā bhavet || 24 ||
pañcakhādyaṃ paraṃ proktaṃ ghṛtapūramanantaram |
śālibhaktena naivedyaṃ guṇakāratadanantaram || 25 ||
nānāvidhānaṃ naivedyaṃ kārtikyāṃ parikalpayet |
pūjānāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ || 26 ||
śaṃkarāya namaḥ pādau gauye gulphe śivāya ca |
śivāyai jānunī pūjya śaṃbhavāyodbhavāya ca || 27 ||
kaiṭiṃ manmathanāśāya madanāyai surerśvare |
nābhi bhavāya saṃpūjya bhavānyai nama ityumām || 28 ||
vakṣo devādhidevāya aparṇāyai namaḥ śivām |
ratanau viśveśvarāyeti surakāntyai namo namaḥ || 29 ||
kaṇṭha bhīmograrūpāya girijāyai namaḥ śivām |
skandhaṃ tridaśavandyāya triśūlinyai namaḥ śivām || 35||
bāhū dhūrjayetyuktvā dhūsarāyai namaḥ śivām |
hastau śūladharāyeti śūlinyai nama ityumām || 31 ||
mukhaṃ devasya saṃpūjya vāmadeveti vāstaḥ |
vāmāyai nama ityuktvā nāsāṃ caiva kapāline || 32 ||
mṛḍānyai nama ityuktvā lalāṭaṃ cendudhāriṇe |
alakāyai namaḥ paścātrinetrāya namastathā || 33 ||
tryakṣyai saṃpūjayedevīṃ śiro gaṅgādharāya ca |
kātyāyanīṃ tataḥ pūjya vyomakeśāya vai namaḥ || 34 ||
keśānsaṃpūjya vidhivatkeśinyai ca namo namaḥ |
sāmrapatre tu saṃsthāpya kalaśopāra vinyaset |
śuklavastreṇa saṃchādya saṃpūjya vidhivadvijāḥ || 36 ||
ācāryāyātha taṃ dadyādvittaśāyyavivarjitaḥ |
kalaśāḥ sodakā deyā brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sadakṣiṇāḥ || 37 ||
brāhmaṇānbhojayedbhaktyā śivabhaktiparāyaṇān |
evaṃ karoti yo viprā bhaktyā'naṅgatrayodaśīm || 38 ||
prāpnoti rājyaṃ saubhāgyaṃ putrāṃśca cirajīvinaḥ |
śivalokaṃ ca saṃprāpya śaṃbhoḥ priyatamo bhavet || 39 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde'naṅga-trayodaśī- vratakathanaṃ nāma ṣoḍaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 16 ||
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ–
yaduktaṃ bhavatā sūta naiṣkalaṃ jñānamuttamam |
-
śrutaṃ cākhilamasmābhirmanāṃsi hṛṣitāni naḥ || 1 ||
bhaktiśca śāśvate śaṃbhau jātā'smākaṃ hi śāśvatī |
varṇāśramācāravidhimidānīṃ brūhi tattvataḥ || 2 ||
sūta uvāca -
caturṇāmapi varṇānāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣyāmi suvratāḥ |
yaduktaṃ bhānunā pūrve manave parameṣṭhine || 3 ||
yena viśveśvaraḥ śaṃbhuḥ karmayogarataiḥ sadā |
ārādhyate na cānyena ityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ || 4 ||
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaśturthaḥ śūdra ucyate |
varṇāścatvāra evaite traya ādyā dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ || 5 ||
gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho yatistathā |
catvāraśvā''śramārateṣāṃ pañcamo nopapadyate || 6 ||
sarveṣāmāśramāṇāṃ ca vihitaṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam |
na daṇḍena vinā kaśvidāśramīti nigadyate || 7 ||
brahmacārī bhaveddaṇḍī kṛṣṇājinadharaistathā |
mekhalī ca tathā muṇḍī śikhī vā yadi vā jaṭī || 8 ||
bhikṣāhāreṇa satataṃ vartanaṃ tasya suvratāḥ |
agnikārya tathā kuryātsāyaṃ prātaryathāvidhi || 9 ||
amikāryaparityāgī patitaḥ sarvakarmasu |
snātvā saṃtarpya devādīndevatābhyarcanaṃ tataḥ || 10 ||
abhivādanaśīlaḥ syādvṛddheṣu ca yathākramam |
kṛte'bhivādane kuryānnaiva pratyabhivādanam || 11 |
karoti nābhivādyo'sau yathā śūdrastathaiva saḥ |
ādhyātmikaṃ vaidikaṃ vā tathā laukikameva vā || 12 ||
ādadīta guroryasmāttaṃ pūrvamabhivādayet |
asāvahamiti brūyātpratyutthāya yavīyasaḥ || 13 ||
nābhivāyāstu vipreṇa kṣatriyādyāḥ kathaṃcana |
śiṣṭānāṃ ca gṛhānnityaṃ bhikṣāmāhṛtya suvrataḥ || 14 ||
nivedya gurave'śrīyādvāgyatastadanujñayā |
bhaikṣeṇa vartanaṃ nityaṃ naikānnādī vratī bhavet || 15 ||
upavāsasamā bhikṣā proktā vai brahmacāriṇām |
anārogyamanāyuṣyamasvargyaṃ cātibhojanam || 16 ||
apuṇyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ tasmāttatparivarjayet |
prāṅmukho'nnādi bhuñjīta sūryābhimukha eva vā || 17 ||
nābādadaṅmukho nityaṃ vidhireṣa sanātanaḥ |
pādau prakṣālya vidhivadācamya prayato dvijaḥ || 18 ||
bhuñjīta maunī satataṃ smaredevaṃ sadāśivam |
sopānatko jalastho vā̃ noṣṇīṣī cā''camedbudhaḥ || 19 ||
na caiva varṣadhārābhirna tiṣṭhanpralapanna ca |
prāśnīyātrirapaḥ pūrvaṃ brāhmaṇa prayato dvijaḥ || 20 ||
saṃvṛttā mūlena mukhaṃ caivamupaspṛśet |
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ ca saṃspṛśennayanadvayam || 21 ||
aṅguṣṭhatarjanībhyāṃ ca saṃspṛśenāsikāpuṭe |
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayogena spṛśecchratrayugaṃ dvijaḥ || 22 ||
sarvābhiraṅgulībhiśca hṛdayaṃ ca talena vā |
saṃspṛśedvai śirastadvadaṅguṣṭhenāthavā dvayam || 23 ||
vinyasya dakṣiṇe karṇe brahmasūtramudaṅmukhaḥ |
divā mūtrapurīṣe ca śarvaryā dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ || 24 ||
ācchādya parṇairvasudhāṃ tṛṇairvā maunasaṃyutaḥ |
śiraḥ prāhṛtya viprendrā nānyathā ca kadācana || 25 ||
pathi goṣṭhe nadītīre chāyāyāṃ kūpasaṃnidhau |
tuṣāṅgārakapāleṣu na kṣetre na catuṣpathe || 26 ||
nodyāne na śmaśāne ca na paśyaṃstārakādikān |
na caivābhimukhaḥ strīṇāṃ gurubrāhmaṇayorgavām || 27 ||
śaucaṃ paścātprakurvīta gandhalepakṣayāvadhi |
āntaraṃ manasaḥ śuddhiryathā bhavati tadvijāḥ || 28 ||
jitendriyaḥ syātsatataṃ vaśyātmā'krodhanaḥ śuciḥ |
prayuñjīta sadā vācaṃ madhurāṃ hitabhāṣiṇīm || 29 ||
paropaghātaṃ paiśanyaṃ kaॉma lobhaṃ tathaiva ca |
dyūtaṃ janaparīvādaṃ strī velyālambhanaṃ tathā || 30 ||
gandhamālyaṃ rasaṃ chatraṃ varjayeddantadhāvanam |
sarva paryuṣitaṃ varṇya kṛtaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ tathā || 31 ||
malāpakarṣaṇaṃ snānaṃ śūdrādyairabhibhāṣaṇam |
guroravajñāṃ satataṃ brahmacārī vivarjayet || 32 ||
udakumbhaṃ sumanaso gośakṛnmṛttikī kuśān |
gurvarthamāharennityaṃ bhaikṣaṃ cāharahaścaret || 33 ||
ācamya saṃyato nityamadhīyīta chudaṅmukhaḥ |
upasaṃgṛhya tatpādau vīkṣamāṇo gurormukham || 34 ||
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vedaścakṣuḥ sanātanam |
vedaḥ śreyaskaraḥ puṃsāṃ nānya ityabravīdraviḥ || 35 ||
anadhītya dvijo yastu śāstrāṇi subahūnyapi |
śṛṇoti brāhmaṇo nāsau narakāṇi prapadyate || 36 ||
nādhītavidyo yo vima ācāreṣu pravartate |
nāsscāraphalamāpnoti yathā śūdrastathaiva saḥ || 37 ||
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ yaccānyatkarma vaidikam |
anadhītasya viprasya sarvaṃ bhavati niṣphalam || 38 ||
anadhītasya viprasya putro vā'dhyayanānvitaḥ |
śūdraputraḥ sa vijñeyāṃ na vedaphalamaśrute || 39 ||
vedaṃ vedau tathā vedavedāṃśca caturo dvijāḥ |
adhītya guruve dattvā dakṣiṇāṃ ca bhavedgṛhī || 40 ||
rūpalakṣaṇasaṃyuktāṃ kanyāmuddāhayettataḥ |
amātṛgotraprabhavāmasamānārṣagotrajām || 41 ||
mātṛtaḥ pañcamādūrdhvaṃ pitṛtaḥ saptamāttathā |
agotrakula saṃpanna rogahīnāṃ surūpiṇīm || 42 ||
mātṛtaḥ pañcamādavapitṛttaḥ saptamāttathā |
kanyāṃ vivāhayedyastu gurutalpī bhaveddhi saḥ || 43 ||
brāhmeṇaiva vivāhena daivenāpi tathaiva ca |
ārṣa vai kecidicchanti dharmakāryeṣu garhitam || 44 ||
dhārayedvaiṇavīṃ yaṣṭimantarvāsastathottaram |
yajñopavītadvitayaṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum || 45 ||
chatraṃ coṣṇīpamamalaṃ pāduke vā'pyupāna hau |
raukme ca kuṇḍale nityaṃ kṛttakeśanakhaḥ śuciḥ || 46 ||
śuklāmbaradharo nityaṃ sugandhaḥ priyadarśanaḥ |
na jīrṇamalavadvāsā bhavedvai vibhave sati || 47 ||
ṛtugāmī bhavedvipro niṣiddhatithivarjitaḥ |
paṣṭaṣṭamyau pañcadaśīmamāvāsyāṃ caturdaśīm || 48 ||
brahmacārī bhavennityaṃ janma ca viśeṣataḥ |
ādadītā''vasathyāgniṃ juhuyājjātavedasam || 49 ||
vedoditaṃ varka karma nityaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ |
akurvāṇaḥ patatyāśu nirayānatibhīṣaṇān || 50 ||
kuryādrahmāṇi karmāṇi saṃdhyopāsanameva ca |
pāpaṃ na gṛhayedvidvānna dharma khyāpayetkacit |
vayasaḥ karmaṇo'rthasya śrutasyābhijanasya ca || 52 ||
vaiṣavānbuddhisādṛśyamācaranvicaretsadā |
śrutismṛtyuditaḥ samyaksādhubhiryaśca sevitaḥ || 53 ||
tamācāraṃ niṣeveta sādhūnvakṣyāmi sāṃpratam |
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye madhyadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 54 ||
tatrotpannā dvijā̃ ye vai sāghavaste prakīrtitāḥ |
yastairanuṣṭhito dharmaḥ śrutismṛtyo saṃgataḥ || 55 ||
sadācāraḥ sa vai prokto devadevena śaṃbhunā |
kurukṣetrāśca matsyārthe pāñcālāḥ śūrasenajāḥ || 56 ||
ete deśāḥ puṇyadeśāḥ sarve cānye ca ninditāḥ |
deśepaveṣu nivasedrāhmaṇairdharmakāṅkṣibhiḥ || 57 ||
atraiva dṛśyate dharmoṃ nānyatretyabravīdraviḥ |
aṅgavaṅgakaliṅgāṃśca saurāṣṭraṃ gurjaraṃ tathā || 58 ||
ābhīraṃ kauḍūṇaṃ caiva drāviḍaṃ dakṣiṇāpatham |
andhaṃ ca māgadhaṃ caiva deśānetāṃśca varjayet || 59 ||
nityaṃ svādhyāyaśīlaḥ syātpañcayajñaparāyaṇaḥ |
śānto dānto jitakrodho lobhamohavivarjitaḥ || 60 ||
sāvitrījāpyanirataḥ śivabhaktiparāyaṇaḥ |
śrāddhakṛddānanirataḥ kṣamāyukto dayālukaḥ || 61 ||
gṛhasthastu samākhyāto na gṛheṇa gṛhī bhavet |
na śarīraṃ vinā devaḥ pūjyate girijāpatiḥ || 62 ||
brahmacārī gṛhastho vā vānaprastho'thavā yatiḥ |
śivabhaktiyutaṃ karma kurvanmucyeta bandhanāt || 63 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde varṇāśramācāra- vidhikathanaṃ māma saptadaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 17 ||
sūta uvāca -
vadenaivābhiyaṃ vākyaṃ nānṛtaṃ na ca marmabhit |
na hiṃsyātsarvabhūtāni na vedānāṃ ca kutsanam || 1 ||
nindakānāṃ maheśasya śuddhirna khalu dṛśyate || 3 ||
jalaṃ tṛṇaṃ vā śākaṃ vā mṛdaṃ vā kāṣṭhameva vā |
parasyāpaharajñjanturnarakaṃ pratipadyate || 4 ||
nityayacanako na syādyācitaṃ naiva yācayet. |
prāṇānapaharatyeṣa yācakastasya durmatiḥ || 5 ||
grahītavyāni puṣpāṇi devārcanavidhau dvijaiḥ |
naikasmādeva niyatamananujñāya kevalam || 6 ||
tṛṇaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ prakāśaṃ vai haredbudhaḥ |
dharmārtha hai aur nyathā patito bhavet || 7 ||
tilamudrayavādīnāṃ muṣṭiryādyā yadi sthitaiḥ |
kṣudhārtarnānyadā viprairdharmavidbhiriti sthitiḥ || 8 ||
anṛtātpāradāryācca tathā'bhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇāt |
aśrautadharmacaraṇātkṣipraṃ naśyati vai kulam || 9 ||
jñānavṛddhastapovṛddho vayovṛddha iti trayaḥ |
pūrvaḥ pūrvo'bhivādyaḥ syātpūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ || 10 ||
tripuṇḍradhārī satataṃ brāhmaṇaḥ sarvakarmasu |
bhasmanaivāgrihotrasya śivāgnijanitena vā || 11 ||
na mūkhaiḥ saha saṃvāsaḥ patitairna kadācana |
vedanindāratenaiva na cāpīśvaranindakaiḥ || 12 ||
paiśunyaṃ śuṣkavairāṇi vivādaṃ varjayetsadā |
dhayantīṃ gāṃ parakṣetre na cā''cakṣīta kasyacit || 13 ||
bahubhirna virodhaṃ ca kuryānna kṛtibhistathā |
tithiṃ pakṣasya na brūyānakṣatrāṇi na nirdiśet || 14 ||
na pāpaṃ pāpināṃ brūyāttathā'pāpamapāpinām |
satyena tulyadoṣī syādasatyena dvidoṣabhāk || 15 ||
yāni mithyābhiśastānāṃ patantyaśrṛṇi rodanāt |
tāni putrānpaśūnghnanti teṣāṃ mithyābhiśaṃsinām || 16 ||
brahmahatyā surāpānaṃ steyaṃ gurvaṅgannāgamaḥ |
dṛṣṭaṃ virodhanaṃ vṛddhairnārita midhyābhiśaṃsini || 17 ||
mānaṃ madaṃ tathā śokaṃ dveṣaṃ ca parivarjayet |
ravivāre na kurvīta bhṛṣṭabhairavabhakṣaṇam || 18 ||
dhanakāmo janaḥ satyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā |
ravivāre tu lavaṇaṃ varjya bhojanapātrake || 19 ||
tathā tailopamarde ca dhanakāmena bhūtale |
na kuryātkasyacitpīḍāṃ sutaṃ śiṣyaṃ ca tāḍayet || 20 ||
na nadīṣu nadīṃ brūyātparvateṣu ca parvatam |
pravāse bhojane cāpi na tyajetsahayāyinam || 21 ||
śirobhyaṅgāvaśiṣṭena tailenāṅgaṃ na lepayet |
ne sarpaśastraiḥ krīḍeta svāni khāni na saṃspṛśet || 22 ||
na saṃhatābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kaṇḍūyedātmanaḥ śiraḥ |
na laukikaiḥ ratavairdevāṃratoṣayedvāhya jairapi || 23 ||
na dantairnakharomāṇi cchindyātsu na bodhayet |
na bālātapamā sevettamaṃ vivarjayet || 24 ||
nāśuddho' paricarena devānkīrtaye dṛṣīn |
na vāmahastenojanya pitre kutre |
vā jalam || 25 ||
kareṇaikena yadvāri pītaṃ tanmadirāsamam |
viśveśvaramumākāntaṃ viśvāntaryāmiṇaṃ vibhum || 26 ||
na brahmādyaiḥ samaṃ brūyācchaktibhirna ca pārvatīm |
brūyādyadi samaṃ śaṃbhuṃ brahmaviṣṇvādibhiḥ suraiḥ || 27 ||
yaḥ kaścittamasā''viṣṭaḥ kadācinnaiva taṃ spṛśet |
sarvasmādadhikaṃ brūyādbhagavantamumāpatim || 28 ||
tathā devīṃ ca girijāṃ dvijaiḥ śreyorthibhiḥ sadā |
parastriyaṃ na bhāṣeta nāyājyaṃ yājayedvijāḥ || 29 ||
na nindedyoginaḥ siddhāntratino no yatastathā || 30 ||
na cāsskāmedgurośchāyāṃ na tatho''jñāṃ guroḥ sadā |
vakṣyamāṇena vidhinā snānaṃ kuryātsamāhitaḥ || 31 ||
bhūmiṃ vyāhṛtibhiḥ spṛṣṭrā khanamānaṃ dhru cāśayā |
? uddhṛtā'sīti saṃgṛhya gandhadvāreti gomayam || 32 ||
apāghamityapāmārga dūrvā saṃgṛhya durvayā |
jalatīraṃ samāsādya śucau deśe samāhitaḥ || 33 ||
ādityā iti saṃprokṣya kūlaṃ tīrthasya suvrataḥ |
śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya gāyatryā prokṣayettataḥ || 34 ||
bhāgadvayaṃ sa tāṃ paścādekaṃ dikṣu visarjayet |
yata indrādimatraiśca caturbhistu yathākramam || 35 ||
avagāhya jale paścāttīre caivopaviśya ca |
avaśiṣṭena bhāgena mantraiśvā''lepayetkramāt || 36 ||
akṣībhyāmitimantreṇa mukhamālepayedbudhaḥ |
grīvābhyāmiti ca grīvāṃ tallina tathā bhujau || 37 ||
śarīraṃ yajñamuktvā'tha hṛdayaṃ parilepayet |
nābhimānandanandeti śiṣṭaṃ mūrdhni vinikṣipet || 38 ||
mūrdhānamitimantreṇa tiladūrvākṣatādikam |
hiraṇyaśṛṅgamityuktvā tīrthaṃ saṃprārthya buddhimān || japecchuddhamatiḥ paścātsūktaṃ caivāghamarṣaṇam || 39 ||
dvipadāṃ ca japedevīṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanīm |
idaṃ tu vāruṇaṃ snānaṃ mantrasnānamathocyate || 40 ||
tu āgneyaṃ bhasmanā snānaṃ vāyavyaṃ rajasā mavām |
divyamātapavarṣeṇa tattu kāryamanantaram || 41 ||
ārdreṇa vāsasā cānyanmānasaṃ śivacintanam |
svānānāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ mānasaṃ snānamuttamam || 42 ||
atra khanitvā ca śalākayetyapekṣitamiti pratibhāti |
uktvā'tha hṛdayamityādi
tato darbhāsane sthitvā gāyatrī prajapedvijaḥ || 44 ||
traivarṇikānāṃ sarveṣāṃ gāyatrī paramā gatiḥ |
yadgāyatryāḥ paraṃ tattvaṃ devadevo maheśvaraḥ || 45 ||
iti jñātvā japedvidvān gāyatryāḥ phalamaśnute |
yo hyanyathā tu manute gāyatrī śivarūpiṇīm || 46 ||
pacyate sa mahāghore narake kalpasaṃkhyayā |
pādācatvāro gāyatryā vedācatvāra eva te || 47 ||
viraściviṣṇusdeśāḥ pādānāṃ devatāḥ kramāt |
evaṃ jñātvā vidhānena gāyatrī vedamātaram || 48 japenmāheśvaraṃ jyotirnityameva prakāśate |
upatiṣṭhedathā''dityaṃ rudrarūpiṇamavyayam || 49 ||
bhaktaiḥ stotraiśca mantraiśca vedetihāsasaṃbhavaiḥ |
pāvamānāni sūktāni brahmayajñaprasiddhaye || 50 ||
japetsamāhito bhūtvā rudrāṃścaiva viśeṣataḥ |
maunenā''gatya bhavanaṃ pūjayecchivamavyayam || 51 ||
ṣaḍakṣareṇa mantreṇa mānastokyā tathaiva ca |
praḍakṣarātparo mantro vedeṣu ca caturṣvapi || 52 ||
nāstītyuvāca bhagavāndevadevaḥ svayaṃ raviḥ |
patraiḥ puṣpaiḥ phalairvāpi dūrvābhiruda kairapi || 53 ||
nāsaṃpūjya mahādevaṃ bhuñjīta brāhmaṇaḥ sadā |
brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ karmiṇāṃ yogināmapi || 54 ||
gatirviśveśvaro devo bhavo nānya iti śrutiḥ |
kuryātpañca mahāyajñāngṛhasthaḥ śraddhayā'nvitaḥ || 55 ||
pañcayajñaparityāgādāśramoṃdavahīyate |
devayajño bhūtayajñaḥ pitṛyajñastathā'paraḥ || 56 ||
mānuṣo brahmayajñaśca pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
hutaśeṣeṇa bhūtebhyo bālaṃ bhūtamakhaṃ viduḥ |
vipraṃ tu bhojayedekaṃ pitṛnuddiśya yatnataḥ || 58 ||
nityaśrāddhaṃ tadṛddhiṃ pitṛyajñaṃ pracakṣate |
yathāśaktyannumudṛtya padadyādrāhmaṇāya vai || 59 ||
atithiṃ pūjayedbhaktyā śivabhāvasamanvitaḥ |
so'tithiḥ svargasopānamiti devo'bravīdraviḥ || 60 ||
madadyādvratakāraṃ vā bhikṣāṃ ca bhavabhāvataḥ |
akṣayaṃ tatphalaṃ prāhurbhavabhāvo hi durlabhaḥ || 61 ||
vedābhyāsarato nityaṃ tadvicārarato bhavet |
brahmayajñaḥ samuddiṣṭo brahmalokaphalapradaḥ || 62 ||
etānkṛtvaiva satataṃ bhuñjītā''śramedharmabhiḥ |

anyathā yo hi bhuṅkte'nnaṃ pretya śūkaratāṃ vrajet || 63||
yadi viśveśvare sthāṇī bhaktirekaiva niścalā |
kiṃ taiḥ pañcamahāyajñairanyaiva vividhairmakhaiḥ || 64 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde dvijadharma- kathanaṃ nāmāṣṭādaśo'dhyāyaḥ || 18 ||
sūta uvāca -
śrāddhaṃ darśe'tha kartavyamaṣṭakāsvayanadvaye |
viṣuve ca vyatīpāte tīrtheṣu ca viśeṣataḥ || 1 ||
parīkṣya brāhmaṇānsamyagvedavedāṅgapāragān |
viśeṣācchivabhaktāṃśca rudrajāpyaparāyaṇān || 2 ||
abhāve śivabhaktānāṃ sadācāraratāndvijān |
bhojayecchraddhayā śrāddhe śivabuddhayā samāhitaḥ || 3 ||
vratopavāsaniratāḥ somapāḥ saṃyatendriyāḥ |
agnihotraparāḥ śāntā vahcā gurupūjakāḥ || 4 ||
triṇāciketāḥ śiṣyāśca trimadhutrisuparṇikāḥ |
mantrabrāhmaṇavettāraḥ purāṇaramṛtipāṭhakāḥ || 5 ||
adhyātmaśāstraniratā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ |
ekaṃ vā bhojayedvimaṃ śivabhaktiparāyaṇam || 6 ||
tena pūtā bhavantyeva ye kecitpaṅktidūṣakāḥ |
vadhabandhopajīvī ca vṛṣalaḥ śūdrayojakāḥ || 7 ||
vedavikrayiṇaścaiva śrutivikrayiṇastathā |
vedavikrayiṇaścānye kopinaḥ kuṇḍagolakau || 8 ||
kāyasthā lambakarṇāśca nityaṃ rājopasevakāḥ |
nakṣatratithivaktāro bhiṣakśāstropajīvinaḥ || 9||
vyādhinaḥ kāvyakartāro gāyakācaiva gotriṇaḥ |
vedanindāratāścaiva kṛtaghnāḥ piśunāstathā || 10 ||
hīnātirikta dehāśca śrāddhe varjyāḥ prayatnataḥ |
brahmahatyāmavāmoti yadi strīgamanaṃ bhavet || 11 ||
adhvānaṃ kalahaṃ krodhaṃ putrabhāryāditāḍanam |
śrāddhabhojī bhavedyo hi tadine parivarjayet || 12 ||
prakṣālayettataḥ pādāvarcite maṇḍale śubhe |
caturastraṃ brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyasya trikoṇakam || 13 ||
vartulaṃ caitra vaiśyasya śūdrasyābhyukṣaṇaṃ smṛtam |
upaveśya tato viprāndattvā caitra kuśāsanam || 14 ||
paścācchrāddhasya rakṣārthaṃ tilāṃśca vikirettataḥ |
viśvedevānathā''hūya viśvedevāsa ityṛcā || 15 ||
śaṃnodevyā jalaṃ kṣiptvā sapavitre tu bhājane |
yavānyavo'sīti tathā gandhapuṣpaṃ ca nikṣipet |
|| 16 ||
yā divyā iti mantreṇa haste'pyairghyaṃ vinikṣipet |
madadyādgandhamālyādi dhūpaṃ vāsāṃsi śaktitaḥ || 17 ||

japedāyantu na ṛcaṃ tilo'sīti nilāṃstathā |
kṣipadairdhya yathāpūrva vipahaste samāhitaḥ || 19 ||
saṃstravānprakṣipetpātre nyubjaṃ caiva yathā bhavet |
pitṛbhyaḥ sthānamasīti tato'naukaraṇaṃ matam || 20 |
agnau kariṣya ityuktvā kuruṣvetyabhyanujñayā |
annaṃ ghṛtaplutaṃ vahnau juhuyātpitṛyajñavat || 21 ||

mahādevasya purato goṣṭhe vā śraddhayā'nvitaḥ || 22 ||

kecidapyevamicchanti naiva bhānormataṃ dvijāḥ || 23||
vividhaṃ pāyasaṃ dadyādbhakṣyāṇi subahūnyapi |

vividhānyapi māṃsāni pitṛṇāṃ prītipūrvakam |
dattānyapi niṣiddhāni śrāddhaṃ naivākṣayaṃ bhavet || 25 ||
nāśnāti yo dvijo māṃsaṃ niyuktaḥ pitṛkarmaṇi |
sa pretya narakaṃ yāti paśutvaṃ ca prapadyate || 26 ||
dharmaśāstraṃ purāṇaṃ ca tathā'tharvaśirastathā |
rudrāṃśca pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ brāhmaṇāñśrāvayettataḥ || 27 ||
bhuñjīranbrāhmaṇāḥ sarve vāgyatā ghṛtabhojanāḥ |
vikiraṃ nikṣipetpaścāccheṣamannamathābravīt || 28||
hastaprakṣālanaṃ dattvā kuryādvai svastivācanam |
dādvai dakṣiṇāṃ śaktyā svadhākāramudīrayet || 29 ||
dātāro no'bhivardhantāṃ vājevājeti vai ṛcam |
japtvā ca brāhmaṇānstutvā namaskṛtya visarjayet || 30 ||

svādhyāyaṃ ca tathā'dhvānaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet || 31 ||

sūta uvāca -
atha dharmo vanasthānāmucyate śṛṇuta dvijāḥ |
prīto bhavatu yenāsau bhagavānbhaganetrahā || 1 ||

putreṣu bhāryā nikṣipya vanaṃ gacchedvijottamaḥ || 2 ||

dayāṃ ca sarvabhūteṣu na kuryānniśi bhojanam |

sūta uvāca -
tataḥ sasarja bhagavāndevo'sāvātmanaḥ sutān |
sanātanaṃ ca sanakaṃ sanandanamathāpi ca || 1 ||
śaṃbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca pañcaitānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ |
na sṛṣṭau dadhire buddhiṃ śivaikadhyānatatparāḥ || 2 ||
sṛṣṭau teṣvanapekṣeṣu mohāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ |
vapastatāpa paramaṃ na kiṃcitpratyapadyata || 3 ||
gate bahutithe kāle samabhūtkrodhamūrcchitaḥ |

rodayitvā'bjajanmānaṃ tasmādrudra iti smṛtaḥ |
anyāni sapta nāmāni śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ || 6 ||
bhavaḥ śarvastatheśānaḥ paśūnāṃ patireva ca |
bhīmogro mahādeva iti nāmāni sattamāḥ || eit
bhūmirāpo'nalo vāyuvyoma sūrya candramāḥ |
aṣṭamī dīkṣitastatra mūrtirīśasya śūlinaḥ || 8 ||

nīlakaṇṭhāṃstrinetrāṃśca jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitān |
vṛṣadhvajānvītarāgāñjarāmaraṇavarjitān || 11 ||
sarvajña śatakoṭīṃstānsarvānugrāhiṇaḥ parān |
dṛṣṭvā tānvividhānrudrānviraściḥ māha śaṃkaram || 12 ||
jarāmaraṇanirmuktāmīdṛśīṃ mā sṛjaḥ prajām |

rudrairātmasamudbhūtaiḥ krīḍāyuktastadā'bhavat |

draṣṭṛtvamātmasaṃbodho vaṣiṣṭhātṛtvameva ca || 16 |
avyayāni daśaitāni nityaṃ tiṣṭhanti śaṃkare |

tatastamāha bhagavānbrahmā saṃvīkṣya śaṃkaram |
anugṛhya yathā māṃ tvaṃ putratve dattavānvaram || 18 ||

stotreṇānena tuṣṭāva śirasyādhāya cāñjalim || 19 ||
brahmovāca -
namaste'stu mahādeva namaste parameśvara |
namaḥ śivāya devāya namaste brahmarūpiṇe || 20 ||

sṛjatyaśeṣamevedaṃ yaḥ svakarmānurūpataḥ |
svātmanyavasthitastasmai caturvaktrātmane namaḥ || 39 ||

ātmānubhūtiyogena tasmai viśvātmane namaḥ || 40 ||
bibhārte śirasā nityaṃ dvisaptabhuvanātmakam |
brahmāṇḍaṃ yo'khilādhāraṃ tasmai śeṣātmane namaḥ || 41 ||

yo'ntarā sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantā tiṣṭhatīśvaraḥ |
taṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ devaṃ namaste paramātmane || 43 ||
yasya keśeṣu jīmūtā nadyaḥ sarvāṅgasaṃdhiṣu |

tattvaṃ sadā nirākāraṃ cidrūpaṃ pārameśvaram || 46 ||
= yayā saṃtarate māyāṃ yogī saṃkṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ |
aparāntāmaparyantāṃ tasmai vidyātmane namaḥ || 47 ||

sūta uvāca -
uttānapādasya suto dhruvo nāma mahāmanāḥ |
ārādhya paramaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam || 1 ||

prasādāttasya devasya prāptavānthānamuttamam || 2 ||

sārvabhaumau mahātmānau madbhaktau pitṛtatparau |
evaṃ labdhavaro rājā deveśe puruṣottame || 10 ||

sūta uvāca -
yo'sau śikhaṇḍinaḥ putro brahmacaryāśrame rataḥ |

abhivandya muneḥ pādau śirasā prāñjalirnṛpaḥ || 24 ||
abravīttaṃ muniśreṣṭhaṃ sarvabhūtānukampinam |
adya dhanyaḥ kṛtārtho'smi saphalaṃ jīvitaṃ mama || 25 ||

yattatpāpataṃ yogamanyāśramamiti śruy || 68 ||

sūta uvāca -
svayaṃbhuvā samāviṣṭaḥ pūrva dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ |
prajā sṛjeti rūgīdau rururja ca surāsurān || 1 ||
prajāpateraṇasya kanyāri nīti ditā |
ṣaṣṭiṃ dakṣo'sṛjatkanyā askiyāṃ vai prajāpatiḥ || 2 ||
dadau ca daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa |
saptaviṃśatiṃ somāya cato'riṣṭanemine || 3 ||
dve caiva bahuputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate |
dvai caivāṅgirase tadvadau dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ || 4 ||
sādhyā viśvā ca saṃkalpā muhūrtā ca hyarundhatī |
marutvatī vasurbhānurlambā jāmīti tā daśa || 5 ||
dharmasya patnayastvevāratāsāṃ saṃtatirucyate |
sādhyā babhūvuḥ sādhyāyāṃ viśvāyāṃ viśvadevatāḥ || 6 ||
saṃkalpāyāstu saṃkalpo gṛhatīta murtajāḥ |
arundhatyāstvarundhatyāṃ marutvatyāṃ marutvataḥ || 7 ||
vasottu vasavaḥ proktā bhānoste bhānavaḥ smṛtāḥ |
lambāyāṃ ghoṣanāmāno nāgavīthīstu jāmijāḥ || 8 ||
jyotiṣmantastrayo devā vyāpakāḥ sarvatodiśam |
vasavarate samākhyātāḥ
|| 9 ||
āpo nalaśca somaśca dhruvaścaivānilo'nalaḥ |
pratyūṣaśca prabhāsaśca vasavo'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ || 10 ||
dhruvasya putraḥ kālaḥ syātsarvalokabhayaṃkaraḥ |
viśvakarmā prabhāsasya dharmasyaiṣā tu saṃtatiḥ || 11 ||
aditiya ditiyaiva danurityaparā matā |
ariṣṭā surasā proktā svadhā surabhireva ca || 12 vinatā ca tathā tāmrā kaddū: kodhavaśā virā |
muneśva patnayastvetāḥ kaśyapasya dvijottamāḥ || 13 ||
aṃśurdhātā bhagastvaṣṭā mitro'tha varuṇo'ryamā |
vivasvānsavitā pūṣā aṃśumānviṣṇureva ca || 14 ||
tuṣitā nāma te pūrva cānuṣasyāntare manoḥ |
ādityā aditeḥ putrāḥ proktā vaivasvate'ntare || 15 ||
putradvayaṃ ditiḥ sūte kaśyapānmunipuṃgavāt |
hiraṇyakaśipuṃ tvekaṃ hiraṇyākṣamanantaram || 16 ||
hiraṇyakaśipuryo'sau brahmaṇo varadarpitaḥ |
śakādyā devatāḥ sarvāstena daityena vādhitāḥ || 17 ||
brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatvā procuḥ prāñjalayaḥ surāḥ |

devā ūcu: – devadeva jagannātha caturmukha surottama || 18 ||

bahmovāca-
hiraṇyakaśipurdeva madvareṇātigarvitaḥ |

hantumarhasi taṃ śīghraṃ devānāṃ kāryasiddhaye |

nṛsiṃharūpī bhagavāṃnhiraṇyakaśipoḥ pure || 25 ||
āvirbabhūva bhagavāndevo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ |
muñcannādaṃ mahāghoramasurāṇāṃ bhayaṃkaram || 26 ||

vadhāya preṣayāmāsa prahādādīnmahāsurān || 27 ||

'narasiṃhena te sārdhaṃ yuyudhurdānavāstadā |
prahlādaḥ prāhiṇodrāhmamastraṃ taṃ narakesarim || 29 ||

vinivṛtto'śva saṅgrāmātprahādo daityarāṭ tataḥ |
jñātvā tu bhagavadbhāvaṃ nṛsiṃhatyāmitaujasaḥ || dhyātvāṃ nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ vārayāmāsa dānavān || 34 ||
eṣa nārāyaṇo yogī paramātmā sanātanaḥ |

atha viśvātmako viṣṇuḥ krodhasaṃraktalocanaḥ |
nakhairvidārayāmāsa hiraṇyakaśipuṃ tadā || 37 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde surāsura- sṛṣṭyādikathanaṃ nāmāṣṭāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 28 ||
sūta uvāca -
hate hiraṇyakaśipo prahādo daityasattamaḥ |
hiraṇyākṣaṃ mahābāhuṃ rājye samabhiyojayat ( 3 ) || 1 ||
sospi devānraṇe jitvā svagotte vai palāyitāḥ |
hiraṇyākṣo mahādevaṃ tapasā''rādhya cāntakam || 2 ||
lebhe putraṃ mahābāhuṃ sarvāmaraniṣūdanam |
hiraṇyākṣabhayāddevāḥ śārṅgiṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ || 3 ||
dṛṣṭvā'tha bhagavāndevānhiraṇyākṣavadhāya vai |
vārāhaṃ rūpamāsthāya hiraṇyākṣo niṣūditaḥ || 4 ||
te tasminhiraṇyākṣe prahlādo vaiṣṇavāgraṇīḥ |
tyaktvā tu tāmasī vṛttiṃ svakīyaṃ rājyamāsthitaḥ || 5 ||
tataḥ kadāciddevānāṃ māyayā mohito'bhavat |
kaṃcana brāhmaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛśāṅgaṃ gṛhamāgatam || 6 ||
avajñāmakarodaityaḥ śaptastenāgrajanmanā |
valaṃ yasya samāśritya daitya māmavamanyase || 7 ||
bhaktirvinaśyatu kṣimaṃ tava deve janārdane |
iti śaptvā yayau vipraḥ svāśramaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ || 8 ||
atha daityapatiryuddhamakarodviṣṇunā saha |
piturvadhamanusmṛtya devāśvānye vinirjitāḥ || 9 ||
anugrahādbhagavataḥ pūrvasmādaityarāṭ punaḥ |
tyaktvā māyāmayaṃ sarve śārṅgiṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau || 10 ||
abhiṣicyāndhakaṃ rājye yogayukto'bhavatsvayam |
atha devo mahādevaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarvadehinām || 11 ||
kenāpi hetunā bhikṣāmakarodrāhmaṇaiḥ saha |
saṃsthāpya mandare devīṃ girijāṃ girijāpatiḥ || 12 ||
sanārāyaṇakāndevānakarotpārśvagāśivaḥ |
strīrūpadhāriṇo devāḥ sevante pārvatīṃ tadā || 13 ||
saṃsthāpya nandipramukhānasaṃkhyātāngaṇeśvarān |
mairavaṃ ca samādiśya nandinaṃ dvāradeśataḥ || 14 ||
tataḥ sa bhairavaḥ śaṃbhoḥ śivasyā''jñāṃ vidhāya ca || 25 ||
ādāya sahasā śūlaṃ yayau daityasya saṃgaram |
śūlāgreṇa vinirbhidya nanarta svātmalīlayā || 26 ||
śūlāgre sthāpite daitye brahmādyā munayastadā |
astuvanvividhaiḥ stotraihṛṣṭo lokastadā'bhavat || 27 ||

namāmi mūrdhnā bhagavantamekaṃ samāhitā ṃ yaṃ vidurīśatattvam |

ārṣatvāt |
namo'stu somāyanamadhyamāya namo'stu devāya hiraṇyabāhave ||39||
namo'tiguhyāya guhāntarāya vedāntavijñānaviniścitāya |
trikāladdīnāmaladhāmadhāne namo maheśāya namaḥ śivāya || 40 ||
stavenānena bhagavānprīto bhūtvā'tha bhairavaḥ |
avarodha ca śūlāgrādudāca parameśvaraḥ || 41 ||
tvayā'haṃ stotravaryeṇa toṣito daityapuṃgava |
prīto'smi tava dāsyāmi gāṇapatyaṃ hi durlabham || 42 ||
nandīśvarasamo vatsa bhṛṅgī nāma gaṇo bhava |
evaṃ labdhavaro daityaḥ koṭisūryasamaprabhaḥ || 43 ||
nīlakaṇṭha sinetraśca vṛṣaketurjaṭādharaḥ |
taṃ dṛṣṭvā devatāḥ sarvā harṣanirbharamānasāḥ || 44 ||
tuṣṭuvurgaṇarājaṃ taṃ bhairavasya samīpagam |
atha śaṃbho: samīpasthāṃ devīṃ viśveśvarīṃ śivām || 45 ||
saṃstūya sarvabhāvena śaraṇāgatavatsalām |
putratve jagṛhe daityaṃ prītena manasā śivā || 46 ||
tato'nujñāṃ maheśasya labdhvā'sau kālabhairavaḥ |
mātṛbhiḥ saha viśvātmā pātāle svapuraṃ yayau || 47 ||
viṣṇorbhagavatī mūrtiryatrāste tāmasī parā |
atha tāṃ bhairavo dṛṣṭvā mudā tāṃ pariṣasvaje || 48 ||
ekaiva mūrtirabhavattayo bhairavaśārṅgiṇoḥ |
kālābhairavo yo'sau sa eva nṛhariḥ svayam || 49 ||
bhagavānnṛhariryo'sau sa eva kila bhairavaḥ |
nṛhareḥ pūjanānnūnaṃ prīto bhavati bhairavaḥ || 50 ||
pūjanā bhairavasyaiva nṛhariḥ pūjito bhavet |
ye paśyanti tayorbhedaṃ māyayā mohitā janāḥ || 51 ||
niraye te vipacyante yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam || 52 ||
tasmātpūjyā sadā mūrtī rudranārāyaṇātmikā |
prītā bhūtvā bhagavatī bhavatyajñānahāriṇī || 53 ||
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ prokto mayā'ndhakavadho dvijāḥ |
prādurbhāvo bhairavasya tasya caiva parākramaḥ || 54 ||
imaṃ yaḥ paṭate'dhyāyaṃ mahādevasya saṃnidhau |
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivasyānucaro bhavet || 55 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde hiraṇyākṣavadhā- dikathanaṃ nāmonatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 29 ||
sūta uvāca -
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ mahādo daityasattamaḥ |
andhake nihate daitye tatra rājye sthitaḥ svayam || 1 ||
kṛtvoṃ sa suciraṃ kālaṃ rājyaṃ paramadhārmikaḥ |
rājye virakto matimān śamādiguṇasaṃyutaḥ || 2 ||
rājye matimatāṃ śreṣṭho yabhiṣicya virocanam |
tapovanaṃ gataḥ so'tha vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ || 3 ||
virocanaśca nihato devadevena cakriṇā |
balistasyābhavatputro daityo dharmaparāyaṇaḥ || 4 ||
baddhvā nītaḥ sa pātālaṃ devadevena cakriṇā |
bāṇāsurastasya suto bhakto viśveśvare śive || 5||
dattaṃ bhagavatā tasmai gāṇapatyamanuttamam |
tāraśca śamvaracaiva kapila: śaṃkarastathā || 6 ||
svarbhānurṣṭaṣaparvā ca bāṇasyaite sutā dvijāḥ |
kaśyapātsurasā jajñe khecarānmunipuṃgavāḥ || 7 ||
anantādyāḥ kādraveyā balino balavattarāḥ |
gandharvāñjanayāmāsa tathā'riṣṭā tu kaśyapāt || 8 ||
vinatā janayāmāsa vikhyātau garuḍāruṇau |
paśvādīnsthāvarāntāṃśca tathā'nyānsuṣuvurdvijāḥ || 9 ||
sthāvarāñjaṅgamāṃścaiva samutpādyātha kaśyapaḥ |
punaḥ saṃtānahṛddhyarthaṃ tatāpa paramaṃ tapaḥ || 10 ||
tapaḥprabhāvātsaṃbhūtau vatsaraśvāsitaḥ sutau |
naidhruvo vatsarājjāto raibhyacaiva mahāmatiḥ || 11 ||
sumedhā suṣuve putrānnaivānkuṇḍapāyinaḥ |
asitādekaparṇāyāṃ samabhūddevalo muniḥ || 12 ||
ārādhya devalaḥ śaṃbhuṃ parāṃ siddhimavāptavān |
śāṇḍilyo devalājjāta ete'patyāstu kāśyapāḥ || 13 ||
tṛṇabindustu rājarṣiḥ kanyāmilavilābhidhām |
pulastyāya dadau tasyāṃ viśravāḥ samajāyata |
|| puṣpotkaṭā tathā vākā kaikasī devavarṇinī |
catasraḥ patnayastasya paulastyasya mahātmanaḥ || 15 ||
kubero devavarṇinyāṃ kaikasyāṃ rāvaṇastathā |
kumbhakarṇaḥ śūrpaṇakhā tathaiva ca vibhīṣaṇaḥ || 16 |
puṣpotkaṭāyāmabhavaṃstrayaḥ putrāśca kanyakāḥ |
bhūtā mṛgāḥ piśācāśca sarve vai daṃdriṇastathā || 19||
paulastyā iti te sarve marīceḥ kaśyapaḥ sutaḥ |
bhṛgoḥ sakāśādabhavacchuko daityagururmahān || 20 ||
prāptā saṃjīvinī vidyā yena śukreṇa dhīmatā |
mahādevaṃ samārādhya pūrā badarikāśrame || 21 |
jarāmaraṇanirmukto vajrakāyo mahāmuniḥ |
yogācārya iti khyātaḥ prasādāgirijāpateḥ || 22 ||
anasūyā tu suṣuve kramātputratrayaṃ dvijāḥ |
dattātreyaṃ candramasaṃ tathā durvāsamaṃ munim || 23 ||
ātreyā iti te khyātā nirapatyastathā ṛtuḥ |
vasiṣṭhāya dadau kanyāṃ nārado munipuṃgavāḥ || 24 ||
arundhatīmarundhatyāṃ śaktirnāma babhūva ha |
śakteḥ parāśarastasmātkṛṣṇadvaipāyano muniḥ || 25 ||
dvaipāyanācchuko jajñe pañca putrāḥ śukasya te |
bhūriśravāḥ prabhuḥ śaṃbhuḥ kṛṣṇo gauraśca pañcamaḥ || 26 ||
kanyā kīrtimatī nāma vaṃśā ete prakīrtitāḥ |
kaśyapādaditirlebhe bhāskaraṃ tejasā'dhikam || 27 ||
saṃjñā rājñī prabhā chāyā bhānorbhāryāḥ smṛtāstvimāḥ |
sūte sūryānmanuṃ saṃjñā yasya vaṃśe'bhavannṛpāḥ || 28 |
yamaṃ ca yamunāṃ caiva rājñī revantameva ca |
prabhā prabhātamādityācchāyā sāvarṇineva ca || 29 ||
śaniṃ ca tapatīṃ caiva viṣṭiṃ caitra yathākram |
ikṣvākurna bhagaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireva ca || 30 ||
nariṣyantaśca nābhāgo hyariṣṭaḥ karūṣastathā |
vṛṣadhvajo mahātejā nava vaivasvatāḥ samāḥ || 31 ||
ilā jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca kanyā etāstrayaḥ (!) smṛtāḥ |
ikṣvākośvābhavatputro vikukṣiriti viśrutaḥ || 32 ||
vai
tasya putraśataṃ tvāsītkakutstha jyeṣṭha īritaḥ |
tasmātsuyodhano jajñe pṛthustasya suto'bhavat || 33 ||
viśvakastasya putro'bhūddamakastasya vai sutaḥ |
tasmāccharyātirabhavadyuvanāśvaśca tatsutaḥ || 34 ||
śrāvastistasya putro'bhūcchrāvastī yena nirmitā |
tasmātkuvalayaḥ khyāto dhundhumārastato'bhavat || 35 ||
dhundhumārestrayaḥ putrā dṛḍhāśvādyā mahaujasaḥ |
dṛḍhāśvasya ca dāyādo hariścandrastato'bhavat || 36 ||
rohitastasya putro'bhūdrohitalyāpi tatsutaḥ |
dhumdhustasmādabhūtputro dhundhoḥ putrau babhūvatuḥ || 37 ||
sudevo vijayaścaiva kuruko vijayātsmṛtaḥ |
ko'tha kurukājjajñe tasmādvāhurabhūtsutaḥ || 38 ||
sagarastasya putro'bhūt pautrastasyāṃśumānsmṛtaḥ |
tasya putrī dilīpastu tasmājjajñe bhagīrathaḥ || 39 ||
prīto'bhūttapasā śaṃbhudī varamanuttamam |
gaṅgāṃ babhāra śirasā rakṣārthī jagatāṃ haraḥ || 40 ||
daśāyutānāṃ varṣāṇi dvisahastraṃ śatadvayam |
mahādevādvaraṃ labdhvā rājyaṃ kṛtvā bhagīrathaḥ || 41 ||
virakta rājyabhogebhyo viśvaṃ matvendrajālavat |
jābālaṃ samanuprāpya yattajjñānaṃ śivātmakam || 42 ||
muneranugrahāṃlabdhvā parāṃ siddhiṃ gato nṛpaḥ |
śrutastasyābhavatputro nābhāgastatsuto'bhavat || 43 ||
sindhudvīpa tato jajñe ayutāyustato'bhavat |
ṛtuparṇastu tatputraḥ sudhāmā tatsuto'bhavat || 44 ||
yasmai dattaṃ bhagavatā gāṇapatyamanuttamam |
kalmāṣapādastatputraḥ kṣetrajastatsuto'śmakaḥ || 45 ||
ṛpervasiṣṭhādviprendrānnakulastatsuto'bhavat |
nakulasyābhavatputro nāmnā śataratho nṛpaḥ || 46 ||
abhūdilaghilastasmādvṛddhaśarmā tato'bhavat |
tasmādviśvasaho nāma khaṭṭāstatsuto'bhavat || 47 ||
dīrghabāhustato jajñe raghustasyābhavatsutaḥ |
raghorajastu vikhyāto rājā daśarathastataḥ || 48 ||
tasya putrāśca catvāro dharmajñā lokaviśrutāḥ |
rāmo'tha bharataścaiva tṛtīyo lakṣmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || 49 ||
caturthaścaiva śatrughno rāmo nārāyaṇaḥ svayam |
dharmaḥ satyasaṃkalpo mahādevaparāyaṇaḥ || 50 ||
sītā tasyābhavadbhāryāṃ pārvatyaṃśasamudbhavā |
janakene purā gaurī tapasā toṣitā yataḥ || 51 ||
janakā dadau śaṃbhuḥ prīto dhanuranuttamam |
taddhanurbhañjayāmāsa janakasya gṛhe sthitam || 53 ||
dṛṣṭvā parākramaṃ tasya rāmasya guṇaśālinaḥ |
janakaḥ pradadau tasmai sītāṃ brahmavidāṃ varaḥ || 53 ||
pitrā kṛto'bhiṣekārthaṃ rāmo rājyasya vai yadā |
vārayāmāsa kaikeyī tadā rājñaḥ priyā vadhūḥ || 54 ||
rājaṃstvayā varo dattaḥ pūrvameva yataḥ prabho |
rājānaṃ matsutaṃ tasmādbharataṃ kartumarhasi || 55 ||
iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā rājye tamabhiṣicya saḥ |
preṣayāmāsa taṃ rāmaṃ vanaṃ prati salakṣmaṇam || 56 ||
vanaṃ gatvā nivasato bhāryāṃ dṛṣṭvā'tha rākṣasaḥ |
rāvaṇo nāma paulastyo nītvā laṅkāṃ punaryayau || 57 ||
adṛṣṭvā tāṃ tataḥ sītāṃ duḥkhitau rāmalakṣmaṇau |
sakhyaṃ vānararājena gatvā dāśarathī dvijāḥ || 58 ||
sugrīvasya sakhā vīro hanumānnāma vānaraḥ |
gatvā'tha rāvaṇapurīmapaśyajjanakātmajām || 59 ||
aśrupūrṇekṣaṇāṃ sītāmindīvaranibhānanām |
viśvāsārthaṃ dadau tasyai rāmasyaibāḍulīyakam || 60 ||
dṛṣṭvā'ṅgulīyakaṃ sītā mahṛṣṭā ca tadā'bhavat |
samāśvāsya tataḥ sītāṃ prayayau rāghavāntikam || 61 ||
rāmastamāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā praharṣotphullalocanaḥ |
śrutvā tadvacanādvṛttaṃ yuddhāya kṛtaniśvayaḥ || 62 ||
setuṃ kṛtvā'tha rakṣobhiryuddhaṃ kṛtvā mahāmanāḥ |
nihatya rāvaṇaṃ rāmo bhrātṛbhiḥ saha suvrataḥ || 63 ||
ānayāmāsa tāṃ sītāmaśokavanamadhyagām |
pratiṣṭhāpya mahādevaṃ setumadhye'tha rāghavaḥ || 64 ||
labdhavānparamāṃ bhaktiṃ śive śivaparākramaḥ |
rāmeśvara iti khyāto mahādevaḥ pinākadhṛk || 65 ||
tasya darśanamātreṇa brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati |
abhiṣiktastato rājye rāmo rājīvalocanaḥ || 66 ||
pālayanpṛthivīṃ sarvā dharmeṇa munipuṃgavāḥ |
ayajadevadeveśamaśvamedhena śaṃkaram || 67 ||
tasya prasādātsvapadaṃ prāptavānatha rāghavaḥ |
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ rāmasya caritaṃ mayā || 68 ||
idaṃ vistarato viprāḥ proktaṃ vālmīkinā punaḥ |
kuśako lavaśvānyaḥ putrau rāmasya suvratau || 69 ||
satyasandho mahāvaya mahādevaparāyaṇai |
atithiśca kuśājjajñe niṣadhastatsuto'bhavat || nalastasyābhavatputro nabhastasyābhavatsutaḥ || 70 ||
tatacandrāvalokaca tārāpīḍastato'bhavat |
tataścandragirirnāīma bhānujittatsuto'bhavat || 71 ||
ete sarve nṛpāḥ proktā ikṣvākukulasaṃbhavāḥ |
dharmātmāno mahāsattvāḥ kīrtimanto dṛḍhavratāḥ || 72 ||
imaṃ yaḥ paṭhate nityamivāko śamuttamam |
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sūryaloke mahīyate || 73 ||
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sutaśaunakasaṃvāde prahādarājyārohaṇā- dīkṣvākukulasaṃbhavanṛpamālikāntakathanaṃ nāma triṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 30 ||
sūta uvāca -
ailaḥ purūravāvāsssīdrājā paramadhārmikaḥ |
urvaśyāṃ janayāmāsa paṭ putrānmathitaujasaḥ || 1 ||
jayadhvajastu matimānnārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ || 12 ||
jayadhvajasya dāyādāstālajaṅghā iti smṛtāḥ |
teṣāṃ jyeṣṭho vītihotraḥ sarve te yādavāḥ smṛtāḥ || 13 ||
viśrutastasya dāyādastasya patnī pativratā |
ramamāṇastayā rājā kadācidyamunātaṭe || 14 ||
apaśyadurvaśīṃ tatra vīṇāvādanalālasām |
urvaśīmabravīdrājā smaravāṇena pīḍitaḥ || 15 ||
prāptānujñastato rājā jagāma svapurīṃ prati || 20 ||
dṛṣṭvā pativratāṃ bhāryāmabhavadbhayavihvalaḥ |
ceṣṭitaṃ tasya sā jñātvā mahinā svena bhāminī || 21 ||
mā bhaiṣīriti taṃ prāha bhartāraṃ sā pativratā |
na doṣastava rājendra sarve kāmasya ceṣṭitam || 22 ||
kāmena svargamāpnoti kāmena narakaṃ tataḥ |
vidhinā sevitaḥ kāmaḥ svargadaḥ śvabhramanyathā || 23 ||
tasmāttvayā narapate vidhiṃ hitvā sa sevitaḥ |
tasmātpāpaṃ mahajjātaṃ kuru pāpaviśodhanam || 24 ||
bhāryānigaditaṃ śrutvā yayau kaṇvāśramaṃ prati |
jñātvā tadvacanācchuddhiṃ jagāma himavagirim || 25 |
mārge'paśyatsa gandharva viśvāvasumariṃdamam |
sakāntaṃ krīḍamānaṃ taṃ śobhitaṃ divyamālayā || 26 ||
dṛṣṭvā mālāṃ sa rājendraḥ samārāpsarasaṃ tadā |
urvaśyā eva yogyaiṣā mālā tānyasya kasyacit || 27 ||
evaṃ saṃcintya manasā mālāmāhartumudyataḥ |
tena sārdhaṃ mahadyuddhaṃ gandharveṇa nṛpottamaḥ || 28 ||
kṛtvā gṛhītvā tāṃ mālāṃ jagāmāpsarasaṃ prati |
anviṣyamāṇaḥ sakalāṃ babhrāma sa vasuṃdharām || 29 ||
viraśceḥ kāryamuddiśya gatvā punarihāgataḥ || 36 ||
gamiṣyāmi punastatra yatrāste satyalokapaḥ |
iti śrutvā munervākyaṃ rājā'nujñāpya nāradam || 37 ||
taṃ pradeśa gatastūrṇa tatrāpaśyatsa corvaśīm |
mālāṃ nivedayāmāsa sā tayā'laṃkṛtā'bhavat || 38 ||
ramamāṇastayā sārdhaṃ gataṃ varṣaśataṃ punaḥ |
kadācittamapṛcchatsā rājānaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ || 39 ||
svakīyaṃ nagaraṃ gatvā bhavatā tatra kiṃ kṛtam |
brūhi rājanmahābāho yadyasmi tava vallabhā || 40 ||
iti pṛṣṭastayā rājā provāca tadaśeṣataḥ |
tasyeritamathāsssyaṃ rājānaṃ pratyabhāṣata || 41 ||
ita urdhvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ sthātavyaṃ naiva suvrata |
śāpaṃ dāsyati te kaṇvo bhāryā tava mamānagha || 42 ||
tayā cokto'pi tanvaṅgayā na tatyāja ha urvaśīm |
jñātvā'tha tasya nirvandhamakarodātmanastanum || 43 ||
tvayā'haṃ rantumicchāmi tvaṃ māṃ rantumihārhasi |
sā nṛpasya vacaḥ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā taṃ madanopamam || 16 |
krīḍamānā tadā tena cirakālaṃ sahorvaśī |
rāte varṣasahastre tu viraktaḥ kāmabhogataḥ || 17 ||
āhorvaśīṃ gamiṣyāmi svapurīmiti viśrutaḥ |
bhogenaitāvatā nālamavocaditi sā punaḥ || 18 ||
na gantavyaṃ tvayā rājansthātavyaṃ prītaye mama |
abravīttāṃ tato rājā purīṃ gatvā yaśasvinīm || 19 ||
āgamiṣyāmyahaṃ kṣiprama parisaraṃ tava |
prāptānujñastato rājā jagāma svapurīṃ prati || 20 ||
dṛṣṭvā pativratāṃ bhāryāmabhavadbhayavihvalaḥ |
ceṣṭitaṃ tasya sā jñātvā mahinā svena bhāminī || 21 ||
mā bhaiṣīriti taṃ prāha bhartāraṃ sā pativratā |
na doṣastava rājendra sarve kāmasya ceṣṭitam || 22||
kāmena svargamāpnoti kāmena narakaṃ tataḥ |
vidhinā sevitaḥ kāmaḥ svargadaḥ śvabhramanyathā || 23 ||
tasmāttvayā narapate vidhiṃ hitvā sa sevitaḥ |
tasmātpāpaṃ mahajjātaṃ kuru pāpaviśodhanam || 24 ||
bhāryānigaditaṃ śrutvā yayau kaṇvāśramaṃ prati |
jñātvā tadvacanācchuddhiṃ jagāma himavagirim || 25 ||
mārge'paśyatsa gandharva viśvāvasumariṃdemam |
sakāntaṃ krīḍamānaṃ taṃ śobhitaṃ divyamālayā || 26 ||
dṛṣṭvā mālāṃ sa rājendraḥ samārāpsarasaṃ tadā |
urvaśyā eva yogyaiṣā mālā nānyasya kasyacit || 27 ||
evaṃ saṃcintya manasā mālāmāhartumudyataḥ |
tena sārdhaṃ mahadyuddhaṃ gandharveṇa nṛpottamaḥ || 28 ||
kṛtvā gṛhītvā tāṃ mālāṃ jagāmāpsarasaṃ prati |
anviṣyamāṇaḥ sakalāṃ vabhrāma sa vasuṃdharām || 29 ||

mālāṃ nivedayāmāsa sā tayā'laṃkṛtā'bhavat || 38 ||
ramamāṇaratayā sārdhaṃ gataṃ varṣaśataṃ punaḥ |
kadācittamapṛcchatsā rājānaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ || 39 ||
svakīyaṃ nagaraṃ gatvā bhavatā tatra kiṃ kṛtam |
brūhi rājanmahābāho yasmi tava vallabhā || 40 ||
iti pṛṣṭastayā rājā provāca tadaśeṣataḥ |
tasyeritamathāsskarṇya rājānaṃ pratyabhāṣata || 41 ||
ita ūrdhvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ sthātavyaṃ naiva suvrata |
śāpaṃ dāsyati te kaṇvo bhāryā tatra mamānagha || 42 ||
tayā cokto'pi tanvaṅgayā na tatyāja ha urvaśīm |
jñātvā'tha tasya nirvandhamakarodātmanastanum || 43 ||
balibhiḥ palitākīrṇāṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā rājasattamaḥ |
tatkṣaṇādurvaśīṃ tyaktvā tapase kṛtaniścayaḥ || 44 ||
dvādaśāhānyabhūdrājā kandamūlaphalāśanaḥ |
tāvatkālaṃ ca vāyvāśī tataḥ kaṇvāśramaṃ yayau || 45 ||
dṛṣṭvā munivaraṃ śāntaṃ śivadhyānaikatatparam |
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhaktyā māñjaliḥ pārśvasaṃsthitaḥ || 46 ||
yadvṛttamātmanaḥ sarve muneḥ sarvaṃ nyavedayat |
munirviditvā tatpāpamabravītpāpaśodhanam || 47 ||
muninā preṣito rājā gatvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm |
snātvā saṃtarpya jāhnavyāṃ dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaraṃ śivam || 48 ||
mukto'sāvenaso rājā jagāma svapurīṃ tadā |
vasūni brāhmaṇebhyaśva dattvā rājyamapālayat || 49 ||
urvaśyāṃ viśrutājjātāḥ sapta putrā mahaujasaḥ |
kroṣṭoryadu॑sutasyā''sanvaṃśyāḥ satkīrtiśālinaḥ || 50 ||
śṛṇudhvaṃ tānmuniśreṣṭhā mukhyāneva na cāparān |
koṣṭovaṃśe ṛthaḥ khyāto vidarbhaḥ kośalastathā || 51 ||
sāttvataśca tataḥ khyāto mahābhojastataḥ paraḥ |
bhojaśca satyavākcaiva satyakaḥ sātyakistataḥ || 52 ||
krathakaśca suṣeṇaśca subhojo naravāhanaḥ |
āhūko devakacaiva śrīdevo devasutrataḥ || 53 ||
ugrasenaśca kaṃsaśca vasudevo mahāyaśāḥ |
ugrasenasya kanyāyāṃ devakyāṃ vasudevataḥ || 54 ||
bhṛgoḥ śāpavaśādviṣṇuḥ saṃbhūtastridaśeśvaraḥ |
rohiṇī nāma yā patnī vasudevasya śobhanā |
. || tasyāṃ saṃkarṣaṇo jāto yo'nantaḥ śeṣasaṃjñitaḥ |
poḍaśastrīsahasrāṇi patnayo mādhavasya yāḥ || 56 ||
tāsu jātā hyasaṃkhyātāḥ pradyumnapramukhāḥ sutāḥ |
kṛṣṇo'pi devakīsūnuḥ paramātmā sanātanaḥ || 57 ||
kṛtakṛtyo'pi yogātmā māyāvī viśvabhuksvayam |
na kṛṣṇādadhikastasmādasti māheśvarāgraṇīḥ || 60 ||
tasmāttatpūjanācchaṃbhurbhavatyeva supūjitaḥ |
hareravajñākaraṇādbhavedīśaḥ parāṅmukhaḥ || 61 ||
tasmātpūjyaḥ sadā śāṅgī mahādevaparāyaṇaiḥ |
tadbhaktaiśca viśeṣeṇa prītaye girijāpateḥ || 62 ||

|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde puruyaduvaṃśa - kathamaṃ nāmaikatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 31 ||

yasmiñśarīramevā''tmā nāsti pāratrikī gatiḥ || 43 ||

aṇoralpataraṃ prāhurmahato'pi mahattaram || 59 ||

sūta uvāca -
atha nandīśvaraḥ prāha brahmādīnparayā mudā |
