ṛṣaya ūcuḥ –
kathaṃ jālaṃdharo daityo nihataḥ śūlapāṇinā |
sudarśanena cakreṇa vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam || 1 ||
sūta uvāca -
āsītkṛtāntasaṃkāśī jālaṃdhara iti smṛtaḥ |
jalamaṇḍalasaṃbhūtastena devā vinirjitāḥ || 2 ||
lokapālāśca sādhyāśca vasavaśca marudgaṇāḥ |
viśvedevāstathā''dityā rudrāścaiva vinirjitāḥ || 3 ||
brahmāṇaṃ ca suraśreṣṭhaṃ samare munipuṃgavāḥ |
jagāma jetuṃ deveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ daityanivarhaṇam || 4 ||
tena sārdhamabhūdyuddhaṃ jālaṃdharasureśayoḥ |
vinirjitya tato viṣṇuṃ daityānmatīdamabravīt || 5 ||
devā vinirjitāḥ sarve varjayitvā trilocanam |
tamadya jetumicchāmi bhagavantaṃ maheśvaram || 6 ||
nandīśvareṇa sahitaṃ sāmyaṃ caiva raṇāṅgaṇe |
jālaṃdharavacaḥ śrutvā daiteyāra te dvijottamāḥ || 7 ||
yayurdevaṃ tamīśānaṃ yoddhumudyuktamānasāḥ |
tato jālaṃdharī daityo daityaiśva sahito balī || 8 ||
rathairnāgaiśca saṃnaddhaḥ prayayau śaṃkarāntikam |
dṛṣṭvā jālaṃdharaṃ śaṃbhurañjanādriyopamam || 9 ||
prahasannabravīddaityaṃ brahmaṇo varadarpitam |
yuddhenālaṃ diteḥ putra madbāṇairniśitairiha || 10 ||
kṣaṇādvicchinnasarvāṅgī mṛtyorgrāsaṃ gamiṣyasi |
śrutvā jālaṃdharo vākyaṃ devadevasya śūlinaḥ || 11 ||
kupita: māha deveśaṃ bhagavantaṃ trilocanam |
anena vāklāpena kiṃ maheśa vṛthā tava || 12 ||
gadayā tāḍayāmi tvāmanayā tīkṣṇadhārayā |
jālaṃdhara uvācaṃ- rekhāmātraṃ kimuddhartu kimidaṃ bhāṣase śiva ||17||
mervādayo'pi tiṣṭhanti kiṃ mayā na vicālitāḥ |
yā tvayā likhitā rekhā cakrarūpā maheśvara || 18 ||
tāmuddhṛtya tato hanmi tvāṃ nandipramukhaiḥ saha |
bālatve nirjito brahmā tarasaiva purā mayā || 19 ||
nikṣipto bhagavānviṣṇulīlayā śatayojanam |
indrādyā lokapālāca baddhāḥ kārāgṛhe sthitāḥ || 20 ||
dāsībhūtāḥ striyasteṣāṃ vartante mahe śiva |
dorbhyāṃ viyannadī ruddhā krīḍārtha himavadbhirau || 21 ||
diggajāśca vinikṣiptāḥ sindhau vai rāvaṇādayaḥ |
vaḍavāmukhe ruddhe caikārṇava ivābhavat || 22 ||
tasmānna jānāsi kathaṃ śaṃbho mama parākramam |
tvāmapi prāpayāmyadya jitvā kārāgṛhaṃ prati || 23 ||
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā dānavasya maheśvaraḥ |
netrāgnilavabhāgena camūṃ tasyādahatkṣaṇāt || 24 ||
akṣauhiṇīnāṃ sāhasraṃ līlayaiva maheśvaraḥ |
kṛtvā tadbhasmasādvimā jālaṃdharamathābravīt || 25 ||
īśvara uvāca -
samayo yaḥ kṛtaḥ pūrva lekhāmuddharaṇaṃ prati |
kuru daitya tathā śīghraṃ tato māṃ jetumarhasi || 26 ||
atha śaṃbhorvacaḥ śrutvā madāndho daityapuṃgavaḥ |
dorbhyāmāsphovya vegena lekhāmuddhartumudyataḥ || 27 ||
sudarśanākhyaṃ yaccakraṃ kṛcchreṇa mahatā dvijāḥ |
śrāvayedvā dvijānbhaktyā brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati || 33 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde jālaṃdhara- arari nāma saptatriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 37 ||
sūta uvāca -
caturṣvapi ca vedeṣu purāṇeṣu ca sarvaśaḥ |
śrīmaheśātparo devo na samāno'sti kaścana || 1 ||
brahmā viṣṇurvārātiḥ sarve yasya vaśe sthitāḥ |
utpattiḥ sarvadevānāṃ sa eva dhyeya ucyate || 2 ||
nāsti śaṃbho: paro dharmo nāstyarthaḥ śaṃkarātparaḥ |
śivādanyatsukhaṃ nāsti mokṣo naiva harātparaḥ || 3 ||
yadā carmavadākāśaṃ veṣṭayiṣyanti mānavāḥ |
tadā śivamavijñāya duḥkhasyānto bhaviṣyati || 4 ||
sraṣṭṛtvaṃ brahmaṇo yena dhyeyatvaṃ yena śārṅgiṇaḥ |
viṣṇutvaṃ yena śakrasya tasmādanyaḥ paro na hi || 5 ||
ṛṣaya ūcu: - kecillokā maheśānaṃ tyaktvā keśavakiṃkarāḥ |
tatra kiṃ kāraṇaṃ sūta vada saṃśayanāśaka || 6 ||
antakāle smarantyeva prāyeṇa garuḍadhvajam |
vidyamāne śive viṣṇoḥ prabhau śrīpārvatīpatau || 7 ||
caturṣvapi ca vedeṣvityādi śivanindaka kāraṇamityantamadhyā yatrayaṃ
na dṛśyate |
khasaṃjñitapustake saptatriṃśādhyāyasamāptisthale kiṃcidvahirlikhitamasti |
tadyathā - pūrvatrā dhyāyasamāptisthalavyatyāsaṃ kṛtvā'tyamadhyāyavayaṃ madhvācāryakathāparaṃ vaiṣṇavairapalapitamasti tatpusta- kāntareṣu draṣṭavyam-iti |
viṣṇoḥ smaraṇamātreṇa sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet |
śaṃbhuprasāda evaipa nāsti kāryā vicāraṇā || yaḥ śaṃbhuṃ tattvato vetti sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ svayam |
yastu nārāyaṇaṃ vetti sa śakro vibudheśvaraḥ || 12 ||
ya indraṃ vetti deveśaṃ lokapālo jalādhipaḥ |
evaṃ sarvalokapālāñjānāti sa ihāmaraḥ || 13 ||
devāñjānāti yaṣṭavyāsa ṛṣirvedavitsvayam |
ṛṣīnyo vetti samyaktvātsa eva brāhmaṇottamaḥ || 14 ||
sarvadevamayaṃ vipraṃ yo jānāti sa vedavit |
rahasyaṃ vetti vedasya sa eva haravallabhaḥ || 15 ||
janmādikāraṇaṃ śaṃbhuṃ viṣṇuṃ brahmādipūrvajam |
na jānanti mahāmūrkhā viṣṇumāyāvimohitāḥ || 16 ||
āsītpratardano nāma rājā paramadhārmikaḥ |
saptadvīpapatiḥ pṛthvīprabhurekaḥ pratāpavān |
|| śūraḥ puṇyamatirbhogī dātā vedārthapālakaḥ |
rakṣitā sarvasetūnāṃ brahmaṇyo brāhmaṇapriyaḥ || 18 ||
tasya rājye sadā devā gṛhṇanti haviruttamam |
na pāpaṇḍī na vā bauddhastasya rājye'bhavajjanaḥ || 19 ||
kadācitsa purīṃ tyaktvā krīḍārthaṃ nirgato bahiḥ |
tadā dadarśa kṣapaṇaṃ rājā vismayamāgataḥ || 20 ||
pṛṣṭaḥ kastvaṃ kuto yātaḥ kiṃ kāryaṃ ca tavepsitam |
kutra yāsyasi tatsarvaṃ kiṃjātīyo bhavānvada || 21 ||
kṣapaṇaka uvāca -
rājanvaṇigahaṃ śānto yatiḥ śīlavate sthitaḥ |
madīyāñcalasaṃlagnāḥ santyatra vaṇijaḥ pare || 22 ||
rājovāca -
ko dharmaḥ kiṃ nu tatra tvaṃ jñāyate kena vakti kaḥ |
kṣapaṇaka uvāca -
ahiṃsā paramo dharmastattattvaṃ yattanordamaḥ |
budhyate bauddhajainābhyāṃ vaktā tasya jino mataḥ || 24 ||
vedavedāṅgavettāro yājñikā vaiṣṇavā dvijāḥ |
māheśvarā mahāpūjyā na vyakto'haṃ bhayānnṛpa || 25 ||
sūta uvāca -
tato rājā parāṃ cintāṃ prāpto duḥkhitamānasaḥ |
dhigrājyaṃ mama durbuddhervedavāhyo'sti matpure || 26 |
evaṃ hanmi yadā pāpaṃ tadetanmāninī prajā |
kathayiṣyati śāntātmā hato rājñā kubuddhinā || 27 ||
etasminnihate kiṃ syādbhavanti bahavastathā |
dayāśabdaṃ puraskṛtya dharmo vicariṣyati || 28 ||
vedabāhyāḥ prajā rājñā śāsituṃ naiva śakyate |
tadā tatpāpabhāgī syādityāha bhagavānmanuḥ || 29 ||
sūta uvāca -
tyaktvā rājyaṃ tapastepe tato rājā pratardanaḥ |
sāvitrīṃ manasā dhyātvā nityamekāgramānasaḥ || 30 ||
tataḥ katipayāhobhirbrahmā pratyakṣatāṃ gataḥ |
mahatā tapasā tuṣṭa idaṃ vacanamabravīt || 31 ||
brahmovāca -
putra prāpto'smi saṃtoṣaṃ varaṃ varaya suvrata |
kathaṃ tvaṃ khidyase citte rājyaṃ tyaktaṃ kutastvayā || 32 ||
rājovāca -
vedāḥ pramāṇaṃ vaktayeva jānātyeva ca yatmajā |
śaṅkāmātraṃ bhavennaiva vedaprāmāṇyagocaram || 33 ||
iti yāce varaṃ deva kimanyena vareṇa me |
yāce niṣkaṇṭakaṃ rājyaṃ saptadvīpāvanīpatiḥ || 34 ||
sūta uvāca -
evamastviti saṃmocya brahmā'ntardhānamāyayau |
pratardano'pi rājarṣiḥ saṃtuṣṭaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ || 35 ||
tataḥ prabhṛti tadrājye sarvo dharmo vyavasthitaḥ |
vedavedāṅgavettāro brāhmaṇāḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ || 36 ||
agnihotrāṇi yajñāśca yatyo brahmacāriṇaḥ |
śaivā nānāvidhāḥ puṇyā vaiṣṇavāḥ śubhalakṣaṇāḥ || 37 ||
tasya rājye mahāpuṇye na pāpaṇḍī nai haitukī |
varṇāśramācāravatāṃ kriyāḥ sarvāstadā'bhavan || 38 ||
utsavā viṣṇubhaktānāṃ śivapūjā gṛhe gṛhe |
sarve devānmānayanti na kaṃcidveṣṭi mānavaḥ || 39 ||
tarkavedāntamīmāṃsāvyākhyānāni gṛhe gṛhe |
vedanirghoṣavadrājyaṃ yajñastambhāḥ sthale sthale || 40 ||
anekabhogasaṃyuktā hṛṣṭāḥ puṣṭāḥ striyaḥ satīḥ |
rakṣanti patayaḥ puṇyā yathā vṛddhapuraskṛtāḥ || 41 ||
sūta uvāca -
evaṃ bahutithe kāle. gate ye daityadānavāḥ |
pāpiṣṭhā hīnakarmāṇo mlecchāste'pi divaṃ gatāḥ || 42 ||
yeṣāṃ tu saṃtatiḥ śuddhaṃ vedamārga hi manyate |
te sarve narakānmuktvā prāptā evāmarāvatīm || 43 ||
sarvatra tulasīvṛndaṃ sarvatra haripūjanam |
vilvadalaistu sarvatra pūjyate girijāpatiḥ || 44 ||
kathaṃ tepāṃ tu pitaro narake nivasanti hi |
tasminrājye samāgatya kiṃ kuryuryamakiṃkarāḥ || 45 ||
sūta uvāca -
śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve yadāsītparamādbhutam |
svargagāmiṣu sarveṣu vyāpārarahite yame || 46 ||
pūjitāḥ sarvalokeṣu sarve devā vasūvire |
tadā'sau dharmarāgatvā śakralokaṃ mahāmanāḥ || 47 ||
uvāca sarvadevānāṃ purataḥ prāñjaliḥ sthitaḥ |
yama uvāca -
caturaśītilakṣāṇāṃ jīvānāṃ yā sthitiḥ sadā || 48 |
tāṃ naṣṭāmadhunā vedmi yadi devaḥ pramāṇavān |
yasyāṃ kīṭādiyonau yaḥ sthito jīvo'tipāpavān || 49 ||
narake saṃyaminyāṃ vā tatputreṇa sa uddhṛtaḥ |
śrāddhadevārcanādīni karoti śrutiniśvayaḥ || 50 ||
indra uvāca -
asmākaṃ hīnajīvānāṃ ko viśeṣo yadā śrutiḥ |
pramāṇayati tattvena vayaṃ devā yadājñayā || 51 ||
purohita tava prajñā śobhanā pratibhāti me |
pūrva cārvākavauddhādimārgāḥ saṃdarśitāstvayā || 52 ||
tena mārgeṇa vibhrāntā vedamārgabahiṣkṛtāḥ |
daityāśca dānavācaiva tathā kuru dvijottama || 53 ||
kathaṃ sā cālyate tāta na śakyaṃ hi śubhā'dhunā || 55 ||
vidhidattavarasyāhamucchettuṃ śaktimānkatham |
indrādaya ūcuḥ–
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca durdarśānāṃ bhavo yadā || 56 ||
tadā śukraḥ svayaṃ teṣāṃ kṛpayā sodyamo bhavet |
tasmāsvaṃ vipraśārdūla kasmādasmānupekṣase || 57 ||
asādhyaṃ tava kiṃ mānya vayaṃ tvaccharaṇaṃ gatāḥ |
asmākaṃ durjanāḥ sarve vedakarmaratāḥ kṛtāḥ || 58 ||
teṣāṃ vyāmohanāya tvaṃ kuru yatnaṃ kṛpānidhe |
devānāṃ rakṣasāṃ caiva daityānāṃ pāpakarmaṇām || 59 ||
sūta uvāca -
evaṃ bruvatsu deveṣu vṛhaspatirudāradhīḥ |
upāyaṃ cintayāmāsa sṛṣṭeḥ saṃrakṣaṇāye ca || 60 ||
gururuvāca –
gṛṇvantu tridaśāḥ sarve mamopāyaṃ vadāmyaham |
devaḥ kaścidyadi bhavetkapaṭī vaiṣṇavaḥ svayam || 61 ||
śaṅkhacakrāṅkitatanustulasīkāṣṭhabhūṣitaḥ |
ūrdhvapuṇḍraṃ ca vibhrāṇo harināmākṣaraṃ japan || 62 ||
devatāmātranindī ca akṛtvā matimīśvare |
śivadveṣṭā mahāpāpaprerakaḥ śivanindakaḥ || 63 ||
dambhena yadi tadrājye śivanindā kṛtā bhavet |
tadā tatpūrvajāḥ sarve narakaṃ yānti dāruṇam || 64 ||
tato deveṣu sarveṣu na kaścidavadattathā |
kathayanti sma cānyonyaṃ naitatkarmāsti sundaram || 65 ||
kaścāṇḍālaḥ śivaṃ brūyātsādhāraṇyena viṣṇunā |
yasya prasādādvaikuṇṭhaḥ prāptavānīdṛśaṃ padam || 66 ||
sūta uvāca -
tataḥ kiṃnaramāhūya provācedaṃ śacīpatiḥ |
yāhi kiṃnara māyāvī bhūtvā tvaṃ vaiṣṇavo bhuvam || 67 ||
paraṃ tveko mahāviṣṇuḥ śivastasya ca kiṃkaraḥ || 70 ||
sūta uvāca -
prerito'sau balāttena bhīto'gacchacchanaiḥ śanaiḥ |
dāmbhikaṃ rūpamāsthāya yathā sādhuṃ vadejjanaḥ || 71 ||
sarvavaiṣṇavacihnāni dhṛtvā bhrābhyati tatpure |
śiṣyānkaroti tānpūrve vadenmānyo na śaṃkaraḥ || 72 ||
kacidati na dhyeyo na mukhya iti ca kvacit |
kacidutkṛṣṭajīvo'yaṃ kacicchrīviṣṇukiṃkaraḥ || 73 ||
iti nānāvidhā buddhirnarāṇāṃ bheditā yadā |
tadā śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto rājagehaṃ viśatyapi || 74 ||
cālito rājaloko'pi viruddhaṃ naiva dṛśyate |
viṣṇubhakto mahāśānto vedavedāṅgapāravān || 75 ||
upāyanānyanekāni hayāṃśca syandanānvasu |
lokāḥ sarve dadatyeva guptaṃ pāpaṃ na dṛśyate || 76 ||
sūta uvāca -
ekasminsamaye vimā ekādaśyāmupoṣitāḥ |
janāḥ prātaścakrapāṇiṃ jamatkartuṃ gatāḥ śubhāḥ || 77 ||
tatropaviṣṭaḥ śiṣyaiḥ strairvvataḥ svīyena tejasā |
na kaṃcinmanyate vipraṃ yo bhasmāṅkitabhālavān || 78 ||
etasminnantare rājā prāptavān śrīpratardanaḥ |
to bahuvidhairvibhaiḥ kuśahastaiḥ śucitrataiḥ || 79 ||
riṇaḥ kecidūrdhvapuṇḍradharāstathā |
==
paṭhantaḥ śivasūktāni viṣṇumuktāni cāpare || 80 ||
etairvahuvidhairviprairvṛto rājopaviśya saḥ |
uvāca vacanaṃ yuktaṃ komalākṣarasaṃyutam || 81 ||
svāminnāgatavānsākṣādbhagavānharipārṣadaḥ |
kaṭhoraṃ vākyametatte bhāti cetasi me'śaniḥ || 92 ||
vaiṣṇavābhāsa uvāca -
naikāgramanasaste tu ye'rcayantīha dhūrjaṭim |
śmaśānavāsī digvāsā brahmamastakagbhavaḥ || 93||
sarpahāraḥ kathaṃ sevyo viṣadhārī jaṭādharaḥ |
tasmādviṣṇuḥ sadā sevyaḥ sundaraḥ kamalāpatiḥ || 94 ||
rājovāca -
nānārūpāṇi rudrasya ke jānanti narādhamāḥ |
tvaṃ vaiṣṇava ivāssbhāsi vedārthe naiva vetsi re || 95 ||
sūta uvāca -
cintayitvā tato rājā viduṣo brāhmaṇottamān |
āhūya nirṇayaṃ cāsya kariṣyāmīti tattvataḥ || 96 ||1820||
iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde śivamahimādi- kathanaṃ nāmāṣṭātriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 38 ||
trailokyanātha kimidaṃ tvayi dṛśyate'dya |
ākāramātrarahitaḥ puruṣaḥ purāṇa-
stvayyeva viśvamiha rajjubhujaṃgamātram || 12 ||
śailāḥ patanti jaladhirmarutāmupaiti
kṛtvā'pi pūjyatamamūrtimmiṃ girīśaṃ
no manyate tadiha vajrasamaṃ mamaitra || 14 ||
lakṣmīruvāca -
sarvātmā sarvavitkartā vaktā dhartā'vyayaḥ prabhuḥ |
tvaṃ sākṣī sarvalokānāṃ tvattaḥ parataro'rita kaḥ || 15 ||
śrīnārāyaṇa uvāca -
asti sarva varārohe mayi tattathyameva hi |
śrīmaheśava rālabdhaṃ madīyaṃ na hi kiṃcana |
|| ekaḥ sṛjati bhūtāni matsamāni kiyantyapi |
tattattvaṃ vedamyahaṃ devi madīyāḥ kecanāpare || 17 ||
vedavedāṅgavettṛṇāṃ sahasrāṇyagrajanmanām |
hananānmucyate jīvo na tu śrīśivalanāt || 18 ||
gurvaṅganāgamana kṛtsadā madyaniṣevakaḥ |
brāhmaṇasvarṇahārī ca kadācinmucyate janaḥ || 19 ||
strīghno goghno nṛpaghnaśca tathā viśvāsaghātakaḥ |
kṛtaghno nāstiko lubdhaḥ kadācinmucyate janaḥ || 20 ||
na tu śrīrudrasāmānyadarśī mucyeta bandhanāt |
virañciviṣṇuśebhyaḥ sarvotkṛṣṭaṃ na jāyate || 21 ||
viṣṇunā yadi vā tulyaṃ mucyante naiva jantavaḥ |
svāmī madīyaḥ śrīkaṇṭharatasya dāso'smi sarvadā || 22 ||
lakṣmīruvāca_gacchāmastatra vaikuṇṭha yatra svāmyasti te vibho |
kailāsaparvate ramye praṇamāmaḥ sadāśivam || 23 ||
sūta uvāca -
tatastai garuḍārūḍhau gatvā kailāsaparvatam |
nānāvidhaiḥ stotrapadaiḥ saṃtuṣṭaṃ cakratuḥ kṣaṇāt || 24 ||
tato brahmādayo devāḥ siddhāstatrā''gatā girau |
rudraḥ kautūhalaprepsuḥ sarvaistaiḥ parivāritaḥ || 25 ||
bhavānīsahitastatra gato yatra pratardanaḥ |
sarvadevavimānānāṃ madhye tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ || 26 ||
śrīmaheśa uvāca_kathayantu kathaṃ yete militāḥ sarvanirjarāḥ |
kiṃ kāryaṃ kimapūrva vā rājā cintāturaḥ katham || 27 ||
devā ūcuḥ -
svāminpratardana rājā vidhilabdhavaro'bhavat |
vedamārgapravaktā ca svayaṃ tasya pravartakaḥ || 28 ||
sṛṣṭirakṣārthamasmābhiḥ kapaṭaṃ kṛtamīśvara |
sarvadhātuśca bhavato helanaṃ kāritaṃ suraiḥ || 29 ||
tatkṣamasva mahādeva kiṃnaro'yaṃ pravartitaḥ |
kalpito vaiṣṇavo'smābhistava nindāparāyaṇaḥ || 30 ||
sūta uvāca -
- etasminneva kāle tu rājā vṛttāntameyivān |
---
tīvraṃ khaḍgaṃ samādāya hatavānkiṃnaraṃ kudhā || 31 ||
tatpakṣapātino ye ca teṣāṃ śīrṣāṇi kaṃdharāt |
pṛthakkṛtāni paśvādyā hatā aśvā anekaśaḥ || 32 ||
na taṃ vārayate kaścidrājānaṃ puṇyacetasam |
mahādevena śamitaḥ krodhastasya mahātmanaḥ || 33 ||
tataḥ kolāhale śānte nandī kautukapūrvakam |
yuyoja hayaśīrṣe taccharīrāṇi pṛthakpṛthak || 34 ||
śīrṣāṇi hayagātraiśca samyaksaṃyojya buddhimān |
uvāca vacanaṃ tathyaṃ devasaṃsadi śuddhagīḥ || 35 ||
yena vaktreṇa giriśo helitaratanmukhaṃ hayaḥ |
mudrādhāraṇagarveṇa helitastattanurhaḥ || 36 ||
brahmovāca taṃ tadadhunā tathyaṃ rājapa rājyakartari |
bhaviṣyaṃ kathayiṣyāmi tacchṛṇudhvaṃ samāhitāḥ || 37 ||
ghore kaliyuge prāpte mlecchairvyāptei bhuvastale |
sarvācāraparibhraṣṭā bhaviṣyanti narādhamāḥ || 38 ||
tadā''ndhradeśamadhye tu dākṣiṇātyo bhaviṣyati |
brāhmaṇo durbhagaḥ kaścidvidhavā brāhmaṇīrataḥ || 39 ||
tasya pāpiṣṭhaviprasya vyabhicārātsuto'naghaḥ |
bhaviṣyati guṇānveṣī daivādadhyayanotsukaḥ || 40 ||
padmapādukamācārya varaṃ vedāntavādinam |
advaitāgamavoddhāraṃ praṇamya prārthayiṣyati || 41 ||
ko vidhiḥ kutra vā dattā tathyaṃ śīghraṃ vadānyathā || 48 ||
bhasmasāttvāṃ kariṣyāmi hīnaṃ brāhmaṇavarcasā |
ityevaṃ kathite sarva kathayiṣyati tattvataḥ || 49||
śāpaṃ dāsyatyathā''cāryaḥ siddhānto mā sphuratvalam |
siddhānte jaḍatā te'stu paramadvaitadarśane || 50 ||
kathaṃ tvadīyā sevā me niṣphalā syādvada prabho |
ityādi vahunirvedaṃ yadā tveṣa kariṣyati || 51 ||
paścāddvadiṣyati svāmī pūrvapakṣo'stu te dṛḍhaḥ |
siddhānte sarvathaivā''ndhyaṃ mama vākyaṃ na cānyathā || 52 ||
madhunā tena śāstrāṇāṃ pūrvapakṣo vilokitaḥ |
bhaviṣyati ca vedāntamanyathā kartumudyataḥ || 53 ||
yathā yathā kaledevāḥ pracāraḥ saṃbhaviṣyati |
tathā tathā'yamunmārgaḥ śivadveṣṭarbhaviṣyati || 54 ||
pūrvaṃ tu drāviḍā deśātkarṇāṭaka tilaṅgayoḥ |
śanairgodāvarītīre prasṛto'yaṃ bhaviṣyati || 55 ||
pūrṇe kaliyuge prāpta āryāvarte caliṣyati |
māyāvādamasacchāstraṃ vadiṣyanti narādhamāḥ || 56 ||
teṣāṃ darśanamātreṇa sacaila snānamācaret |
bhadrātvaṃ ca yathā viṣṭe rāhoḥ svarbhānutā yathā || 57 ||
haritvaṃ ca yathā'neke tathaite tattvavādinaḥ |
yoganindāparā nityamagrihotrasya nindakaḥ || 58 ||
vedāntasamamityāhuḥ purāṇāni ca ye narāḥ |
kevalaṃ vepamātreṇa narā narakagāmiṇaḥ || 59||
saṃbhāṣaṇe kṛte yeṣāṃ pateca brahmavarcasaḥ |
varaṃ bauddhastathā jainaḥ kāpālika mato'pi vā || 60 ||
vyaktaṃ vadati vedānāmaprāmāṇyaṃ tu taiḥ kimu |
vedaprāmāṇyavatkṛtvā'bhimānī na ca vaidikaḥ || 61 ||
īśvaraṃ vacanādvakti paraṃ cānīśvaraḥ khalaḥ |
sūta uvāca -
evaṃ jāte tataḥ sarve yathāgatamito gatāḥ |
pratardano'pi rājarṣiḥ kṛtvā rājyamakaṇṭakam || 62 ||
dehānte muktimāpannaḥ parāmadvaitalakṣaṇām |
tataḥ paraṃ bhaviṣyanti tasya śiṣyā anekaśaḥ || 63 ||
saṃnyāsiveṣamātreṇa kurvāṇā jīvikāṃ nijām |
rājasevāṃ prakurvāṇāḥ pracchannāḥ kaulikā api || 64 ||
agamyāgamane saktā abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe |
apeyaniratāḥ kecinnānābhogasamākulāḥ || 65 ||
yānārūḍhāḥ sadā rājasevāyāṃ tatparā api |
advaitanindāniratāḥ pracchannagranthagauravāḥ || 66 ||
anyadarśana siddhāntaṃ naiva jānanti tattvataḥ |
tatra doṣasya buddhayā vai paṭhiṣyanti kalau yuge || 67 ||
anyadaivatanāmāni yadi heyāni tatkatham |
vedaṃ paṭhanti pāpiṣṭhāḥ kathaṃ tarka vadanti hi || 68 ||
mīmāṃsāśāstrasadgranthānālokya ca punaḥ punaḥ |
pūrvapakṣaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ grahīṣyanti samatsarāḥ || 69 |
svakīyaṃ na vadiṣyanti yato nāsti pramākaram |
iṃsānparamahaṃsāṃ nindiṣyanti ca jārajāḥ || 70 ||
jātamātraṃ naraṃ kaṃcinmuṇḍayitvā maṭhādhipam |
kāṣāyavastramātreṇa kariṣyanti narādhamāḥ || 71 ||
māṭhāpatyaṃ ca sevā ca dhanasaṃgraha eva ca |
dāsīgamanamīrṣyā ca pañcadhā tattvavādinaḥ || 72 ||
saṃsāravattvamityeva paraṃ te tattvavādinaḥ |
māyāvilasitaṃ viśvamiti māyaikavādinaḥ || 73 ||
śuddhaṃ tattvaṃ na jānanti viśvaṃ tattvaṃ vadanti ca |
śabdamātreṇa te jātāḥ kalau hā tattvavādinaḥ || 74 ||
bhaviṣyati yadā viprāḥ pāpānāṃ mabhavaḥ kalau |
tathā tathā bhaviṣyanti chudīcyāṃ dambhavaiṣṇaṣāḥ || 75 ||
śivasāmānyavaktāraṃ śivasāmānyadarśinam |
dṛṣṭvā svāyātsacailaḥ saśivasāmānyasaṅginnam || 76 ||
madhudarśitamārgeṇa pāpiṣṭhā vaiṣṇavāḥ kalau |
bhaviṣyanti tato mlecchāḥ śūdrā yūthabahiṣkṛtāḥ || 77 ||
tasmācchṛṇudhvaṃ viprendrā māhātmyaṃ pārvatīpateḥ |
bhaktiṃ tasya sadā kartumudyatā bhavata dhruvam || 78 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtakṣaunakasaṃvāde kalipraveśādi- kathanaṃ nāmonacatvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 39 ||
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ -
sūta bhadraṃ samācakṣva sevako yasya mādhavaḥ |
--
śrīmaheśasya viṣṇośca tulyatvaṃ bruvate katham || 1 ||
bruvanti tulyatāṃ kecidvaiparītyena kecana |
ekatvaṃ kecidīśena keśavasya vadanti hi || 2 ||
atra siddhāntamaryādāṃ brūhi tattvena sūtaja |
avādhāṃ yena cāsmākaṃ saṃśayo vinivartate || 3 ||
sūta uvāca -
śṛṇvantu ṛṣayaḥ sarve śrutisiddhāntamuttamam |
maheśānna paraṃ tattvaṃ sarvavedeṣu gīyate || 4 ||
baikuṇṭhaprabhṛtīnāṃ tu maheśakṛpayā punaḥ |
śrutismṛtipurāṇānāṃ siddhānto'yaṃ yathārthataḥ |
indropendrādayaḥ sarve maheśasyaiva kiṃkarāḥ || 6 ||
vedāntavedyamīśānaṃ pārvatīramaṇaṃ prabhum |
yo jānāti sa vaikuṇṭho duḥkhahā sarvadehinām || 7 ||
vaikuṇṭhaṃ manyate samyagīśānaṃ sa puraṃdaraḥ |
ya indraṃ manyate sarvasvāminaṃ sa ṛṣirmataḥ || 8||
svargalokaṃ samāpnoti munyājñāpratipālakaḥ |
advaitaṃ śivamīśānamajñātvā naiva mucyate || 9 ||
ghore kaliyuge prāpte śrīśaṃkaraparāṅmukhāḥ |
bhaviṣyanti narāstathyamiti dvaipāyano'bravīt || 10 ||
rudrodhāgninirdagdhe manmathe tasya bhāryayā |
ratyā vilapite tasya sakhāyo'pyatiduḥkhitāḥ || 11 ||
vasantādaya āgatya tāmūcuḥ kiṃ vidhīyate |
sarvalokeśituḥ śaṃbhorvarākā vairavā (kā) raṇe || 12 ||
ratiruvāca ---
manyeta ghātakaḥ sabaileoke'pūjyo bhavedayam |
tathā vighnaḥ prakartavyo yena kenāpi hetunā || 13 ||
asyāpakīrtirvaktavyā na caledyadi kiṃcana |
tena me duḥkhaśāntiḥ syātkiṃcinmātraṃ na cānyathā || 14 ||
vasantādaya ūcuḥ caturdaśasu vidyāsu gīyate candraśekharaḥ |
vedāntā yaṃ ca gāyanti munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ || 15 ||
brahmā devatāḥ sarvā indropendrādayastathā |
nyūnatāṃ tasya yo brūte karmacāṇḍāla ucyate || 16 ||
tena tulyo yadā viṣṇurbrahmā vā yadi gadyate |
ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ || 17 ||
tulyatā yadi no śakyā nyūnatāyāstu kā kathā |
mitrasyā''nṛṇyamicchāmaḥ saṃkaṭaṃ pratibhāti naḥ || 18 ||
sūta uvāca ---
vicāthaivaṃ tadā sarve mahāmohapuraḥsarāḥ |
tapastepurmahāraudraṃ sarvalokabhayaṃkaram || 19 ||
kadācidbhagavānbrahmā prādurāsīdayānidhiḥ |
pañcamo hetuvādaśca madhunā sarva āśritāḥ |
tānuvāca tato brahmā vṛṇīdhvaṃ manasepsitam || 21 ||
yathā vāṇī ca bhavatāṃ tathā'haṃ dātumudyataḥ |
mohādyā ūcuḥ -
asmākaṃ paramaṃ mitraṃ kaṃdarpo nāśitaḥ prabho ||22||
mahādevena tenāmī ānṛṇyaṃ kartumudyatāḥ |
bhaviṣyāmo vayaṃ tāta rudrapūjābhinindakāḥ || 23 ||
yathā na labhate pūjāmasmattaścandraśekharaḥ |
brahmovāca -
adhunā na bhavedevaṃ bhaviṣyatyatha tacciram || 24 ||
bhaviṣyāma iti proktaṃ bhavatto nānyathā kvacit |
ye bhavadvaśagā lokāstebhyaḥ pūjā na dhūrjaṭeḥ || 25 ||
prārthito'yaṃ varo datto yatheṣṭaṃ kartumarhatha || 26 ||
sūta uvāca -
ityuktvā tānatho brahmā tatraivāntaradhīyata |
sarve te mantrayāṃcakruḥ kalinā saha duḥkhitāḥ || 27 ||
kaliruvāca -
bhavadbhiradhunā noktaṃ bhaviṣyāma itīritam |
tato matsamaye prāpte sarvameva bhaviṣyati || 28 ||
asmatta iti yatproktaṃ tena cāsmadvaśe sthitāḥ |
nindākarā bhaviṣyanti nāramānyo manyate na saḥ || 29 ||
lobhamohādisaṃyuktāḥ prāpte ca mayi dāruṇe |
hetuvādaṃ puraskṛtya śivabhaktiparāṅmukhāḥ || 30 ||
sūta uvāca -
tataḥ kaliyuge prāpte sarvadharmavivarjite |
mlecchairbrāhmaṇadhenūnāṃ vidhvaṃsanakare khare || 31 ||
asvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāre jaina vauddhādi saṃkule |
brāhmaṇe mlecchamārgasthe gū̃dre brāhmaṇaghātini || 32 ||
tadā vasantaḥ karṇāṭatilaṅgādikadūṣakaḥ |
madhunāmā ca vidhavākṣetre viprādbhaviṣyati || 33 ||
golakaḥ sa tu pāpiṣṭhaḥ padmapādukamīśvaram |
vedāntavyākhyānarataṃ śiṣyatvenārcayiṣyati || 34 ||
śāstraṃ pūrṇa tato'dhītya sthita āhnikavarjitaḥ |
kimagnihotraṃ ko yāgo hetumevaṃ kariṣyati || 35 ||
gururākarṇya tadvākyaṃ brāhmaṇo na bhavedayam |
iti niścitya taṃ duṣṭaṃ vakṣyati śrutatadvacāḥ || 36 ||
gururuvāca -
ko varṇastava me brūhi yathārtha vedadūṣaka |
karmabrahmodbhavadveṣṭā notpattirbrāhmaṇāttava || 37 ||
madhuruvāca—
brāhmaṇādahamutpanno brāhmaṇyāṃ ca na saṃśayaḥ |
satyaṃ vadāmi no mithyā kathaṃ māṃ paśyase guro || 38 ||
gururuvāca -
tvanmātā kena dattā re kasya putrī kadā katham |
kasmai dattā ca vidhinā kena tadbrūhi mā ciram || 39 ||
madhuruvāca -
vidhavā jananī nātha brāhmaṇena tapasvinā |
garbhiṇī samabhūttasmādayaṃ dehastato'bhavat || 40 ||
gururuvāca -
kapaṭena yataḥ śāstraṃ matto'dhītaṃ durātmanā |
tena siddhāntamaryādā kadācinmā sphuratviyam || 41 ||
madhuruvāca -
bhaviṣyati mahābhāga vacanaṃ tava nānyathā |
pūrvapakṣoṃ mama hṛdi prādurbhavatu niścalaḥ || 42 ||
-
gururuvāca —
andhatā tavaṃ siddhānte pūrvapakṣe ca pāṭavam |
bhavatyeva paraṃ tvekaṃ pāpāḥ śiṣyā bhavantu te || 43 ||
mohātsiddhāntarahitā lobhātte nṛpasevakāḥ |
krodhātkaṭhinavaktāro dambhādveṣeṇa sundarāḥ || 44 ||
hetuvādena śāstrāṇi sarvāṇi na vidanti te |
nirayeṣveva ghoreṣu gamiṣyantyacirācciram || 45 ||
sūta uvāca -
madhunāmā tataḥ prāpya śāpaṃ taṃ duṣṭabuddhimān |
bādarāyaṇasūtrāṇāṃ vyākhyānaṃ sa kariṣyati || 46 ||
madhvācāryastato bhāvādākṣiṇātyo mahānkalau |
tacchiṣyāḥ pratiśiṣyāśca nā''ryāvarte na cotkale || 47 ||
na gauḍe va ca gaṅgāyāstīre godāvarītaṭe |
mārbudāraṇyamadhye ca tatpracāro bhaviṣyati || 48 ||
yathā yathā kalervoraḥ pracāro hi bhaviṣyati |. tathā tathā mahārāṣṭra haitukā viralāḥ kvacit || 49 ||
tato'tiduṣṭasamaye mahāmlecchaistiraskṛte |
pañcavarṣastu saṃnyāsī paṭhitvā duṣṭabuddhimān |
śiṣyopaśiṣyasaṃyukto hetuvādaṃ kariṣyati || 51 ||
tattvaṃ saṃsāra ityeva na bādhyaḥ satya eva hi |
vadatyatastattvabādīḥ mithyāvādī sa ucyate || 52 ||
mithyābhūtaḥ prapañco'yaṃ mayā nirmita iṣyate |
māyāvādina ityete vastutastattvavādinaḥ || 53 ||
sacchāstraṃ jaiminīyaṃ tu karmakāṇḍapravartakam |
gautamīyaṃ tu sacchāstramīśvarapratipādakam || 54 ||
puṃsprakṛtyorvivekasya bodhakaṃ kāpilaṃ matam |
tathā vaiśeṣikaṃ śāstramīśvarapratipādakam || 55 |
pātañjalaṃ yogaśāstraṃ śaivaṃ tacchāstramiṣyate |
vedāntaśāstramūrdhanyamadvaitaṃ yacca bodhayet || 56 ||
vedāḥ sarve ṣaḍaṅgāstu purāṇānītihāsakaḥ |
smṛtiśvopapurāṇāni tathopasmṛtayaḥ śubhāḥ || 57 ||
anyonyaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ prāmāṇyamadhikārataḥ |
tātparye ca pumartheṣu sarvāṇyevaṃ jaguḥ kila || 58 |
kiṃcidvirodhe satyeva na virodho'sti tattvataḥ |
manyante śrīmaheśānaṃ sarvāṇyeva parātparam || 59 ||
pāpiṣṭhā naiva manyante vedamārga vahiṣkṛtāḥ |
ācārya madhunāmānaṃ vadanto vidhavāsutam || 60 ||
pracchanno'sau mahāduṣṭacārvāko madhusaṃjñakaḥ |
bhaviṣyati kalau viprāḥ śivanindāpravartakaḥ || 61 ||
mohātsiddhāntabāhyatvaṃ krodhācchāstraniṣedhanam |
lobhena nṛpateḥ sevā dambhādanyapratāraṇam || 62 ||
gaṇikāmaithunaṃ kāmāddhetuvādena vāditā |
bhaviṣyati kalau viprāḥ ṣoḍheyaṃ tattvavāditā || 63 ||
pañcavarṣa yatiṃ kṛtvā krameṇā''dāya bālakam |
māṭhāpatyaṃ vidhāsyanti dravyalobhena nāstikāḥ || 64 ||
pāramparya maṭhasyaiva rakṣiṣyantyabhirāgiṇaḥ |
bhogāsaktāśca pāpiṣṭhā dāsīgamanakāriṇaḥ || 65 ||
nāmnā saṃnyāsinastīrthe yānārūḍhāḥ sasevakāḥ |
naravāhanamārūḍhāḥ śikhāsūtra bahiṣkṛtāḥ || 66 ||
tatpakṣapātino mūḍhā gṛhasthāḥ śivanindakāḥ |
mithyā vaiṣṇavamānena grastā nirayagāmiṇaḥ || 67 ||
vaiṣṇavā veṣamātreṇa tantumātreṇa vāḍavāḥ |
vādinaḥ krodhamātreṇa vidvāṃso hetuvādataḥ || 68 ||
paṭhiṣyanti ca śāstrāṇi keciddūpaṇasiddhaye |
svakīyaṃ gopayiṣyanti parakīyeṇa paṇḍitāḥ || 69 ||
sūta uvāca -
mahāmohādayaḥ sarve ratimāśvāsya bhāminīm |
procuśca ślakṣṇayā vācā tadduḥ khavinivārakāḥ || 70 ||
mohādaya ūcu: - rate mā kuru saṃtāpamahaṃ mohaḥ kaleḥ sakhā |
krodhaḥ patyuḥ paro bandhurlobhamohau ca devarau || 71 ||
māpte kaliyuge pūrṇe mohalobhādayo vayam |
vasantaṃ madhunāmānamavatīrṇa ca dakṣiṇe || 72 ||
samāśritya tato hetuvādaṃ kuṭila buddhayaḥ |
kariṣyāmo yathā śakyaṃ śivapūjānivāraṇam || 73 ||
sūta uvāca -
iti te ratimāśvāsya yathāgatamito gatāḥ |
iti sarve samākhyātaṃ śivanindakakāraṇam || 74 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde maheśaviṣṇutu- lyatvakāraṇādikathanaṃ nāma catvāriṃśo'dhyāyaḥ || 40 ||
ṛṣaya ūcu: – sudarśanākhyaṃ yaccakraṃ labdhavāṃstatkathaṃ hariḥ |
-
mahādevādbhagavataḥ sūta tadvaktumarhasi || 1 ||
sūta uvāca -
devāsurāṇāmabhavatsaṅgrāmo'dbhutadarśanaḥ |
devā vinirjitā daityairviṣṇuṃ śaraṇamāgatāḥ || 2 |
stutvā taṃ vividhaiḥ stotraiḥ praṇamya purataḥ sthitāḥ |
bhayabhītāśca te sarve kṣatāṅgāḥ kreśitā bhṛśam || 3||
tāndṛṣṭvā prāha bhagavāndevadevo janārdanaḥ |
kimarthamāgatā devā vaktumarhatha sāṃpratam || 4 ||
vacaḥ śrutvā harerdevāḥ praṇamyocuḥ surottamāḥ |
nirjitā dānavaiḥ sarve śaraṇaṃ tvāmihā''gatāḥ || 5 ||
gatistvameva devānāṃ trātā tvaṃ puruṣottama |
hantumarhasi tāśīghramadhyānvārijekṣaṇa || 6 ||
jālaṃdharavadhārthāya yaccakraṃ śūlapāṇinaḥ |
mahādevavarāllabdhaṃ jahi tena mahābalān || 7 ||
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhagavānvārijekṣaṇaḥ |
ahaṃ devāstathā nūnaṃ kariṣyāmīti suvratāḥ || 8 ||
himavatparvataṃ gatvā pūjayāmāsa śaṃkaram |
liṅgaṃ tatra pratiṣṭhāpya snāpya gandhodakaiḥ śubhaiḥ || 9||
tvaritākhyena rudreṇa saṃpūjya ca maheśvaram |
tato nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa tuṣṭāva parameśvaram || 10 ||
pratināma ca padmāni tairiṣṭvā vṛṣabhadhvajam |
bhavādyairnāmabhirbhaktyā stotuṃ samupacakrame || 11 ||
viṣṇuruvāca -
bhavaḥ śivo haro rudraḥ puṣkalo mugdhalocanaḥ |
agragaṇyaḥ sadācāraḥ sarvaḥ śaṃbhurmaheśvaraḥ || 12 ||
īśvaraḥ sthāṇurīśānaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt |
varīyānvarado vanyaḥ śaṃkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ || 13 ||
gaṅgādharaḥ śūladharaḥ parārthaikamayojakaḥ |
sarvajñaḥ sarvadevādirgiridhanvā jaṭādharaḥ || 14 ||

cacāla brahmabhuvanaṃ cakampe ca vasuṃdharā |

śaṃbhorbhagavatastejastadṛdṛṣṭvā prahasaṃśivaḥ |

devakāryemi jñātamidānīṃ madhusūdana |

gṛhītvā tadguṇairdaityāhi viṣṇo mamājñayā || 151 ||

abravītkhaṇḍaparaśuṃ prāñjaliḥ praṇayānvitaḥ || 154 ||

bhagavandevadeveśa paramātma śivāvyaya |

budabudairardhacandraitha svarṇairaśvatthapatrakaiḥ || 24 ||
sitairvikasitaiḥ padma raktainīlotpalaistathā |
vimānena vicitreṇa muktādānā dvijottamāḥ || 25 ||
sitamṛtpātrakaiścaiva suślakṣṇaiḥ pūrṇakumbhakaḥ |
phalapallavamālābhivaijayantībhiraṃśuḥ || 26 ||
pañcāśadīpamālābhirdhūpaiśca vividhaistathā |
pañcāśailasaṃyuktaṃ likhitvā padmamuttamam || 27 ||
tadvarṇastathā cūrṇaiḥ śvetacūrṇairathāpi vā |
eka hastapramāṇena kṛtvā padmaṃ vidhānataḥ || 28 ||
karṇikāyāṃ vyasedevaṃ devyā deveśvaraṃ bhavam |
parṇāni vinyase rudreḥ prāgādyanukramāt || 29 ||
praṇavādinamontāni sarvavarṇāni suvratāḥ |
saṃpūjyaivaṃ suraśreṣṭhaṃ gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt || 30 ||
brāhmaṇānbhojayettatra pañcāśadvidhipūrvakam |
akṣamālāpavītaṃ ca kuṇḍale ca kamaṇḍalum || 31 ||
āsanaṃ ca tathā daṇḍamuṣṇīṣaṃ vastrameva ca |
dattvā teṣāṃ dvijendrāṇāṃ devadevāya śaṃbhave || 32 ||
mahācaruṃ nivedyaivaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gomithunaṃ tathā |
ante ca devadevāya dattvā tadvarṇamaṇḍalam || 33 ||
yāgopayogidravyāṇi śivāya vinivedayet |
oṃkārāyaṃ japeddhīmānprativarṇamanukramāt || 34 ||
evamālikhya yo bhaktyā varṇamaṇḍalamuttamam |
yatphalaṃ labhate martyastadvadāmi samāsataḥ || 35 |
sāṅgānvedānyathānyāyamadhītya vidhipūrvakān |
iṣṭvā yajñairyathānyāyaṃ jyotiṣṭomādibhiḥ kramāt || 36 ||
tato viśvajitā ceṣṭvā putrānutpādya mādṛśān |
vānaprasthāśramaṃ gatvā sadāraḥ sāgnireva ca || 37 ||
cāndrāyaṇādikānkṛtvā sarvānsaṃnyasya vai dvijāḥ |
brahmavidyāmadhītyaiva jñānamāpādya yatnataḥ || 38 ||
jñānena jñeyamālokya yogavitphalamāpnuyāt |
tatphalaṃ labhate sarve varṇamaṇḍaladarśanāt || 39 ||
yena kenāpi vā''likhya pralipyā''yatanāśramam |
uttare dakṣiṇe vāpi pṛṣṭhato vā dvijottamāḥ || 40 ||
catuṣkoṇe'pi vā cūrṇairalaṃkṛtya samantataḥ |
vikīrya gandhakusumairdhūpaidapaiśvaturvidhaiḥ || 41 ||
prārthayedevamīśānaṃ śivaloke sa gacchati || 42 ||
tatra bhuktvā mahānbhogānkalpakoṭiśataṃ naraḥ |
svadehagandhaiśva śubhaiḥ pūrayaśivamandiram || 43 ||
kramādgāndharvamāsādya gandharvaiśva supūjitaḥ |
kramādāgatya loke'sminrājā bhavati vīryavān || 44 ||
āpaḥ pūtā bhavantyetā vastrapūtāḥ samudbhavāḥ |
aphenā muniśārdūlā nādeyāśca viśeṣataḥ || 45 ||
tasmādvai sarvakāryāṇi vaidikāni dvijottamāḥ |
adbhiḥ kāryāṇi satataṃ pūtābhiḥ sarvasiddhaye || 46 ||
ahiṃsā tu paro dharmaḥ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ yataḥ |
tasmātsarvaprayatnena vastrapūtena kārayet || 47 ||
yānamabhayaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvadānottamottamam |
tasmātsā parihartavyā hiṃsā sarvatra sarvadā || 48 ||
manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ |
yadā darśitapanthānaḥ śivalokaṃ vrajanti te || 49 ||
trailokyamakhilaṃ hatvā yatpāpaṃ jāyate nṛṇām |
śivālaye nihatyaikamapi tatpāpamāpnuyāt || 50 ||
śivārthaṃ sarvadā kāryā puṣpāhaṃsā dvijottamaiḥ |
yajñārtha paśuhiṃsā ca rājñā duṣṭasya śāsanam || 51 ||
naṃ hantavyāḥ striyaḥ sarvā atreśva kulasaṃbhavāḥ |
brahmahatyāsamaṃ pāpamātreyyā vaghato bhavet || 52 ||
striyaḥ sarvā na hantavyā sarvaiścaiva dvijātibhiḥ |
sarvadharmeṣu viprendrāḥ pāpakarmaratā api || 53 ||
tasmādahiṃsādiyutaḥ śāntaḥ śivajanapriyaḥ |
bhaktiṃ śive samāsthāya tasmiñjanmani mucyate || 54 ||
viśveśvare virūpākṣe viśvavyāpini viśvage |
sarvamanyatparityajya bhaktiḥ kāryā manīṣibhiḥ || 55 ||
putravittādiṣu yathā saktaṃ cittaṃ sadā nṛṇām |
tathā sakṛdvirūpākṣe dūraṃ kiṃ śāṃkaraṃ padam || 56 ||
bhajante ye yathā śaṃbhuṃ phalaṃ teṣāṃ tathāvidham |
prayacchati mahādevo bhaktirnaivāsti niṣphalā || 57 ||
ucchiṣṭaḥ pūjayedīśaṃ mohāndho yadudvijādhamaḥ |
piśācaloke vipulānbhogānbhuṅkte sa mānavaḥ || 58 ||
saṃkruddho rākṣasasthānamabhakṣī yākṣamāpnuyāt |
gānaśīlo hi gāndharva nṛtyaśīlastathaiva ca || 59 |
khyātiśalastathaivendramabbhakṣaścāndramāpnuyāt |
gāyatryā pūjayedīśamabdamekaṃ nirantaram || 60 ||
prājāpatyamathā''sādya sṛṣṭikartā svayaṃ bhavet |
brāhmaṃ ca praṇavenaiva tenaivā''moti vaiṣṇavam || 61 ||

sūta uvāca -
purā brahmādayo devā draṣṭukāmā maheśvaram |
mandaraṃ prayayuḥ sarve śaṃbhoḥ priyataraṃ girim || 3 |
stutvā prāñjalayodevā harasya purataḥ sthitāḥ |
tāndṛṣṭvā'tha mahādevo līlayā parameśvaraḥ || 4 ||
nepāmapahṛtaṃ jñānaṃ brahmādīnāṃ divaukasām |
devācchaṃstaṃ devamātmānaṃ purataḥ sthitam || 5 ||
āsaṃste sakṛdajñānāttamāhuḥ ko bhavāniti |
abravīdbhagavānīśo hyahameva purātanaḥ || 6 ||
āsaṃ prathamamevāhaṃ vartāmi ( ? ) ca surottamāḥ |
bhaviṣyāmi ca loke'sminmatto nānyo'sti kaścana || 7 ||
vyatiriktaṃ ca matto'sti nānyatkiṃcitsurottamāḥ |
nityānityo'hamevāsmi brahmā'haṃ brahmaṇaspatiḥ || 8 ||
diśaśva vidiśaścaiva prakṛtiśca pumānaham |
trinubjagatyanuṣṭup ca paktiśchandatrayīmayaḥ || 9 ||
satyo'haṃ sarvataḥ śāntastretāgnigaurahaṃ guruḥ |
goryahaṃ ca haravāhaṃ dyaurahaṃ jagatāṃ prabhuḥ || 10 ||
śreṣṭho'haṃ sarvatattvānāṃ variṣṭho'hamapāṃ patiḥ |
āpo'haṃ bhagavānīśastejo'haṃ vedirapyaham || 11 ||
ṛgvedo'haṃ yajurvedaḥ sāmavedo'hamātmabhūḥ |
atharvaṇo'tha mantro'haṃ tathā cāṅgirasāṃ baraḥ || 12 ||
itihāsapurāṇāni kalpo'haṃ kalpanā hyaham |
akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ cāhaṃ kṣāntiḥ śāntirahaṃ khagaḥ || 13 ||
guhyeo'haṃ sarvavedeṣu āraṇyo'hamajo'pyaham |
puṣkareṃ ca pavitraṃ ca madhyaṃ cāhaṃ tataḥ param || 14 ||
bahiścāhaṃ tathā cāntaḥ purastādahamavyayaḥ |
jyotiścāhaṃ tamaścāhaṃ brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ || 15 ||
buddhiśvāhamahaṃkārastanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca |
evaṃ sarve ca māmeva yo veda sa surottamaḥ || 16 ||
sa eva sarvavitsarvaḥ sarvātmā sarvadarśanaḥ |
gāṃ gobhirbrāhmaṇānsarvānbrāhmaṇyena havīṃṣi ca || 17 ||ḥ haॅvipā yastathā satyaṃ satyena ca surottamāḥ |
dharma dharmeṇa ca tathā tarpayāmi svatejasā || 18 ||
ityādi bhagavānuktvā tatraivāntaradhīyata |
nāpaśyaṃste tato devaṃ rudraṃ paramakāraṇam || 19 ||
taṃ devāḥ paramātmānaṃ rudraṃ dhyāyanti śaṃkaram |
sanārāyaṇakā devāḥ sendrāśca munayastathā || 20 ||
tatordhvabāhavo devā vastuvaśaṃkaraṃ tadā |
devā ūcu: - ya epa bhagavāndro brahmā viṣṇurmaheśvaraḥ || 21 ||
skandañcāgnistathā candro bhuvanāni caturdaśa |
bhūtāni ca tathā sūryaḥ somāṣṭa grahāstathā || 22 ||
prāṇaḥ kālo yamo mṛtyumṛtaṃ parameśvaraḥ |
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca vartamānaṃ maheśvaraḥ || 23 |
ન
viśvaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jagatsarvaṃ satyaṃ tasmai namo namaḥ |
omādau ca tathā madhye bhūrbhuvaḥ svastathaiva ca || 24 ||
ante tvaṃ viśvarūpo'si śīrṣe ca jagataḥ sadā |
tvaṃ dvividhordhvadhastattvaṃ sureśvaraḥ || 25 ||
śāntiśca tvaṃ tathā puṣṭistuṣṭiśvāpyahutaṃ hutam |
viśvaṃ caiva tathā'viśva dattaṃ khādattamīśvaraḥ || 26 ||
ṛtaṃ vā'pyathavā deva paramapyaparaṃ dhruvam |
parāyaṇaṃ satataṃ caiva asatāmapi śaṃkara || 27 ||
apāma somamamṛtā abhūmāganma jyotiravidāma devān |
kiṃ nūnamasmānkṛṇavadarātiḥ kimu dhūrtiramṛta martyasya || 28 ||
etajjagadveditavyamakṣaraṃ sūkṣmamavyayam |
prājāpatyaṃ pavitraṃ vā saumyamagrāhyamagriyam || 29 ||
āgneyenāpi cā'yaṃ vāyavyena samīraṇam |
saumyena saumyaṃ grasate tejasā svena līlayā || 30 ||
tasmai namo'pasaṃhartre mahāgrāsāya śūline |
hṛdisthā devatāḥ sarvā hṛdi prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ || 31 ||

= sa yo jīvottaraḥ sākṣātsa ākāraḥ sanātanaḥ |
oṃkāro yaḥ sa vai devaḥ maṇavo vyāpya tiṣṭhati || 33 ||
anantatāraḥ sūkṣmaśca śuklaṃ vaidyutameva ca |
parabrahma sa īśāna eko rudraḥ sa eva ca || 34 ||

ūrdhvamunnāmayatyevaṃ sa oṃkāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 35 ||

yathā'nye ca tato'nanto rudraḥ paramakāraṇam || 37 ||

sarvalokānkrameṇaiva vo gṛhṇāti maheśvaraḥ ||

eṣa hi devaḥ pradiśo nu sarvāḥ pūrvo hi jātaḥ sa u garbhe antaḥ |

sūta uvāca -
vakṣyāmi śivamāhātmyaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ |
bahubhirbahudhā śāstraiḥ kīrtitaṃ munipuṃgavaiḥ || 1 ||
sadasarūpamityāhuḥ sadasaccāpi saṃsthitam |
taṃ śivaṃ munayaḥ kecidyaṃ prapaśyanti sūrayaḥ || 2 ||
bhūtabhāvavikāraiṇa dvitīyena saducyate |
avyaktena vihīnaṃ syādavyaktamasadityapi || 3 ||
ubhe te śivarūpeṇa śivādanyanna vidyate |
tayoḥ patitvācca śivaḥ sadasatpatirucyate || 4 ||
kṣarākṣarātmake māhuḥ kṣarākṣaraparaṃ tathā |
śivaṃ maheśvare kecinmunayastattvacintakāḥ || 5 ||
uktamakṣaramavyaktaṃ vyaktākṣaramudāhṛtam |
rūpe te śaṃkarasyaiva nānā paramucyate || 6 ||
tayoḥ paraḥ śivaḥ śāntaḥ kṣarākṣaraparo budhaiḥ |
ucyate paramārthena mahādevo maheśvaraḥ || 7 ||
samaṣṭi yapaṃ samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam |
vadanti kecidācāryaiḥ śivaṃ paramakāraṇam || 8 ||
samaṣṭimāhuravyaktaṃ vyaṣṭiṃ vyaktiṃ munīśvarāḥ |
rūpe te gadite śaṃbhornāstyanyadvastu kiṃcana || 9 ||
tayoḥ kāraṇabhāvena śivo hi parameśvaraḥ |
ucyate yogaśāstrajñaiḥ samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam || 10 ||
kṣetra kṣetrajñarūpati śivaḥ kaiśvidudāhṛtaḥ |
caturviṃśatitattvāni kṣetraśabdena sūrayaḥ |

na kiṃcica śivādanyaditi māhurmanīṣiṇaḥ |
kecidevaṃ praśaṃsanti mahādevaṃ munīśvaram || 13 ||
vedārthatattvaviduṣaḥ samyavaśrutyanusārataḥ |

buddhayā vicārayatyeṣa para eva maheśvaraḥ |

" mahipani mahāmāye cāmuṇḍe muṇḍadhātini || 31 ||

sūta uvāca -
evaṃ munīnāṃ gaditaṃ bhavānyāścaritaṃ śubham |

ṛṣaya ūcu: - tithīnāṃ nirṇayaṃ sūta prāyaścittavidhiṃ tathā |
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ vyāsaśiṣya mahāmate || 1 ||
sūta uvāca -
śṛṇudhvamṛṣayaḥ sarve tithīnāṃ nirṇayaṃ param |
anirṇītāsu tithiṣu na kiṃcitkarma sidhyati || 2 ||
śrautaṃ smārta vrataṃ dānaṃ yaccānyatkarma vaidikam |
nirṇītāsu tithiṣveva karma kurvīta nānyathā || 3 ||
prāyaḥ prāntamupoṣyaṃ syattithedaiva phalepsubhiḥ |
mūlaṃ hi pitṛtuṣṭyarthaṃ pitryaṃ coktaṃ maharṣibhiḥ || 4 ||
yāṃ prāpyāstamupaityarkaḥ sā cetsyātrimuhūrtikā |
dharmakṛtyeṣu sarveṣu saṃpūrṇā tāṃ tristithim || 5 ||
kṣaye pūrvā kartavyā vṛddhī kāryā tathottarā |
-
kṛṣṇāṣṭamī ca bhūtā ca kartavyā saṃmukhī tithiḥ || 8 ||
śukla dve dve tathā kṛṣṇe yugādī kavayo viduḥ |
śukle pūrvāhnike kārye kṛṣṇe caivāparāhnike || 9 ||
nāgaviddhā tu yā ṣaṣṭhī śivaviddhā tu saptamī |
daśamyaikādaśī viddhā nopoṣyaiva kathaṃcana || 10 ||
jñātvaivaṃ sūryacandrābhyāṃ tithiṃ sphuṭataraṃ vratī |
ekādaśīṃ tṛtīyāṃ ca ṣaṣṭhīṃ copavasetsadā ||| 11 ||
phalamekādaśī hanti vihitaṃ daśamīyutā |
pāraṇaṃ tu trayodaśyāmullaṅghya dvādaśīvratam || 12 |
pāraṇā he na labhyeta dvādaśī sakalā'pi cet |
tadānīṃ daśamīviddhānyaikādaśī tithiḥ || 13 ||
śukle vā yadi vā kṛṣṇe bhavedekādaśadvayam |
uttarāṃ tu yatiḥ kuryātpūrvāmeva sadā gṛhī || 14 ||
darśa ca paurṇamāsaṃ ca saptamīṃ pitṛvāsaram |
pūrvaviddhamakurvāṇo narakaṃ pratipadyate || 15 ||
sinīvālī dvijaigrahyā sāgnikaiḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi |
kuhū̃: strībhistathā śūdrairapi cānyairanagnikaiḥ || 16 ||
pāraṇe maraṇe nṝṇāṃ tithistātkālikī smṛtā |
niśātrateṣu ca grāhyā pradoṣavyāpinī sadā || 17 ||
upoṣitavyaṃ nakṣatraṃ yenāstaṃ yāti bhāskaraḥ |
yacca vā yujyate vibhāḥ pradoṣe himaraśminā || 18 ||
arvākṣoḍaśa nāḍyaistu parataścaiva poḍaśa |
puṇyakālo'rkasaṃkrāntau snānadānajapādiṣu || 19 ||
āsanna saṃkramaṃ puṇyaṃ dinārghe snānadānayoḥ |
rātrau saṃkramaṇe bhānorviṣuvatyayane dine || 20 ||
sūryendugrahaṇaṃ yāvattāvatkuryājjapādikam |
na svapyānna ca bhuñjīta snātvā bhuñjīta muktayoḥ || 21 ||
ādityaśītakiraṇau grastāvantaṃ gatau yadā |
dṛṣṭvā tadā'nyadivase snātvā bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ || 22 ||
sūtake mṛtake vā'pi nopavāsaṃ tyajedavatī |
yasmādbhaaadishta gardino vedavādibhiḥ || 23 ||
tasmātpramādaduḥkhe vā sūtake vyasane'pi ca |
snātvā kārya vrataṃ vimā anyathā vratalopabhāk || 24 ||
devārcanādikaṃ karma kārya dīkṣānvitaiḥ sadā |
nāsti śāvaṃ yatasteṣāṃ sūtakaṃ ca yadātmanām || 25 ||
śive devārcanaṃ yasya yasya vā'gniparigrahaḥ |
brahmacāriyatīnāṃ ca śarīre nāsti sūtakam || 26 ||
mahacchabdaprayuktā yā yā ca sopapadā tithiḥ |
sāmāvāsyāsamā jñeyā dānādhyayanakarmasu || 27 ||
mārgā hyaparapakṣe tu pūrvamadhyā tu śabditā |
syuścaturaṣṭakāstisraḥ saptamyādiṣvanukramāt || 28 ||
mādhe pañcadaśī kṛṣṇā narbhasye ca trayodaśī |
tṛtīyā mādhave śuklā navamī kārtike sitā || 29 ||
etā yugādayaḥ proktāḥ sarvāścākṣaya puṇyadāḥ |
siṃhavṛścikayoḥ kumbhasaṃkrāntiṣu ( ! ) bhavantyuta || 30 ||
kramātkṛtayugādīnāṃ yugāntāśca maharṣayaḥ |
śrāddhapakṣe trayodaśyāṃ maghāsvinduḥ kare raviḥ || 31 ||
yadā tadā gajacchāyā śrāddhe puṇyairavāpyate |
dhanustrīmī nayugmāṅkāḥ ṣaḍaśītimukhāḥ smṛtāḥ || 32 ||
aśvayukśukla navamī dvādaśī kārtike sitā |
tṛtīyā caitramāsasya tathā bhādrapadasya ca || 33 ||
saṃkrāntayastathā puṇyā bhāsvato dvādaśaiva hi || 36 |
parvasveteṣu dānāni dhenu śailādikāni ca |
prayacchanti dvijendrebhyo labhante cākṣayāṃ gatim || 37 ||
pānīyamapyeṣu tilairvimiśraṃ dadyātpitṛbhyaḥ prayato manuṣyaḥ |

sūta uvāca -
prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvaṃ munipuṃgavāḥ |
sarveṣāmeva varṇānāṃ śuddhimāha yathā raviḥ || 1 |
dvividhaṃ pāpamityuktaṃ prakaṭaṃ guptameva ca |
prakaṭaṃ prakaṭenaiva rahasyena tathetarat || 2 ||
vedaśāstrārthavidvāṃso dharmaśāstrārthapāragāḥ |
kāmakrodhavinirmuktāḥ śāntātmāno jitendriyāḥ || 3 ||
samāḥ śatrau ca mitre ca hiṃsālobhavivarjitāḥ |
ekaviṃśatisaṃkhyākāḥ sapta pañca trayo'tha vā || 4 ||
yaṃ brūyurukta saṃkhyākāḥ sa dharmaḥ syāditi śrutiḥ |
brahmahā madyapaḥ steyī gurutalpaga eva ca || 5 ||
mahāpātakinaścaite yaśca taiḥ saha saṃset |

brahmahā dvādaśābdāni niyatātmā vane vaset || 7 ||
|| bhikṣāhāreṇa satataṃ dhṛtvā śavaśirodhvajam |
ekakālaṃ caredbhaikṣaṃ doṣaṃ vikhyāpayannṛṇām || 8 ||
pūrṇe tu dvādaśe varṣe brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati |
jvalantaṃ praviśedagniṃ bhṛgoḥ patanameva ca |
kuryādanaśanaṃ vā'pi brāhmaṇārthe tyajedasūn || 12 ||

gatvā vārāṇasīṃ vā'pi kālāttatra tyajedasūn || 11 ||

bhrātṛbhāryā bhāgineyīṃ gatvā pāpāpanuttaye || 20 ||
cāndrāyaṇāni catvāri pañca vā kathitāni vai |
mātulasya sutāṃ gatvā sakhibhāryāṃ tathaiva ca || 21 ||

udakyāgamane caiva trirātreṇa viśudhyati || 22 ||

ślokārthe nāsti |
veśyāyā gamane caiva prājāpatyaṃ samācaret || 24 ||

na tasyā gamane pāpaṃ prajotpattau tathaiva ca |
raṇḍāyā gamane caiva caretsāṃtapanaṃ vratam || 27 ||
saṃvatsareṇa bhavati gurutalpasamo hi saḥ |
nahīṃ śailūṣikīṃ caiva rajakīṃ veṇujīvanīm || gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ kuryāttathā carmopajīvanīm |
dīkṣitaṃ kṣatrimaṃ hatvā caredrahmaṇo vratam || 29 ||
adīkṣitasya hanane ṣaḍabdaṃ kṛcchramācaret |
vaiśyaṃ tu kāmato hatvā tryabdakṛcchraṃ samācaret || 30 ||
nihatya brāhmaṇī viprastvaṣṭavarṣe vrataṃ caret |
varṣaṣaṭkaṃ tu rājanyāṃ vaiśyāṃ saṃvatsaratrayam || 31||
caitsareṇa viśuddhaḥ syācchūdrastrīvadha eva ca |
veśyāṃ hatvā pramādena kiṃciddānamihocitam || 32 ||
markaṭaṃ nakulaṃ kākaṃ varāhaṃ mūṣakaṃ tathā |
mārjāraṃ vātha maṇḍūkaṃ śvānaṃ vai kukkuṭaṃ kharam || 33 ||
pādakṛcchraṃ careddhatvā kṛcchramaśvavadhe smṛtam |
taptakṛcchraṃ hastivadhe pārākaṃ govadhe smṛtam || 34 ||
kāmato govadhe naiva śuddhirdṛṣṭā manīṣibhiḥ |
bhakṣyabhojyāpaharaṇe yānaśayyāsanasya ca || 35 ||
puṣpamūlaphalānāṃ ca pañcagavyaṃ viśodhanam |
tṛṇakāṣṭhadrumāṇāṃ ca śuṣkānnasya guḍasya ca || 36 ||

kāmatodumbaraṃ jagdhvā taptakṛcchraṃ samācaret |
alābuṃ kiṃśukaṃ jagdhvā prājāpatyaṃ samācaret || 40 ||

prājāpatyaṃ caretsamyagretoviṇmūtrabhakṣaṇe || 42 ||

mahāpātakinaṃ spṛṣṭvā vedavikrayiṇaṃ tathā |
rajasvalāṃ ca cāṇḍālīmajñātvā yadi bhojayet || 46 ||

ahorātreṇa śuddhiḥ syācchramaśrukarmaṇi maithune |
kharayānaṃ samāruhya tathā caivoyānakam || 48 ||
nano yastu viśedāpatrirātreṇa viśudhyati |
pāpānāmadhikaṃ pāpaṃ devatānāṃ ca nindanam || 49 ||

sakṛdyaḥ kurute nindāṃ śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ || 50 ||
taraya śuddhirna dṛṣṭā'sti purāṇe munibhiḥ kṛtā |

śṛṇoti gurunindāṃ yastasya cāndrāyaṇatrayam || 52 |
ekāsanaṃ copaviśedguruṇā saha mūḍhadhīḥ |
prāyaścittaṃ na tasyāsti pāpaṃ gurutaraṃ hi tat || 53 ||
prāyaścittamapīcchanti kecidajñānataḥ kṛte |
kuryātsāṃ tapanaṃ caiva cāndrāyaṇacatuṣṭayam || 54 ||
yo'yaṃ śuddhividhiḥ prokto guroraṅgīkṛtepsayā |
vāgdattasyāpradānena brahmahatyāsamaṃ bhavet || 55 ||
prāyaścittaṃ na tasyāsti dattaigrāmaśatairapi |
śivadravyāpaharaṇaṃ gurorapyaṇumātrakam || 56 ||
kutsanaṃ ca tathā śaṃbhorgurorapi tathaiva ca |
tathā ca śivabhaktānāṃ : jñānasya ca vidūṣaṇam || 57 ||
girijāyāśca viṣṇośca skandasyebhamukhasya ca |
yogināṃ ca tathā nindā nindino'pi tathā dvijāḥ || 58 ||
pāpānyetāni sarvāṇi brahmahatyāsamāni vai |
tasmānna nindedetāṃstu karmaṇā manasā girā || 59 ||
yadīcchecchāśvataṃ rathānamiti devo'bravīdraviḥ |
prāyaścittasya sarvasya paścāttāpo hi kāraṇam || 60 ||
na tena rahitaṃ pāpaṃ gacchatīti hi niścitam |
prāyaścitte kṛte paścāttasminpāpe pravartate || 61 ||
kṛtaṃ tvakṛtameva syāttatpāpaṃ pūrvavatsthitam |
sthūlāni yāni pāpāni sūkṣmāṇi vividhānyapi || 62 ||
tāni nāśayati kṣipraṃ muhūrta śivacintanam |
sarvapāpāpanodārthaṃ prāyaścittaṃ vadāmyaham || 63 ||
samāhito jale magnaḥ śivaṃ dhyāyanprasannadhīḥ |
aṣṭakṛtvo hara iti japanpāpaiḥ pramucyate || 64 ||

guruṇā daivataiḥ sārdhaṃ punareva sa devarāṭ |

ityuktvā mayayurdevāḥ śakrādyā brahmaṇā saha |
meroruttarattaḥ śṛṅgaṃ yatra tiṣṭhati mādhavaḥ || 42 ||
guptastiṣṭhatyameyātmā tārakādbhayapīḍitaḥ |
sabrahmakānsurāndṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭaḥ provāca mādhavaḥ || 43 ||
mādhava uvāca -
upāyaścintitaḥ ko'tra vadhārthaṃ tārakasya hi |
asti ceducyatāṃ devāḥ śarma no jāyate yathā || 44 ||
sūta uvāca -
evaṃ viṣṇorvacaḥ śrutvā brahmādyāḥ surasattamāḥ |
yathoktaṃ brahmaṇā tebhyastathoktaṃ viṣṇave surai: || 45 |
kimidānīṃ tu kartavyamiti saṃcintya devarāṭ |
so'smaranmanasā kāmamajeyamasuraiḥ suraiḥ || 46 ||
śakrasya cintitaṃ jñātvā kāmo ratipatiḥ svayam |
śacīpatiṃ samāgamya prāha puṣpadhanurdharaḥ || 47 ||
koma uvāca -
kiṃ kāryaṃ tridaśaśreṣṭha kartavyaṃ kiṃ mayā prabho |
tītreṇa tapasā ko hi sthānamīheta tāvakam || 48 ||
kiṃ vā kācittavā''deśaṃ kartuṃ necchati cāṅganā |
tāṃ kāminīṃ karomyadya tava dhyānaparāyaṇām || 49 ||
na kaścidasti me śūro na mānī na ca paṇḍitaḥ |
vyāpayāmi jagatkṛtstraṃ brahmāyaṃ ratambagocaram || 50 ||
kakhaga asaṃśita pasnakeṣvayaṃ śloko nāsti |
atha kiṃ bahunoktena durvāsā vā mahāmuniḥ |
so'pi viddhaḥ patatyāśu madvāṇairmarutāṃ pate || 51 ||
indra uvāca -
jānāmyahaṃ raternātha sāmarthyaṃ puṣpadhanvinaḥ |
nūnaṃ hi sarvakāryāṇi tvattaḥ sidhyanti nānyathā || 52 ||
gaccha pārśve maheśasya surāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā |
cittaṃ harasya saṃkṣobhya pārvatyāḥ saṃgamaṃ kuru || 53 ||
etadeva hi me kāryameṣa eva manoratha: !
etasmātkāraṇātvaṃ hi smṛtaḥ puṣpadhanurdhara || 54 ||
evaṃ śakravacaḥ śrutvā valavānmakaradhvajaḥ |
madhoḥ sakhā ratīyuktaḥ pañcavāṇo manobhavaḥ || 55 ||
yatrāssste bhagavāśaṃbhunadṛṣṭyā samāhitaḥ |
niṣkampaḥ svātmanā''tmānaṃ cintayāno maheśvaraḥ || 56 ||
prāpya śaṃbhorāyatanamapaśyanmakaradhvajaḥ |
śailādi dvāradeśe tu meruśṛṅgamivoditam || 57 ||
sarvābharaṇasayuktaṃ sahasrādityavarcasam |
śūlahastaṃ trinetraṃ ca candrāvayavabhūṣaṇam || 58 ||
vajrapāṇi caturbāhuṃ dvitīyamiva śaṃkaram |
taṃ dṛṣṭvā madano vimāścintākrāntastadā'bhavat || 59 ||
kathaṃ praviśya vakṣyāmi śaṃbhuṃ tridaśavanditam |
kathaṃ kāryaṃ kariṣyāmi surāṇāṃ prītivardhanam || 60 ||
cintayitvā tu bahudhā vañcanārthāya nandinaḥ |
vāyurūpaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā sugandhaṃ mṛduśītalam || 61 ||
praviveśa tadā kāmo dakṣiṇāṃ diśamāśrayam |
tena yāmyāṃ diśi gato vāyuti sukhāvahaḥ || 62 ||
adyāpi kāraṇātso'yaṃ sugandho mṛduśītalaḥ |
apaśyattatra madanaḥ sūryakoṭimivoditam || 63 ||
sahasranayanaṃ devaṃ sahasratanumīśvaram |
nīlakaṇṭhaṃ sudhābhāsaṃ śubhrakhaṇḍendudhāriṇam || 64||
jagadutpattisaṃhārasthityanugrahakāriṇam |
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ vidhūmamiva pāvakam || 65 ||
jagatpādaṃ jagacchrotraṃ sūkṣmasthūlaṃ parātparam || 67 ||
rudraṃ śarva paśupatimugraṃ bhīmaṃ bhavaṃ dvijāḥ |
mahādevaṃ maheśānamaṣṭamūrti jagatpatim || 68 ||
vyaktāvyaktaṃ trilokeśaṃ pūjitaṃ ca surāsuraiḥ |
atha dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ mahṛṣṭo makaradhvajaḥ || 69 ||
nikṛṣya cāpamāpūrya sthitaḥ paśyanbhavodbhavam |
evaṃ sthitasya kāmasya sahasrāṇyayutāni ṣaṭ || 70 ||
gatāni tasya varṣāṇi munīndrāśritajanmanaḥ |
tataḥ sa bhagavāndevo netre unmīlya śaṃkaraḥ || 71 ||
apaśyagirijā devīmagre viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ |
girīndraputrī tapasaḥ prasaktāṃ lajjayānvitām || 72 ||
dṛṣṭvā kimati vikalpabuddhyā kāmo'yamatreti vicintyaḥ śarvaḥ |
jñātvā vilokya pravikṛṣṭacāpaṃ netrāgnina 'sau madano'pi dagdhaḥ ||13||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde madanagahanaṃ nāma tripañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ || 53 ||
sūta uvāca -
dagdhe ratipatau śaṃbhuruvācācalakanyakām |
kimahaṃ va deveśi karomi manasi sthitam || 1 ||
varaṃ brūhi mahādevi dāsyāmyadya sureśvari |
mayi prasanne deveśi kiṃ durlabhamihāsti te || 2 ||
śrī pārvatyuvāca -
te tu kāme vada nīlakaṇṭha vareṇa kiṃ deva karomi te'dya |
vinaiva kāmena na cāsti bhāvaḥ strīpuṃsayorbhāskarakoṭikalpaḥ || 3 ||
bhāvasya hāneḥ sukhasaṃnikarṣaḥ kathaṃ bhavedbrūhi sureśavandya |
uvāca bhūyo madanāntakārī dehe na cāhaṃ madanaṃ sunetre ||
netrasya caiva jvalanātmakasya svarūpametadvada kiṃ karomi || 4 ||
tadyathā - girīndra-
putra tarasaḥ prasatāṃ lajjānvitāṃ puṣpagagantakārī || iti |

namāmyahaṃ devavaraṃ prāṇamupendravedhomararājajuṣṭam |

parāparaṃ dhāmanidhiṃ susūkṣmamanādimadhyāntavihīna rūpam || 10 ||
hiraṇyagarbha jagataḥ prasūtiṃ namāmi devaṃ hariṇāṅkacihnam |
pinākapāśāṅkuśaśūlahastaṃ kapardinaṃ meghasahasraghoṣam ||| 11 ||
tamālakaṇṭhaṃ sphaṭikāvadātaṃ namāmi śaṃbhuṃ bhuvanaika siṃham |

tvāṃ namāmi śarabharūpadharoragendrarājahāraṃ calavalayabhūṣaṇaṃ haram |

yadakṣaraṃ nirguṇamaprameyaṃ yajjyotirekaṃ pravadanti santaḥ |
raṃgamaṃ devamanantamūrti namāmi sūkṣmaṃ paramaṃ pavitram || 14 ||
namāmi rudraṃ pramathādhināthaṃ dharmāsanasthaṃ prakṛtidvayastham |
tejonidhiṃ bālaśaśāṅkamauliṃ kālendhanaṃ vahniravīndunetram || 15 ||
sūta uvāca -
prasanno'thābravītrīṃ kālī tripurahā haraḥ |
vayava varaṃ devi dadāmi tava suvrate || 16 ||
devyuvāca -
jīvatvayaṃ mahādeva kāmo lokamatāpanaḥ |
vinā kāmena bhagavannāhaṃ yāce kathaṃcana || 17 ||
īśvara uvāca -
bhavatvanaṅgo madanastvatpriyārthaṃ sulocane |
tena rūpeṇa lokasya kṣobhaṇāya bhavatvalam || 18 ||
jñātuṃ na śaktā brahmādyā mahatvarūpaṃ hi tattvataḥ || 10 ||
icchāśaktirahaṃ rājajñānaśaktira enaḥ |
kūṭasthamacalaṃ sūkṣma satyaṃ nirguṇamavyayam |
ānandamakṣaraṃ brahma tāta jānīhi matpadam || 12 ||
satpadaṃ te prapaśyanti yeṣāṃ bhaktirmayi sthirā |
nānyathā karmakāṇḍaiśca tapobhiścāpi duṣkaraiḥ || 13 ||
śivasya paramā śaktirnityā''nandamayī graham |
brahmaṇo vacanādrājannabhavaṃ dakṣakanyakā || 14 ||
śūlino devadevasya nindakaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ |
vinindya pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ jātā'smi tava kanyakā || 15 ||
svecchayaivāvatāro me naiva cānyavaśātpitaḥ
tasmānmāṃ paramāṃ śaktimiti jñātvā sukhī bhava || 16 ||
nāśayāmi tavājñānaṃ bhavabandhanakāraṇam |
divyaṃ dadāmi te jñānaṃ duḥkhatrayavināśakṛt || 17 ||
evaṃ devyāḥ prasādena himavānparvateśvaraḥ |
labdhvā māheśvaraṃ jñānaṃ jīvanmuktastadā'bhavat || 18 ||
apaśyadakhilaṃ viśvamumāmaheśvarātmakam |
nityānandaṃ nirvibhāgamātmānaṃ ca tadātmakam || 12 ||
mānameyādirahitaṃ bhedābhedavivarjitam |
bāhyābhyantaranirmuktaṃ śuddhaṃ nirguṇamavyayam || 20 ||
na samīpaṃ na dūrasthaṃ na sthūlaṃ nāpi vā kṛśam |
na dīrgha nāpi vā hasvaṃ na pītaṃ nāpi lohitam || 21 ||
na nīlaṃ na ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca na śuklaṃ nāpi karburam |
pāṇipādavinirmukte na śrotraṃ na ca cākṣuṣam || 22 ||
anāsikamajihvaṃ ca manobuddhivivarjitam |
bandhamokṣavinirmuktaṃ bodhābodhavivarjitam || 23 ||
nāssdhārasthaṃ na nābhisthaṃ na hṛdisthaṃ na kaṇṭhagam |
nāpi nāsāgragaṃ viprā na bhrūmadhyagataṃ hi tat || 24 ||
na nāḍītrayamadhyasthaṃ dvādaśāntagarta na ca |
morṇātantubhiṃ tattu vidyutpuñja nibhaṃ na ca || 25 ||
sarvopādhivinirmuktaṃ caitanyaṃ sarvargaṃ śivam |
tadevedamidaṃ viśvaṃ tasmādanyanna vidyate || 26 ||
āsthāya paramāṃ bhaktiṃ śivayoḥ pādapaṅkaje |
pitrorhiraṇyagarbhasya śāṅgiṇaścāpi suvrata || 27 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde māheśvara- jñānakathanaṃ nāma pañcapañcāśo'dhyāyaḥ || 55 ||
sūta uvāca -
āhvānayattato viśvakarmāṇaṃ parvateśvaraḥ |
vivāhamaṇḍapaṃ kartuṃ nānāścaryavibhūṣitam || 1 ||
tenā''hṛtastataḥ śīghraṃ viśvakarmā mahāmatiḥ |
prayayau himavatpārśve kuśalo viśvakarmaṇi || 2 ||
dṛṣṭvā'tha viśvakarmāṇaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ parvatarāṭ svayam |
svāgatāsa napādyādyaiḥ sādairastamapūjayat || 3 ||
vidhivatpūjayitvā tu viśvakarmāṇamabravīt || 4 ||
parvata ra ḍuvāca -
viśvakarmanmahābhājña sarvaśāstraviśārada |
yatkāraṇādihā''hūto mayā tvaṃ tadravīmyaham || 5 ||

āgamiṣyati viśveśīṃ pariṇetuṃ śivaḥ svayam || 6 ||
maṇḍaparataṃtra kartavyo yajñārthaṃ hi hiraṇmayaḥ |
yojanāyuta vistīrṇamane kāścaryasaṃyutam || 7 ||
dṛṣṭamātreṇa sarvasya prītirbhavati vai yathā |
tathā tvaṃ maṇḍapaṃ śīghraṃ kuru viśveśvarapriyam || 8 ||
evamuktastadā tena giriṇā viśvakarmakartṛ |
vaivāhaṃ maṇḍapaṃ śīghrama sṛjadratnavigraham || 9 ||
ratambhairhemamayaiścitrairmaṇibhiḥ sūryasaṃnibhaiḥ |
indranīlamayairdivyaivai duyairvidumairapi || 10 ||

cāmarālaṃkṛtairuccairdarpaṇairvividhairapi |
sūryabimbapratīkāśaiścandravinvasamaprabhaiḥ || 12 ||
oṃ sūryavimbanyādi śāṃti saṃjña pasyornāsti |
dhvajamālākulaṃ divyaṃ patākāne kaśobhitam |
ratnajaiḥ siṃhaśārdūlairgajava papernirantaram || 12 ||
recitaṃ maṇḍapaṃ divyaṃ priyaṃ triravidviṣaḥ |
rudrāṇāṃ ca tathā rūpairgandharvāpsara tathā || 14 ||
devaiścaiva manohāya tathā paraiḥ !
mālābhiḥ stambakairvimā ratnajaiḥ kusumairbhṛśam || 15 ||
kaciccāmīkareṇātha hṛdyāṃ bhūmiṃ vinirmame |

anekākāra vinyāsaistato dhātrīṃ vinirmame || 18 ||
kvacitkalaśavinyāsaiḥ kvacitsvastikabhūṣitaiḥ |
haricandanagandhāyaiḥ karpūrodgāragandhibhiḥ || 19 ||
jātīpāṭalapadmānāṃ campakānāṃ sugandhibhiḥ |
āsanairvividhaiḥ pūtaiścandrajīmṛtasaṃnibhaiḥ || 20 ||
udayārkasamākārairmeruśṛṅgopamairbhṛśam |
tamālapampakābhaiśva indranīlam yaistathā || 21 ||
sindūracayasaṃkāśairjapākusumasaṃnibhaiḥ : |
saṃdhyārāganibhaiśvānyairdāḍimīkusumaprabhaiḥ || hemakummanibhaiśvānyairmuktāphalanibhairapi || 22 ||
tārakāpuñjasaṃkāśaiḥ padmanīlendranīlajaiḥ |
tatraiva maṇḍape divye toyasthānānyakalpayat || 23 ||
dīrghikā stoyapūrṇāśca kṣīrapūrṇāstathaiva ca |
dadhihradānanekāṃśca sudhāsaṃpūritāni vai || 24 ||
ghṛtapūrṇā mahāna ratnasopānamaṇḍitāḥ |
vṛkṣāṃ kāmekāndivyāndarvakāṇāṃ tathobhayoḥ || 25 ||
gajasaṃjila puptako kāmana

ramaṇīyāni divyāni manastuṣṭikarāṇi ca |

śrukā |
-
śailādimabravīdevī viśveśo viśvapūjitaḥ || 1 ||
i.
-
śrībhadānu ca hitārtha rurvadevānāmasmākaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |
vivāhayajña ārabdho nagarājena dhīmatā || 2 ||
dānārthamadrikanyāyāḥ prasthito himavānsvayam |
ahaṃ tatra gamiṣyāmi surairbrahmādibhiḥ saha || 3 ||
tvamihāssvāhaya surānkālānyādīndvijāṃstathā |
dvīpāṃśca sāgararāṃścaiva parvatāṃśca nadīstathā || 4 ||
maṇḍapaṃ sundaraṃ yatra nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā |
tatra tiṣṭhatyumā devī mama dhyānaparāyaṇā || 5 ||
vidyullateva bhāsantī candrakoṭinibhānanā |
evamukto maheśena nandī sūryāyutaprabhaḥ || 6 ||
natvā viśveśvaraṃ devaṃ dhyānārūḍharatadā'bhavat |
dhyātaḥ kṣaṇātsamāyātaḥ kālāgniviśvadāhakaḥ || 7 ||
rudraiḥ parivṛto devaḥ koṭikoṭigaṇeśvaraiḥ |
tato'bravītsakālāgniḥ sarvajñaṃ nandikeśvaram || 8 ||
kimarthamahamāhūto devadevena śaṃnā |
upasthito vā pralayaḥ saṃhariṣyāmi tatkṣaṇāt || 9 ||
evamuktastadā tena śailādistamathābravīt |
pralayārthaṃ na cā''hūtastvaṃ viśveśena śaṃbhunā || 10 ||
grahīṣyati gireḥ putrī patnītvena maheśvaraḥ |
tadarthatvamāhūto brahmādyāca divaukasaḥ || 12 ||
nandino vacanaṃ śrutvā kālāgniridamabravīt |
draṣṭukāmā vayaṃ sarve brahmādyāḥ śūlapāṇinam || 12 ||
śīghraṃ darśaya śailā nirvṛtāḥ smo yathā vayam |
vijñāpaya mahādevaṃ brahmādyācā''gatā iti || 13 ||
sarve tvaddhyānanigtāḥ sarve tvadarśanotsukā |
kālāgnimamukhānāṃ ca vacaḥ śrutvā gaṇāgraṇīḥ || māha viśveśvaraṃ devaṃ snigdhagambhīrayā girā || 14 ||
nandikeśvara uvāca -
brahmādyācā''gatāḥ sarve śūlapāṇe tavā''jñayā |
draṣṭuṃ micchanti te sarve namaskartuṃ tathā mudrā || 15 ||
diśā''deśe purāre māṃ kiṃ vakṣyāmi surāsurān |
cāritā dvāramūleṣu draṣṭukāmāca saṃsthitāḥ || 16 ||
yadadhobhāgamāśritya draḥ kālāgnisaṃjñitaḥ || 17 ||
paśyantu caite bhūteśaṃ śūlaṃ caiva sadojjvalam |
aal viveśa kālāgnirviṣṇurbrahmā śatakratuḥ || 18 ||
anye ca devagandharvā ṛṣayo manavastathā |
sarve kolāhalaṃ kṛtvā devāsuramahoragāḥ || 19 ||
viviśurhara saṃsthānaṃ nadyādyā iva sāgaram |
praviśya bhavane ramye nānādhātuvicitrite || 20 ||
gaṇakoṭisamākīrṇe rudrakoṭisusevite |
agrajanmaguruḥ pūrva rudairdevairvṛtastadā || 21 ||
bhavārimandhakāraṃ tamapaśyadantakācalaḥ |
muktācalapratīkāśaṃ śaśāṅkacayasaṃnibham || 22 ||
nīlakaṇṭhaṃ trinetraṃ ca śūlinaṃ sarvatomukham |
koṭisūryapratīkāśaṃ jagadānandakāriṇam || 23 ||
kapālamālinaṃ devaṃ kapardakṛtabhūṣaṇam |
daśabāhuṃ daśārdhāsyamanantaṃ tejasāṃ nidhim || 24 ||
jagadutpattisaṃhārasthityanugrahakāriṇam |
aprameyamanākāramamapañcamanākulam || 25 ||
siṃhāsanasthamacalaṃ carācaravibhūtidam |

stutvā ca pūjayitvā ca nanāma ca punaḥ punaḥ || 14 ||
gītaiśca vividhairvākyaiḥ praviveśa harastadā |
bhavo'bhavattadā bālodvayaṣṭavarṣākṛtiḥ svayam || 15 ||
hemāṅgo bhagavāñśaṃbhuḥ kirīṭī kuṇḍalī haraḥ |
surāsurāśca viprendrā dṛṣṭvā rūpaṃ pinākinaḥ || 16 ||
avalokya mukhā'nyonyaṃ jahasuste mudā'nvitāḥ |
āsane maje vimā nānāratnaiśca bhūṣite || 17 |
viveśa bhagavāñśūlī mahādevo jagatpatiḥ |
harasya dakṣiṇe vedhā vāmabhāge janārdanaḥ || 18 ||
śailādiragrataḥ śaṃbhoḥ kālarudraśca suvratāḥ |
rudrairgaṇeśvarairdevaiḥ siddhaiśca munibhistathā || 19 ||
upaviṣṭeṣu sarveṣu gandharvādyāḥ samantataḥ |
jagurgītaṃ ca hindolaṃ tumbarurnāradādayaḥ || 20 ||
mattamātaṅgagāminyo geyaṃ tālalayānvitam |
rambhādyapsarasaḥ sarvāḥ kiṃnaryo nanṛturdvijāḥ || 21 ||
vīṇāvallakiveṇūnāṃ mṛdaṅgānāṃ viśeṣataḥ |
dhvanibhirmanasastuṣṭirjajñe sumanasāṃ tadā || 22 ||
atha viśveśvaraḥ śaṃbhurbhūṣaṇaṃ nabhasi sthitam |
prāyacchagirijāyai tadāhlādajanakaṃ mudā || 23 ||
anenālaṃkṛtā deva mama yogyā bhaviṣyāsa |
piturdakṣasya yaḥ kopaḥ pūrvajasya varānane || 24 ||
prahāsyasi tamevā''śu bhāvaṃ caiva tu tāmasam |
tataḥ sā pārvatī devī gṛhītvā''kāśamaṇḍalāt || 25 ||
pituḥ samīpamagamadvastrābharaṇamuttamam |
mahatā hyutsavenāssśu bhūṣayitvā śivāṃ nagaḥ || 26 ||
vastrairābharaṇairdevīṃ divyairvai siṃhavāhinīm |
menotsaṅgangartā bhūyaścandralekheva toyade || 27 ||
tī nirvṛtā devī babhau tāmarasekṣaṇā |
atha devaiḥ parivṛto viṣṇvādyaistripurāntakaḥ || 28 ||
babhrāma muniśārdūlāḥ krīḍāsthānāni kṛtsnaśaḥ |
bhagavandevadeveśa viśveśāndhakasūdana || 29 ||
seyaṃ jalamayī nātha nirmitā viśvakarmaṇā || 31 ||
yā ceyaṃ paramā ramyā toyānāṃ bhrāntikāriṇī |
seyaṃ bhāti mahādeva ratnānāmīdṛśī prabhā || 32 ||
idaṃ ca dvārasaṃsthānaṃ dṛśyate lambakairvṛtam |
kuḍyasya ratnavinyāse lakṣyate dvārarūpatā || 33 ||
idaṃ citrarathākāraṃ dṛśyate vanamuttamam |
prativimbaṃ mahādeva ratnabhūmerna saṃśayaḥ || 34 ||
idaṃ ca mandirākāraṃ sopānacayamaṇḍitam |
prativimvamidaṃ caiva dṛśyate navamaṇḍitam || 35 ||
yā ceyaṃ sāgarākārā dṛśyate toyarūpiṇī |
eṣā'pi parameśāna ratnabhūmirjaloṣitā || 36 ||
yadidaṃ gaganābhāsaṃ mūrtidravyairivorjitam |
krīḍāmaṇḍapametasminpradeśe deva tiṣṭhati || 37 ||
ambarābhairmahāratnairbāhyadeśe vinirmitam |
anekavādyasaṃyuktaṃ ramaṇīyaṃ yayau haraḥ || 38 ||
evaṃ krīḍati deveśe surāsuramahoragāḥ |
vidyādharāstathā yakṣā gandharvāpsarasādayaḥ || 39 ||
dīrghikāsu taḍāgeṣu nadīṣu ca hadeṣu ca |
krīḍāvāpīṣu te ramyairtha bernānāvidhairbhṛśam || 40 ||
babhūvurdevatāḥ sarvāḥ krīḍāratiṣu lālasāḥ |
atha saṃkrīḍya viśvātmā nivṛttastatpradeśataḥ |
vedyāḥ samīpamagamatstūyamāno munīśvaraiḥ || 41 ||
prāpyāssruroha prasabhaṃ sureśastadindranīlāmalavedikāntam |
sahasrapatrairvakulaiśca nāgaiḥ kīrṇa hi yatkāñcanapārijātaiḥ || 42 ||
tataḥ praviṣṭo hariṇāṅkacihnaḥ saraśmijālākula vedikāntam |
viveśa sūryāyutasuprabhāso vṛto virañcyādisuraiḥ samantāt || 43 ||
athopaviṣṭaṃ saṃvīkṣya viśveśaṃ parvateśvaraḥ |
tasya saṃsthāpya purato deveśamabravīdidam || 44 ||
himavānuvāca -
tvamevaikaḥ paraṃ dhāma ardhanārīśvarastataḥ |
devatānāṃ hitārthāya jāto hyardhatanuḥ pṛthak || 45 ||
dakṣasya duhitā devī jagaddhātrī humā satī |
vinindya ca tato dakṣaṃ tyaktvā dehaṃ nijaṃ punaḥ || 46 ||
tavaiva patnī deveśa jātā mama sutā satī |
tataḥ śrutvā girīndrasya vacastribhuvaneśvaraḥ |
prasanno varadaḥ śaṃbhurabravītparvateśvaram || 47 ||
īśvara uvāca -
jānāmyahaṃ yena mamaiva māyā śaktirvaraiṣā nagarājasiṃha |
saṃtyajya dehaṃ tava dhāni jātā yogātsvayaṃ cāruśaśāṅkavaktrā ||48 ||
ācārārthaṃ giriśreṣṭha dattāṃ gṛhṇāmi pārvatīm |
adattāṃ yadi gṛhṇāmi tathā loke'pi vartate ( varteta vai janaḥ ) || 49 ||
atha divyodakaiḥ pūrṇamādāya kalaśaṃ giriḥ |
paripūrṇasya nityasya nityānugrahakāriṇaḥ || 50 ||
prakṣālya pādau śirasā praṇamya bhṛṅgāramādāya sa śailarājaḥ |
mumoca toyaṃ bhavapāṇipaye datteti dattati tadā prajalpan || 51 ||
tato maṅgalanirghoṣaḥ samabhūtridivaukasām |
vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgānāṃ kāhalānāṃ ca niḥsvanaḥ || 52 ||
sā hārakaṇṭhī kaṭisūtradāmā subhrūlatā cāruvilolanetrā |
meroryathaivopari candralekhā tathā babhau parvatarājaputrī || 53 ||
atha vedyāṃ gato brahmā viśvamāyāṃ smarāraṇim |
dadarśodakapātreṇa vibhāvasupurasthitaḥ || 54 ||
māheśvarīṃ kāmamayīṃ dṛṣṭvā tāṃ tu pitāmahaḥ |
akṣaratsahasā śukraṃ bhagnakumbhādivodakam || 55 ||
pādena tanmamardā''śu śukraṃ tatpadmasaṃbhavaḥ |
padmajo'pi mahātejā devadevasya paśyataḥ || 56 ||
maivaṃ madeti taṃ dṛṣṭvā tripurāriḥ pitāmaham |
juhoti va (ajuhodva) canācchaṃbhorvāmenā''dāya pāṇinā || 58 ||
havanācca tataḥ prāptāḥ savitāraṃ viyadgatam |
tejomayāśca te sarve taponiṣṭhāḥ samantataḥ || 59 ||
aṣṭāśītiḥ sahasrāṇi munayastūrdhvaretasaḥ |
māne tvaṅguṣṭhamātrāstu jātā hātha suvarcasaḥ || 60 ||
babhūvuste mahātmānaḥ pataṅgasahacāriṇaḥ |
nispṛhā raśmipāḥ sarve sarve jvalanasaṃnibhāḥ || 61 ||
tato devāḥ sagandharvāḥ siddhāśca munayastathā |
piśācā dānavā daityāḥ kiṃnarāśca mahoragāḥ || 62 ||
vidyādharāśvāpsarasastathā cānye surāsurāḥ |
prahṛṣṭāḥ sarva evaite pārvatyā harasaṃgamāt || 63 ||
mumoca dṛṣṭiṃ ṛturāṭsutuṣṭaḥ puṣpairanekairbhramarākulaiśca |
vādyairvicitrairvaraiśaṅkhanādaiḥ sugītagānairvaramaṅgalaiśca || 64 ||
vīṇāravairdandubhiveṇunādaiḥ samantataḥ karṇasukhaṃ prajajñe |
ānṛtyatībhiḥ surasundarībhirjegīyatībhirvarakiṃnarībhiḥ || 65 ||
daityāṅganābhiśca rasīdatībhiḥ kāmāyate'tīva tadutsarvaṃ ca ( vaśca ) |
kāñcīraveṇātha nitambinīnāṃ manobhirāmeṇa ca nūpurāṇām|| 66 ||
tāsāṃ smitenātha munīndravaryā vabhūva kāmānaladīpacaryā |
homāvasāne madhuparkayuktaṃ devāya tasmai ghubhājanaṃ ca || 67 ||
tato nivedya pramathādhipāya cakāra tuṣṭiṃ paramāṃ virañciḥ || 68 ||
atha deveṣu viśveśo varado'bhūdvijottamāḥ |
varāṃśca vividhāndattvā brahmādibhyo maheśvaraḥ || 69 ||
vyasarjayattataḥ sarvānsthāvarāñjaṅganmāṃstathā |
visarjitāḥ praṇamyeśaṃ prītiṃ te paramāṃ gatāḥ || 70 ||
evaṃ saṃkṣepato viprā vivāho girijāpateḥ |
kathito raviṇā pūrvaṃ yathāvatsamudīritaḥ || 71 ||
śṛṇoti śraddhayā yastu paṭhedvā prayatātmavān |
sarvānkāmānavāprati varṣādarvāṅna saṃśayaḥ || 72 ||
sarvapāpavinirmuktastejasvī priyadarśanaḥ |
jīvedvarṣaśataṃ sāgraṃ gacchedbrahmapadaṃ tataḥ || 73 ||
|| iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde sāmbavivāha- varṇanaṃ nāmaikonaṣaṣṭitamo'dhyāyaḥ || 59 ||
sūta uvāca -
vivāhyādrisutāṃ śaṃbhuyau kailāsaparvatam |
krīḍāṃ vai varṣasāhasrīmakarottatra śaṃkaraḥ || 1 ||
gaṇairnānāvidhaiścaiva siṃhāsyaiḥ śarabhānanaiḥ |
kaiścidvayāghramukhairbhīmaiḥ kaiścidgṛdhamukhairapi || 2 ||
kaiścidgajamukhairanyaiḥ kaiścinmṛgamukhairapi |
kaiśviduṣṭṛmukhaidīyaiḥ kaiśviddhayamukhairapi || 3 ||
kaiściccitramukhairanyaiḥ kaiścidvakamukhairapi |
sūpakāsyaistathā = cānyairmārjāravadanairāpaḥ || 4 ||
sarpāsyairnakulāsyaiśca jambukāsyaistathā'paraiḥ |
śiśumāramukhaiścānyairṛkṣavaktraistathā'paraiḥ || 5 |
mayūravadanairanyairvakavaktraistathā'paraiḥ |
_ _
śākhāmṛgamukhaiścānyaiḥ kharāsyaiśca tathā'paraiḥ || 6 |
anyairasaṃkhyaiḥ pramathairjarāmaraṇavarjitaiḥ |
nityatṛptairnirātaṅgaiḥ kālasaṃharaṇakṣabhaiḥ || 7 ||
sahasrakoṭisaṃkhyākaiḥ svacchandagaticāribhiḥ |
krīḍāṃ vidhāya bhagavānkailāse parvatottame || 8 ||
tapasā mahatā śaṃbhuranugṛhya ca mandaram |
ક
kailāsaṃ saṃparityajya mandare cārukandare || 9 ||
tatrāpi ramamāṇasya gate varṣasahasrake |
devatānāṃ hitārthāya prakṛtyā saha śūlabhṛt || 10 ||
kaiścidavukamukhairityantaḥ sārdhaślokaḥ kajha saṃśita pustaka yonasti
prārthito'haṃ suraiḥ pūrvaṃ tārakasya vadhepsayā || 11 ||
madretasaḥ samutpannastārakaṃ sa haniṣyati |
iti matvā mahādeve ramamāṇe sahomayā || 12 ||
utpātāśca mahāghorāḥ saṃpravṛtta: sudāruṇāḥ |
rusthīni varṣanti nadanto meghasaṃkulāḥ || 13 ||
vāyavaśca mahāvegāḥ parvatāṃścālayanti te |
vimānāni surāṇāṃ ca nipeturvasudhātale || 14 ||
ulkābhirgaganaṃ vyāptaṃ patantībhirdvijottamāḥ |
ketavacoditāḥ sarve jṛmbhanta iva pāvakāḥ 15 || digdāhāśva mahāghorā dauvāgniriva saṃkṣaye |
mṛtyukāle yathā jantunaiva saukhyamavāpnuyāt ||
jagatrayamidaṃ kṛtstraṃ na labheta tathā sukham |
na vedāḥ paṭhitāstasminna viprā jajapurjapam || 17 |
pārvatyāṃ kampamānāyāṃ kampamāne ca śaṃkare |
trailokyamabhavannūnaṃ kampamānaṃ bhayāturam || 18 ||
kaॉlāgnikampito devo virañcirmunibhiḥ saha |
cakrāyudho'pi cātyarthamindrādyaiḥ parivāritaḥ || 19 ||
ye kecidevagandharvāḥ siddhā gaganacāriṇaḥ |
vidyādharāśca yakṣāca saṃprāptāśca vasuṃdharām || 20 ||
etasminnantare prāptaḥ śakraṃ devarṣisattamaḥ |
yathāvanmadhuparkādyaiḥ śakrastamabhyapūjayat || 21 ||
abravīddevarājastamupaviṣṭaṃ mahāmunim |
trikāladarśinaṃ śāntamātmaniṣṭhaṃ taponidhim || 22 ||
śakra uvāca -
utpātāśca mahāghorāḥ saṃpravṛttāḥ sudāruṇāḥ |
kāraṇaṃ vada me sarva śāntiścaiva yathā bhavet || 23||
nārada uvāca -
umayā saha viśveśaḥ paraṃ jyotirmaheśvaraḥ aharniśamaviśrāntaṃ yukta eva pravartate || 24 ||
yadugraṃ gahanaṃ ghoramamadhṛṣyamagocaram |
hṛdi yadbhavatāṃ kāryamagnistatsādhayiṣyati || 39 ||
evamuktvā'tha viśvādiḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ |
abravītkṛṣṇavartmānaṃ devānāṃ sadasi sthitam || 40 ||
śrīviṣṇuruvāca -
śṛṇu madvacanaṃ vahne devānāṃ yadupasthitam |
tvayā tatsādhanīyaṃ hi hitārtha tridivaukasām || 41 ||
aisir devaḥ paraṃ jyotirnīlagrīvo vilohitaḥ |
ramate comayā sārdhaṃ carācarapatiḥ śivaḥ || 42 ||
bhayaṃ tasmātsamutpannaṃ kāraṇāddhi divaukasām |
tasmāddhitāya gaccha tvaṃ mahādevasya saṃnidhau || 43 ||
mukhaṃ tvameva sarveṣāṃ kāryāṇāṃ caiva sādhakaḥ |
ityevaṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā pāvakaḥ keśavāttadā || uvācedaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ śrīvatsāṅkantavakṣasam || 44 ||
agniruvāca-
yaduktaṃ bhavatā deva kiṃ tvayuktaṃ sanātana |
maheśasya raihaḥsthasya praveṣṭuṃ naiva sāṃpratam || 45 ||
dhyānayukto janaḥ kaścinmatra bhojanatatparaḥ |
rahaḥ stho'tha ca dānasthastadayuktaṃ praveśanam || 46 ||
japyopahārayukto vā homayukto'thavā bhavet |
arcanābhirataḥ kaścittadayuktaṃ praveśanam || 47 ||
prākṛtasyāpi deveśa rahaḥsthasya ramāpate |
tasminkāle sureśāna garhitaṃ tu praveśanam || 48 ||
kiṃ punarbhagavānbhīmastigmaraśmirmaheśvaraḥ |
devānāṃ ca hitārthāya prakṛtyā saha saṃgataḥ || 49 ||
nāhaṃ tatra viśe nūnaṃ vibhemi madhusūdana |
āgataṃ māṃ samālokya kṣaṇacchiṃbhuhaniṣyati || 50 ||
jugupsitamidaṃ kāryamiti kaṣṭaṃ bhayāvaham |
vivastrāṃ jananīṃ devīṃ kathaṃ drakṣyāmi keśava || 51 ||
yadugraṃ gahanaṃ ghoramapradhṛṣyamagocaram |
hṛdi yadbhavatāṃ kāryamagnistatsādhayiṣyati || 39 ||
evamuktvā'tha viśvādiḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ |
abravītkṛṣṇavartmānaṃ devānāṃ sadasi sthitam || 40 ||
śrī viṣṇuruvāca -
śṛṇu madvacanaṃ vahne devānāṃ yadupasthitam |
tvayā tatsādhanīyaṃ hi hitārtha tridivaukasām || 41 ||
yo'sau devaḥ paraṃ jyotinīlagrīvo vilohitaḥ |
ramate comayā sārdhaṃ carācarapatiḥ śivaḥ || 42 ||
bhayaṃ tasmātsarmutpannaṃ kāraṇāddhi divaukasām |
tasmāddhitāya gaccha tvaṃ mahādevasya saṃnidhau || 43 ||
mukhaṃ tvameva sarveṣāṃ kāryāṇāṃ caiva sādhakaḥ |
ityevaṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā pāvakaḥ keśavāttadā || uvācedaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ śrīvatsāṅkantavakṣasam || 44 ||
agniruvāca -
yaduktaṃ bhavatā deva kiṃ tvayuktaṃ sanātana |
maheśasya raihaḥsthasya praveṣṭuṃ naiva sāṃpratam || 45 ||
dhyānayukto janaḥ kaścinmantrabhojanatatparaḥ |
rahaḥ stho'tha ca dānasthastadayuktaṃ praveśanam || 46 ||
japyopahārayukto vā homayukto'thavā bhavet |
arcanābhirataḥ kaścittadayuktaṃ praveśanam || 47 ||
prākṛtasyāpi deveśa rahaḥsthasya ramāpate |
tasminkāle sureśāna garhitaṃ tu praveśanam || 48 ||
kiṃ punarbhagavānbhīmastigmaraśmirmaheśvaraḥ |
devānāṃ ca hitārthāya prakṛtyāṃ saha saṃgataḥ || 49 ||
nāhaṃ tatra viśe nūnaṃ vibhemi madhusūdana |
āgataṃ māṃ samālokya kṣaṇācchaṃbhurhaniṣyati || 50 ||
jugupsitamidaṃ kāryamiti kaṣṭaṃ bhayāvaham |
vivastrāṃ jananīṃ devīṃ kathaṃ drakṣyāmi keśava || 51 ||
kiṃ vakṣyati praviṣṭatya vakṣyāmi kimahaṃ vibho |
jalpayiṣyati māṃ devo dhiṅmūrkho'yamiti dhruvam || 52 ||
yadbhāvyaṃ tadbhavatvadya na karomi ca ninditam |
agninā caivaraktastu viṣṇurdānavasūdanaḥ || 53 ||
bhayadaṃ mohadaṃ śrutvā vākyaṃ hṛdayakampanam |
uvāca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ punarvahnimiti stuvan || trailokyarakṣaṇārthāya śakrādīnāṃ ca saṃnidhau || 55 ||
. viṣṇuruvāca -
yaduktaṃ bhavatā vahne satyametanna saṃśayaḥ |
ātmahetorviruddhaṃ syātparārtha naiva duṣyati || 56 ||
pradiṣṭo devadevena saṃhārārthaṃ kapardinā |
praviśa tvamaṇo rūpamādāya na hi duṣyasi || 57 ||
prastutāprastutaṃ nāsti tejomūrteratavānagha |
sarvadā sarvagastvaṃ hi na kacitpratihanyase || 58 ||
bhūtagrāmaṃ samastaṃ vai tvameko vyāpya tiṣṭhasi |
udarasthaḥ pacarayanaṃ prāṇināṃ meṣavāhana || 59 ||
svayaikena jagatkṛtsnaṃ gopyate yadi pāvaka |
kiṃ na prāptaṃ tvayā brūhi doṣaḥ kaḥ syādbhutāśana || 60 ||
jugupsā'sminna kartavyā tvayā vai havyavāhana |
utpannasyāsya kāryasya kāla eṣa tavānagha || 61 ||
tridaśāḥ śaraṇaṃ prāptā hutarbhuktvāṃ vibhāvaso |
aho dhanyataravāsi ślāghyo yadi kariṣyasi || 62 ||
kuru kārya surāṇāṃ tvaṃ magnānāṃ karuṇāṃ kuru |
sarvakāle yathā martyā vīkṣamāṇāstu bhāskaram || 63 ||
tathā tavāssnanaṃ vahne paśyanti surasattamāḥ |
cārucandrapratīkāśaṃ kuṇḍalābhyāmalaṃkṛtam || 64 ||
anena kiṃ na paryāptaṃ vada nūnaṃ vibhāvaso |
evaṃ saṃvodhyamāno'gnirviṣṇunā dvijasattamāḥ || 65 ||
hṛdaye cintitaṃ tena yāsyāmi harasaṃnidhau |
sendrāḥ savaruṇādityāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ |
tubruvuste śubhairvākyaiḥ pāvakaṃ dvijasattamāḥ || 67 ||

devā ūcuḥ -
jalabharo jalotpanna jalājala jalecara |
sarvaga
jalajāmalapatrākṣa yajñadeva hutāśana || 1 ||
kṛṣṇaketo kṛṣṇavartmansvargamārgapradarśaka |
yajñāhuti hutāhāra yajñāhāra harākṛte || 2 ||
pūrṇagarbha gavāṃ garbha jaya deva mahāśana |
tamohara mahāhāra svāhābhartarnamo'stu te || 3 ||
havyavāhana saptārce citrabhāno mahādyute |
analāgne yajñamukha jaya pāvaka saga || 4 ||
vibhāvaso mahābhāga vedabhāpārthabhāṣaṇa |
kṛśāno ṛtusaṃbhārapriya viśvaprabhāvana || 5 |

taba thā- bilvapatrairakhaṇḍaiśva pūjayedinduśekharam - iti 1
cāmaraṃ yaḥ śive dadyānmaṇiratnavibhūṣitam |
hemarūpyādidaṇḍaṃ vā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu || 24 ||
cāmarāsaktahastābhirdivya strīparivāritaḥ |
vimānaṃ varamāruhya gaṇairyāti śivaṃ padam || 25 ||
araṇyasaṃbhavaiḥ puṣpaiḥ patrairvā girisaṃbhavaiḥ |
aparyupitaniśchidvairaraktairjantuvarjitaiḥ || 26 ||
ātmārāmodbhavairvā'pi puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjayecchivam |
puṣpajātiviśeṣeṇa bhavetpuṇyamathottaram || 27 ||
tapaḥ śīlaguṇāḍhyāya vedavedāṅgagāmine |
daśa dattvā suvarṇasya phalaṃ hi tadavāpnuyāt || 28 ||
arkapuṣpaiḥ kṛtā pūjā yadi devāya śaṃbhave |
arkapuṣpasahasrebhyaḥ karavīraṃ praśasyate || 29 ||
karavīrasahasrebhyo bilvapatraṃ viśiṣyate |
bilvapatrasahasrebhyaḥ śamīpatraṃ viśiṣyate || 30 ||
arkapuṣpasahastrebhyaḥ śamīpuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate |
śamī puṣpasahasrebhyaḥ kuśapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate || 31 ||
kuśa puṣpasahastrebhyaḥ padmapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate |
padmapuṣpasahasrebhyo bakapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate || 32 ||
bakapuṣpasahastrebhya ekaṃ dhattūrakaṃ tathā |
dhattūraka sahastrebhyo bṛhatpuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate || 33 ||
bṛhatpuṣpasahastrebhyo droṇapuṣpaṃ viśiṣyate |
droṇapuṣpasahastrebhyaḥ a (bhyo hya) pāmārga viśiṣyate || 34 ||
apāmārgasahastrebhyaḥ śrīmannīlotpalaṃ varam |
nīlotpala sahasreṇa yo mālāṃ saṃprayacchati || 35 ||
śivāya vidhivadbhaktyā tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu |
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca || 36 ||
vasecchivapure śrīmāñśivatulyaparākramaḥ |
karavīrasamā jñeyā jātī vijayapāṭalā || 37 ||
śvetamandārakusumaṃ sitapadmaṃ ca tatsamam |
nāgacampakapuṃnāgā dhatturakasamāḥ smṛtāḥ || 38 ||
randhukaṃ ketakīpuṣpaṃ kunda yūthī madantikāḥ |
śirīṣaṃ cārjunaṃ puṣpaṃ prayatnena vivarjayet || 39 ||
kanakāni kadambāni rātrau deyāni śaṃkare |
divā śeṣāṇi puṣpāṇi divā rātrau ca mallikāḥ || 40 ||
praharaṃ tiṣṭhate jātī karavīramaharniśam |
keśakīṭāpaviddhāni śīrṇaparyuṣitāni ca || 41 ||
svayaṃ patitapuṣpāṇi tyajedupahatāni ca |
mukulainārcayedaśaṃ yasya kasyāpi nārada || 42 ||
kalikairnārcayeddevaṃ campakairjalajairvinā |
na paryupitadoṣo'rita jalajotpalacampakaiḥ || 43 ||
puṣpāṇāmapyalābhe tu patrāṇyapi nivedayet |
phalānāmapyalābhe tu tṛṇagulmauṣadhairapi || 44 ||
auṣadhānāmabhāve tu bhaktyā bhavati pūjitaḥ |
bilvapatrairakhaṇḍaistu sakṛtpūjayate śivam || 45 ||
sarvapāpavinirmukto rudraloke mahīyate |

golakṣasya phalaṃ prāpya śivaloke mahīyate |
bṛhatīkusumairbhaktyā yo liṅga sakṛdarcayet || 47 ||
gavāmayutadānasya phalaṃ prāpya śivaṃ vrajet |

kuśāpāmārgakumudakadambakuraivairapi |

sūryakoṭipratīkāśairvimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ || 51 ||

tāni sākṣātpragṛhṇāti devadevo maheśvaraḥ || 58 ||
kṛṣṇāroḥ sakarpūradhūpaṃ dadyācchivāya vai |
nairantaryeṇa māsārdhaṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu || 59 ||
kalpakoṭisahasrāṇi kalpakoṭiśatāni ca |
bhuktvā śivapure bhogāṃstadante pṛthivīpatiḥ || 60 ||
guggulaṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ sākṣādgṛhṇāti śaṃkaraḥ |
māsārdhaṃ dhūpadānena śivaloke mahīyate || 61 ||
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ yaḥ sājyaṃ guggulaṃ dahet |
sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ yatra devaḥ pinākadhṛt || 62 ||
śrīphalaṃ cā''jyasaṃmiśraṃ dattvā'noti parāṃ gatim |

guḍakhaṇḍaghṛtānāṃ ca bhakṣyāṇāṃ ca nivedanāt |

brahmovāca-
puṣpaṃ vā yadi vā patraṃ sakūliṅge samarpitam |
tadanantaphalaṃ proktaṃ heturbhavati muktaye || 1 ||
tuṣṭe śive padārtha: ko durlabho hi nṛṇāṃ prabho |
tasmātsarvaprayatnena śivaprītyarthamācaret || 2 ||
yāvaddātuṃ śivaḥ śaktastāvaccintayituṃ prabhuḥ |
tatsarvaṃ na naraḥ saukhyaṃ śivaprītyarthamācaret || 3 ||
ṛddhisiddhī na dūrasthe śivaprītyarthakarmaṇām |
narāṇāṃ naranāthe kiṃ prīte tu durlabhaṃ bhavet || 4 ||
viśveśvaraṃ sadā premṇā ye bhajanti narottamāḥ |
iha saukhyaṃ ciraṃ bhuktvā hyante mokṣamavāpnuyuḥ || 5 ||
śrīśaṃbhunāthaṃ bhuvi mānavā ye bhajanti bhaktyā naralokavandyāḥ |
bhavanti te hāṭakapūrṇagehā dehāvasāne śivalokabhājaḥ || 6 ||
brahmā vā surāpo vā steyī vā gurutalpagaḥ |
yo'ntakāle śivaṃ smaryācchivasāyujyamāpnuyāt || 7 ||
nirmālyaṃ dhārayedbhaktyā śirasā pārvatīpateḥ |

avyaktaṃ liṅgāmiyuṃktamānandaṃ tamasaḥ param |

kuru yuddhaṃ mayā sārdhamahameva jagatpatiḥ |
atha vā bhaja māṃ devaṃ trailokyasyābhayapradam || 24 ||
evaṃ madvacanaṃ śrutvā prahasanmadhusūdanaḥ |
māmabravīdameyātmā kathaṃ garvāyase mudhā || 25 ||
kato'haṃ sarvalokānāṃ pālako'haṃ na saṃśayaḥ |
saṃhartā'haṃ punaścānte nānyo'sti sadṛśo mayā || 26 ||
evaṃ vivāde saṃjāte mama devena śārṅgiṇā |
prādurbhūtaṃ tadā liṅgamāvayordarpahāri tat || 27 ||

tasmilliṅge mahādevaḥ svayaṃjyotiḥ sanātanaḥ |

ardhanārīśvaro'nantastejorāśirdurāsadaḥ |

samānya phalaṃ ye pūjayedrācakaṃ naraḥ || 59 ||
kanake |
suyuddhena tathā candanakhaṇḍakaiḥ |
viśveśvaro mahādevaḥ prīyatāmiti bhāvaḥ || 60 ||
dadya svarṇa yathāśakti vācakāya sacandanam |
yace kaśī (śa) ramātrā'pi dattā bhūmiḥ śivārthinā || 61 ||
sātārayati dāturhi pūrvajānsakalānapi |
śrutvā granthamimaṃ samyagdadyādānāni śaktitaḥ || 62 ||
tānyakṣayaphalānyāhurmunayo vedavādinaḥ || 63 ||

iti śrībrahmapurāṇopapurāṇe śrīsaure sūtaśaunakasaṃvāde śivatīrtha - kathanaṃ munipatnīmohanaṃ nāmaikonasaptati- namo'dhyāyaḥ || 69 ||
